├── get-task.js      (ZOSTAW - stary, backup)

3. netlify/functions/auth.js (NOWY)
JavaScript

var crypto = require("crypto");

var headers = {
    "Access-Control-Allow-Origin": "*",
    "Access-Control-Allow-Headers": "Content-Type",
    "Access-Control-Allow-Methods": "POST, OPTIONS",
    "Content-Type": "application/json"
};

function redis(url, token, cmd) {
    return fetch(url, {
        method: "POST",
        headers: { "Authorization": "Bearer " + token, "Content-Type": "application/json" },
        body: JSON.stringify(cmd)
    }).then(function(r) { return r.json(); });
}

function hashPass(pass) {
    return crypto.createHash("sha256").update(pass).digest("hex");
}

function makeToken() {
    return "sess_" + crypto.randomBytes(16).toString("hex");
}

function makeUserId(username) {
    return "user_" + username.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z0-9]/g, "");
}

exports.handler = async function(event) {
    if (event.httpMethod === "OPTIONS") return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: "" };
    if (event.httpMethod !== "POST") return { statusCode: 405, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "POST only" }) };

    var redisUrl = process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_URL;
    var redisToken = process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_TOKEN;

    try {
        var body = JSON.parse(event.body || "{}");
        var action = body.action;

        // === REGISTER ===
        if (action === "register") {
            var username = (body.username || "").trim();
            var email = (body.email || "").trim().toLowerCase();
            var password = body.password || "";

            if (!username || username.length < 3) return { statusCode: 400, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "Nazwa min 3 znaki" }) };
            if (!email || !email.includes("@")) return { statusCode: 400, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "Nieprawidlowy email" }) };
            if (!password || password.length < 6) return { statusCode: 400, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "Haslo min 6 znakow" }) };

            var userId = makeUserId(username);

            // Check if exists
            var existing = await redis(redisUrl, redisToken, ["GET", "userdata:" + userId]);
            if (existing && existing.result) {
                return { statusCode: 400, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "Nazwa zajeta" }) };
            }

            // Check email
            var emailCheck = await redis(redisUrl, redisToken, ["GET", "email:" + email]);
            if (emailCheck && emailCheck.result) {
                return { statusCode: 400, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "Email juz zarejestrowany" }) };
            }

            var userData = JSON.stringify({
                userId: userId,
                username: username,
                email: email,
                passwordHash: hashPass(password),
                createdAt: Date.now(),
                role: "user"
            });

            var ttl = String(60 * 60 * 24 * 365); // 1 rok

            await redis(redisUrl, redisToken, ["SET", "userdata:" + userId, userData, "EX", ttl]);
            await redis(redisUrl, redisToken, ["SET", "email:" + email, userId, "EX", ttl]);
            await redis(redisUrl, redisToken, ["SET", "credits:" + userId, "10", "EX", ttl]);
            await redis(redisUrl, redisToken, ["SET", "usage:" + userId, "0", "EX", ttl]);

            // Create session
            var token = makeToken();
            await redis(redisUrl, redisToken, ["SET", "sess:" + token, userId, "EX", String(60 * 60 * 24 * 30)]);

            // Create plugin connect code
            var connectCode = "rc_" + crypto.randomBytes(6).toString("hex");
            await redis(redisUrl, redisToken, ["SET", "connect:" + connectCode, userId, "EX", String(60 * 60 * 24 * 30)]);

            return {
                statusCode: 200,
                headers,
                body: JSON.stringify({
                    success: true,
                    userId: userId,
                    username: username,
                    sessionToken: token,
                    connectCode: connectCode,
                    credits: 10
                })
            };
        }

        // === LOGIN ===
        if (action === "login") {
            var loginEmail = (body.email || "").trim().toLowerCase();
            var loginPass = body.password || "";

            if (!loginEmail || !loginPass) return { statusCode: 400, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "Podaj email i haslo" }) };

            // Find userId by email
            var emailLookup = await redis(redisUrl, redisToken, ["GET", "email:" + loginEmail]);
            if (!emailLookup || !emailLookup.result) {
                return { statusCode: 401, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "Bledny email lub haslo" }) };
            }

            var loginUserId = emailLookup.result;

            // Get user data
            var userGet = await redis(redisUrl, redisToken, ["GET", "userdata:" + loginUserId]);
            if (!userGet || !userGet.result) {
                return { statusCode: 401, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "Konto nie istnieje" }) };
            }

            var user = JSON.parse(userGet.result);

            if (user.passwordHash !== hashPass(loginPass)) {
                return { statusCode: 401, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "Bledny email lub haslo" }) };
            }

            // Create session
            var loginToken = makeToken();
            await redis(redisUrl, redisToken, ["SET", "sess:" + loginToken, loginUserId, "EX", String(60 * 60 * 24 * 30)]);

            // Create plugin connect code
            var loginConnectCode = "rc_" + crypto.randomBytes(6).toString("hex");
            await redis(redisUrl, redisToken, ["SET", "connect:" + loginConnectCode, loginUserId, "EX", String(60 * 60 * 24 * 30)]);

            // Get credits
            var credGet = await redis(redisUrl, redisToken, ["GET", "credits:" + loginUserId]);
            var creds = credGet && credGet.result ? parseInt(credGet.result, 10) : 0;

            var usageGet = await redis(redisUrl, redisToken, ["GET", "usage:" + loginUserId]);
            var usage = usageGet && usageGet.result ? parseInt(usageGet.result, 10) : 0;

            return {
                statusCode: 200,
                headers,
                body: JSON.stringify({
                    success: true,
                    userId: loginUserId,
                    username: user.username,
                    sessionToken: loginToken,
                    connectCode: loginConnectCode,
                    credits: creds,
                    usage: usage
                })
            };
        }

        // === VERIFY SESSION ===
        if (action === "verify") {
            var verifyToken = body.sessionToken;
            if (!verifyToken) return { statusCode: 400, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "Token required" }) };

            var sessGet = await redis(redisUrl, redisToken, ["GET", "sess:" + verifyToken]);
            if (!sessGet || !sessGet.result) {
                return { statusCode: 401, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "INVALID_SESSION" }) };
            }

            var verifyUserId = sessGet.result;
            var verifyUserGet = await redis(redisUrl, redisToken, ["GET", "userdata:" + verifyUserId]);
            var verifyUser = verifyUserGet && verifyUserGet.result ? JSON.parse(verifyUserGet.result) : null;

            var vCredGet = await redis(redisUrl, redisToken, ["GET", "credits:" + verifyUserId]);
            var vCreds = vCredGet && vCredGet.result ? parseInt(vCredGet.result, 10) : 0;

            var vUsageGet = await redis(redisUrl, redisToken, ["GET", "usage:" + verifyUserId]);
            var vUsage = vUsageGet && vUsageGet.result ? parseInt(vUsageGet.result, 10) : 0;

            // Get connect code or create new
            var vConnectCode = "rc_" + crypto.randomBytes(6).toString("hex");
            await redis(redisUrl, redisToken, ["SET", "connect:" + vConnectCode, verifyUserId, "EX", String(60 * 60 * 24 * 30)]);

            return {
                statusCode: 200,
                headers,
                body: JSON.stringify({
                    success: true,
                    userId: verifyUserId,
                    username: verifyUser ? verifyUser.username : "Unknown",
                    connectCode: vConnectCode,
                    credits: vCreds,
                    usage: vUsage
                })
            };
        }

        return { statusCode: 400, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "Unknown action" }) };

    } catch (err) {
        return { statusCode: 500, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: err.message }) };
    }
};
4. netlify/functions/chat.js (CAŁY NOWY)
JavaScript

var headers = {
    "Access-Control-Allow-Origin": "*",
    "Access-Control-Allow-Headers": "Content-Type",
    "Access-Control-Allow-Methods": "POST, OPTIONS",
    "Content-Type": "application/json"
};

function redis(url, token, cmd) {
    return fetch(url, {
        method: "POST",
        headers: { "Authorization": "Bearer " + token, "Content-Type": "application/json" },
        body: JSON.stringify(cmd)
    }).then(function(r) { return r.json(); });
}

exports.handler = async function(event) {
    if (event.httpMethod === "OPTIONS") return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: "" };
    if (event.httpMethod !== "POST") return { statusCode: 405, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "POST only" }) };

    var redisUrl = process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_URL;
    var redisToken = process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_TOKEN;

    try {
        var body = JSON.parse(event.body || "{}");

        // === ENQUEUE TASKS (from frontend) ===
        if (body.action === "addTasks" || body.action === "addTask") {
            var userId = body.userId;
            if (!userId) return { statusCode: 400, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "userId required" }) };

            var tasks = body.tasks || (body.task ? [body.task] : []);
            var current = await redis(redisUrl, redisToken, ["GET", "tasks:" + userId]);
            var all = [];
            if (current && current.result) {
                try { all = JSON.parse(current.result); } catch(e) { all = []; }
            }
            all = all.concat(tasks);
            await redis(redisUrl, redisToken, ["SET", "tasks:" + userId, JSON.stringify(all), "EX", "3600"]);

            return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ success: true, count: tasks.length }) };
        }

        // === AI CHAT ===
        var sessionToken = body.sessionToken;
        var messages = body.messages || [];
        var model = body.model || "llama-3.3-70b-versatile";
        var mode = body.mode || "quick"; // quick=1 credit, plan=3 credits

        if (!sessionToken) {
            return { statusCode: 401, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "LOGIN_REQUIRED" }) };
        }

        // Verify session
        var sessGet = await redis(redisUrl, redisToken, ["GET", "sess:" + sessionToken]);
        if (!sessGet || !sessGet.result) {
            return { statusCode: 401, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "INVALID_SESSION" }) };
        }
        var userId = sessGet.result;

        // Determine cost
        var cost = mode === "plan" ? 3 : 1;

        // Check and consume credits (atomic)
        var lua = [
            "local cur = tonumber(redis.call('GET', KEYS[1]) or '0')",
            "local cost = tonumber(ARGV[1])",
            "if cur <= 0 then return -1 end",
            "if cur < cost then return -2 end",
            "redis.call('DECRBY', KEYS[1], cost)",
            "redis.call('INCRBY', KEYS[2], 1)",
            "return tonumber(redis.call('GET', KEYS[1]) or '0')"
        ].join("\n");

        var evalRes = await redis(redisUrl, redisToken, [
            "EVAL", lua, "2",
            "credits:" + userId,
            "usage:" + userId,
            String(cost)
        ]);

        var remaining = evalRes ? evalRes.result : -1;

        if (remaining === -1) {
            return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "NO_CREDITS", credits: 0 }) };
        }
        if (remaining === -2) {
            return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "NOT_ENOUGH", credits: 0 }) };
        }

        // Call Groq
        var groqKey = process.env.GROQ_API_KEY;
        if (!groqKey) {
            return { statusCode: 500, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "GROQ_API_KEY missing" }) };
        }

        var aiRes = await fetch("https://api.groq.com/openai/v1/chat/completions", {
            method: "POST",
            headers: {
                "Content-Type": "application/json",
                "Authorization": "Bearer " + groqKey
            },
            body: JSON.stringify({
                model: model,
                messages: messages,
                max_tokens: 8000,
                temperature: 0.5
            })
        });

        if (!aiRes.ok) {
            var errData = await aiRes.json();
            // Refund credit on error
            await redis(redisUrl, redisToken, ["INCRBY", "credits:" + userId, String(cost)]);
            return {
                statusCode: aiRes.status,
                headers,
                body: JSON.stringify({ error: errData.error ? errData.error.message : "Groq error" })
            };
        }

        var data = await aiRes.json();
        var content = "Brak odpowiedzi";
        if (data.choices && data.choices[0] && data.choices[0].message) {
            content = data.choices[0].message.content;
        }

        // Save to history
        var histKey = "history:" + userId;
        var histGet = await redis(redisUrl, redisToken, ["GET", histKey]);
        var history = [];
        if (histGet && histGet.result) {
            try { history = JSON.parse(histGet.result); } catch(e) { history = []; }
        }
        history.push({
            timestamp: Date.now(),
            userMsg: messages.length > 0 ? messages[messages.length - 1].content : "",
            aiMsg: content.substring(0, 500), // save first 500 chars
            mode: mode,
            cost: cost
        });
        // Keep last 50
        if (history.length > 50) history = history.slice(-50);
        await redis(redisUrl, redisToken, ["SET", histKey, JSON.stringify(history), "EX", String(60 * 60 * 24 * 30)]);

        // Get usage
        var usageGet = await redis(redisUrl, redisToken, ["GET", "usage:" + userId]);
        var usage = usageGet && usageGet.result ? parseInt(usageGet.result, 10) : 0;

        return {
            statusCode: 200,
            headers,
            body: JSON.stringify({
                content: content,
                credits: remaining,
                usage: usage,
                cost: cost
            })
        };

    } catch (err) {
        return { statusCode: 500, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: err.message }) };
    }
};
5. netlify/functions/credits-get.js (NOWY)
JavaScript

var headers = {
    "Access-Control-Allow-Origin": "*",
    "Access-Control-Allow-Headers": "Content-Type",
    "Access-Control-Allow-Methods": "GET, OPTIONS",
    "Content-Type": "application/json"
};

function redis(url, token, cmd) {
    return fetch(url, {
        method: "POST",
        headers: { "Authorization": "Bearer " + token, "Content-Type": "application/json" },
        body: JSON.stringify(cmd)
    }).then(function(r) { return r.json(); });
}

exports.handler = async function(event) {
    if (event.httpMethod === "OPTIONS") return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: "" };

    var qs = event.queryStringParameters || {};
    var sessionToken = qs.sessionToken;
    if (!sessionToken) return { statusCode: 400, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "sessionToken required" }) };

    var redisUrl = process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_URL;
    var redisToken = process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_TOKEN;

    var sessGet = await redis(redisUrl, redisToken, ["GET", "sess:" + sessionToken]);
    if (!sessGet || !sessGet.result) {
        return { statusCode: 401, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "INVALID_SESSION" }) };
    }

    var userId = sessGet.result;
    var credGet = await redis(redisUrl, redisToken, ["GET", "credits:" + userId]);
    var credits = credGet && credGet.result ? parseInt(credGet.result, 10) : 0;

    var usageGet = await redis(redisUrl, redisToken, ["GET", "usage:" + userId]);
    var usage = usageGet && usageGet.result ? parseInt(usageGet.result, 10) : 0;

    return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ credits: credits, usage: usage, userId: userId }) };
};
6. netlify/functions/admin.js (NOWY)
JavaScript

var headers = {
    "Access-Control-Allow-Origin": "*",
    "Access-Control-Allow-Headers": "Content-Type",
    "Access-Control-Allow-Methods": "POST, OPTIONS",
    "Content-Type": "application/json"
};

function redis(url, token, cmd) {
    return fetch(url, {
        method: "POST",
        headers: { "Authorization": "Bearer " + token, "Content-Type": "application/json" },
        body: JSON.stringify(cmd)
    }).then(function(r) { return r.json(); });
}

exports.handler = async function(event) {
    if (event.httpMethod === "OPTIONS") return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: "" };
    if (event.httpMethod !== "POST") return { statusCode: 405, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "POST only" }) };

    try {
        var body = JSON.parse(event.body || "{}");
        var password = body.password;
        var action = body.action;

        var adminPass = process.env.ADMIN_PASSWORD || "SIGMAOHIO";

        if (!password || password !== adminPass) {
            return { statusCode: 403, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "FORBIDDEN" }) };
        }

        var redisUrl = process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_URL;
        var redisToken = process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_TOKEN;

        // Add credits
        if (action === "addCredits") {
            var targetUser = body.userId;
            var amount = Number(body.amount);

            if (!targetUser) return { statusCode: 400, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "userId required" }) };
            if (!amount || amount <= 0) return { statusCode: 400, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "amount invalid" }) };

            await redis(redisUrl, redisToken, ["INCRBY", "credits:" + targetUser, String(amount)]);

            var after = await redis(redisUrl, redisToken, ["GET", "credits:" + targetUser]);
            var newCredits = after && after.result ? parseInt(after.result, 10) : 0;

            return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ ok: true, userId: targetUser, added: amount, total: newCredits }) };
        }

        // Get user info
        if (action === "getUser") {
            var lookupUser = body.userId;
            if (!lookupUser) return { statusCode: 400, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "userId required" }) };

            var userData = await redis(redisUrl, redisToken, ["GET", "userdata:" + lookupUser]);
            var credData = await redis(redisUrl, redisToken, ["GET", "credits:" + lookupUser]);
            var usageData = await redis(redisUrl, redisToken, ["GET", "usage:" + lookupUser]);

            var user = userData && userData.result ? JSON.parse(userData.result) : null;
            var creds = credData && credData.result ? parseInt(credData.result, 10) : 0;
            var usage = usageData && usageData.result ? parseInt(usageData.result, 10) : 0;

            if (!user) return { statusCode: 404, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "User not found" }) };

            return {
                statusCode: 200,
                headers,
                body: JSON.stringify({
                    userId: user.userId,
                    username: user.username,
                    email: user.email,
                    credits: creds,
                    usage: usage,
                    createdAt: user.createdAt
                })
            };
        }

        // Set credits
        if (action === "setCredits") {
            var setUser = body.userId;
            var setAmount = Number(body.amount);

            if (!setUser) return { statusCode: 400, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "userId required" }) };

            await redis(redisUrl, redisToken, ["SET", "credits:" + setUser, String(setAmount), "EX", String(60 * 60 * 24 * 365)]);

            return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ ok: true, userId: setUser, credits: setAmount }) };
        }

        return { statusCode: 400, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "Unknown admin action" }) };

    } catch (err) {
        return { statusCode: 500, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: err.message }) };
    }
};
7. netlify/functions/history.js (NOWY)
JavaScript

var headers = {
    "Access-Control-Allow-Origin": "*",
    "Access-Control-Allow-Headers": "Content-Type",
    "Access-Control-Allow-Methods": "GET, OPTIONS",
    "Content-Type": "application/json"
};

function redis(url, token, cmd) {
    return fetch(url, {
        method: "POST",
        headers: { "Authorization": "Bearer " + token, "Content-Type": "application/json" },
        body: JSON.stringify(cmd)
    }).then(function(r) { return r.json(); });
}

exports.handler = async function(event) {
    if (event.httpMethod === "OPTIONS") return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: "" };

    var qs = event.queryStringParameters || {};
    var sessionToken = qs.sessionToken;
    if (!sessionToken) return { statusCode: 400, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "sessionToken required" }) };

    var redisUrl = process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_URL;
    var redisToken = process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_TOKEN;

    var sessGet = await redis(redisUrl, redisToken, ["GET", "sess:" + sessionToken]);
    if (!sessGet || !sessGet.result) {
        return { statusCode: 401, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "INVALID_SESSION" }) };
    }

    var userId = sessGet.result;
    var histGet = await redis(redisUrl, redisToken, ["GET", "history:" + userId]);
    var history = [];
    if (histGet && histGet.result) {
        try { history = JSON.parse(histGet.result); } catch(e) { history = []; }
    }

    return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ history: history }) };
};
8. netlify/functions/queue-dequeue.js (NOWY)
JavaScript

var headers = {
    "Access-Control-Allow-Origin": "*",
    "Access-Control-Allow-Headers": "Content-Type",
    "Access-Control-Allow-Methods": "GET, OPTIONS",
    "Content-Type": "application/json"
};

function redis(url, token, cmd) {
    return fetch(url, {
        method: "POST",
        headers: { "Authorization": "Bearer " + token, "Content-Type": "application/json" },
        body: JSON.stringify(cmd)
    }).then(function(r) { return r.json(); });
}

exports.handler = async function(event) {
    if (event.httpMethod === "OPTIONS") return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: "" };
    if (event.httpMethod !== "GET") return { statusCode: 405, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "GET only" }) };

    var qs = event.queryStringParameters || {};
    var connectCode = qs.connectCode;

    if (!connectCode) return { statusCode: 400, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "connectCode required" }) };

    var redisUrl = process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_URL;
    var redisToken = process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_TOKEN;

    // Resolve connect code to userId
    var connGet = await redis(redisUrl, redisToken, ["GET", "connect:" + connectCode]);
    if (!connGet || !connGet.result) {
        return { statusCode: 401, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "INVALID_CODE", tasks: [] }) };
    }

    var userId = connGet.result;

    // Get tasks
    var taskGet = await redis(redisUrl, redisToken, ["GET", "tasks:" + userId]);
    var tasks = [];
    if (taskGet && taskGet.result) {
        try { tasks = JSON.parse(taskGet.result); } catch(e) { tasks = []; }
    }

    // Clear after fetch
    if (tasks.length > 0) {
        await redis(redisUrl, redisToken, ["DEL", "tasks:" + userId]);
    }

    return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ tasks: tasks, count: tasks.length, userId: userId }) };
};

Lua

local SERVER = "https://fleetyai.netlify.app"
local DELAY = 2

local Http = game:GetService("HttpService")
local Sel = game:GetService("Selection")
local CHS = game:GetService("ChangeHistoryService")

local bar = plugin:CreateToolbar("RoboAI")
local mainBtn = bar:CreateButton("RoboAI", "AI Assistant", "rbxassetid://4458901886")
local wInfo = DockWidgetPluginGuiInfo.new(Enum.InitialDockState.Right, false, false, 300, 450, 260, 300)

local function make(c, p)
    local i = Instance.new(c)
    for k,v in pairs(p) do if k ~= "Parent" then i[k] = v end end
    if p.Parent then i.Parent = p.Parent end
    return i
end

local active = false
local logN = 0
local totalOps = 0

local function log(msg)
    logN = logN + 1
    make("TextLabel", {
        Size=UDim2.new(1,0,0,0), AutomaticSize=Enum.AutomaticSize.Y, BackgroundTransparency=1,
        RichText=true, Text='<font color="#3a6090">['..os.date("%H:%M:%S")..']</font> '..msg,
        TextColor3=Color3.fromRGB(140,170,210), Font=Enum.Font.RobotoMono, TextSize=9,
        TextXAlignment=Enum.TextXAlignment.Left, TextWrapped=true, LayoutOrder=logN, Parent=logBox
    })
    task.defer(function() logBox.CanvasPosition = Vector2.new(0, logBox.AbsoluteCanvasSize.Y) end)
end

local function getParent(n)
    local m = {
        ServerScriptService = game:GetService("ServerScriptService"),
        ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"),
        ServerStorage = game:GetService("ServerStorage"),
        Workspace = workspace,
        StarterPlayerScripts = game:GetService("StarterPlayer"):FindFirstChild("StarterPlayerScripts"),
    }
    return m[n] or game:GetService("StarterGui")
end

local function findScript(name, parent)
    local p = getParent(parent)
    for _, child in ipairs(p:GetChildren()) do
        if child.Name == name and (child:IsA("BaseScript") or child:IsA("ModuleScript")) then
            return child
        end
    end
    return nil
end

local function runTask(t, idx, total)
    local name = t.scriptName or "Script"
    local stype = t.scriptType or "LocalScript"
    local parent = t.parent or "StarterGui"
    local action = t.action or "create"
    local prefix = total > 1 and ("["..idx.."/"..total.."] ") or ""

    if action == "delete" then
        log('<font color="#ffd166">🗑 '..prefix..'Usuwanie: '..name..'</font>')
        local e = findScript(name, parent)
        if e then e:Destroy() log('<font color="#2ce6a6">✅ Usunieto</font>') else log('<font color="#ffd166">⚠ Nie znaleziono</font>') end
    elseif action == "update" then
        log('<font color="#22a7ff">✏️ '..prefix..'Update: '..name..'</font>')
        local e = findScript(name, parent)
        if e then e.Source = t.code Sel:Set({e}) CHS:SetWaypoint("Update "..name) log('<font color="#2ce6a6">✅ Zaktualizowano</font>')
        else action = "create" end
    end

    if action == "create" then
        log('<font color="#22a7ff">📝 '..prefix..name..'</font>')
        task.wait(0.3)
        local ok, err = pcall(function()
            local old = findScript(name, parent)
            if old then old:Destroy() end
            local inst
            if stype == "ModuleScript" then inst = Instance.new("ModuleScript")
            elseif stype == "Script" then inst = Instance.new("Script")
            else inst = Instance.new("LocalScript") end
            inst.Source = t.code
            inst.Name = name
            inst.Parent = getParent(parent)
            Sel:Set({inst})
            CHS:SetWaypoint("RoboAI: "..name)
        end)
        if ok then log('<font color="#2ce6a6">✅ '..name..' → '..parent..'</font>')
        else log('<font color="#ff4d6d">❌ '..tostring(err)..'</font>') end
    end

    totalOps = totalOps + 1
    statsLbl.Text = totalOps.." operacji"
end

local function poll(code)
    local ok = pcall(function()
        local url = SERVER.."/.netlify/functions/queue-dequeue?connectCode="..code
        local resp = Http:GetAsync(url, true)
        local data = Http:JSONDecode(resp)

        if data.error == "INVALID_CODE" then
            log('<font color="#ff4d6d">❌ Nieprawidlowy kod!</font>')
            active = false
            return
        end

        if data.tasks and #data.tasks > 0 then
            log('<font color="#22a7ff">📦 '..#data.tasks..' operacji</font>')
            table.sort(data.tasks, function(a,b) return (a.order or 0) < (b.order or 0) end)
            for i, t in ipairs(data.tasks) do
                runTask(t, i, #data.tasks)
                if i < #data.tasks then task.wait(0.4) end
            end
            log('<font color="#2ce6a6">✅ Gotowe!</font>')
        end
    end)

    if ok then
        sDot.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(44,230,166)
        sTxt.Text = "Polaczono"
        sTxt.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(44,230,166)
    else
        sDot.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255,209,102)
        sTxt.Text = "Blad"
    end
end

local function start()
    local code = codeInput.Text:match("^%s*(.-)%s*$")
    if not code or code == "" then
        log('<font color="#ff4d6d">Wpisz Connect Code ze strony!</font>')
        return
    end

    -- Save code
    plugin:SetSetting("RoboAI_ConnectCode", code)

    if active then return end
    active = true
    goBtn.Text = "⏸ ROZLACZ"
    goBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255,77,109)
    log('<font color="#2ce6a6">🚀 Polaczono!</font>')
    log('<font color="#22a7ff">Kod: '..code:sub(1,8)..'...</font>')

    task.spawn(function()
        while active do
            poll(code)
            task.wait(DELAY)
        end
    end)
end

local function stop()
    active = false
    goBtn.Text = "▶ CONNECT"
    goBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0,180,220)
    sDot.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255,209,102)
    sTxt.Text = "Rozlaczono"
    sTxt.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255,209,102)
    log('<font color="#ffd166">⏸ Stop</font>')
end

goBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function() if active then stop() else start() end end)
mainBtn.Click:Connect(function() w.Enabled = not w.Enabled end)
log('<font color="#22a7ff">🌊 RoboAI v6</font>')
log('<font color="#6ea2d6">Wpisz Connect Code i kliknij CONNECT</font>')

var redisUrl = process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_URL;
var redisToken = process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_TOKEN;

try {
    var body = JSON.parse(event.body);

    // STORE TASKS
    if (body.action === "addTasks" || body.action === "addTask") {
        if (!redisUrl || !redisToken) {
            return { statusCode: 500, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ success: false, error: "Redis not configured" }) };
        }

        var pluginKey = body.pluginKey;
        var newTasks = body.tasks || [body.task];

        // Get existing
        var getRes = await fetch(redisUrl + "/get/" + pluginKey, {
            headers: { "Authorization": "Bearer " + redisToken }
        });
        var getData = await getRes.json();

        var allTasks = [];
        if (getData.result && getData.result !== null) {
            try {
                allTasks = JSON.parse(getData.result);
            } catch(e) {
                allTasks = [];
            }
        }

        for (var i = 0; i < newTasks.length; i++) {
            allTasks.push(newTasks[i]);
        }

        // Save as string using SET with POST body
        var saveRes = await fetch(redisUrl, {
            method: "POST",
            headers: {
                "Authorization": "Bearer " + redisToken,
                "Content-Type": "application/json"
            },
            body: JSON.stringify(["SET", pluginKey, JSON.stringify(allTasks), "EX", "3600"])
        });
        var saveData = await saveRes.json();

        return {
            statusCode: 200,
            headers,
            body: JSON.stringify({ success: true, count: newTasks.length, total: allTasks.length, redis: saveData })
        };
    }

    // AI CHAT
    var apiKey = body.apiKey;
    var messages = body.messages;
    var model = body.model;
    var testMode = body.testMode;

    if (!apiKey) {
        return { statusCode: 400, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "Brak klucza API" }) };
    }

    if (testMode) {
        var test = await fetch("https://api.groq.com/openai/v1/models", {
            headers: { "Authorization": "Bearer " + apiKey }
        });
        return {
            statusCode: test.ok ? 200 : 401,
            headers,
            body: JSON.stringify(test.ok ? { success: true } : { error: "Zly klucz API Groq" })
        };
    }

    var aiRes = await fetch("https://api.groq.com/openai/v1/chat/completions", {
        method: "POST",
        headers: {
            "Content-Type": "application/json",
            "Authorization": "Bearer " + apiKey
        },
        body: JSON.stringify({
            model: model || "llama-3.3-70b-versatile",
            messages: messages,
            max_tokens: 8000,
            temperature: 0.7
        })
    });

    if (!aiRes.ok) {
        var errData = await aiRes.json();
        return {
            statusCode: aiRes.status,
            headers,
            body: JSON.stringify({ error: errData.error ? errData.error.message : "Blad Groq" })
        };
    }

    var data = await aiRes.json();
    var content = "Brak odpowiedzi";
    if (data.choices && data.choices[0] && data.choices[0].message) {
        content = data.choices[0].message.content;
    }

    return {
        statusCode: 200,
        headers,
        body: JSON.stringify({ content: content })
    };

} catch (err) {
    return {
        statusCode: 500,
        headers,
        body: JSON.stringify({ error: "Server error: " + err.message })
    };
}

Zrobię, ale muszę powiedzieć jedną rzecz techniczną (żeby nie było kolejnych “czemu nie działa”):

Roblox Plugin nie ma dostępu do konta Google w przeglądarce, więc nie da się go “w 100% automatycznie” zmapować do użytkownika bez żadnego kodu/sesji.
Da się natomiast zrobić tak jak lemonade.ai:

✅ 1 raz (na użytkownika) “Connect code”
✅ potem plugin sam się łączy zawsze (bo zapisze token w ustawieniach pluginu)
✅ każda osoba ma własne queue/tasky, kredyty i historię
✅ admin ma panel z hasłem SIGMAOHIO (serwerowo)

Poniżej masz kompletny plan i kluczowe pliki.

A) Architektura (per-user jak w lemonade)
Redis keys

credits:{userId} – kredyty
usage:{userId} – użycia/wywołania
history:{userId} – historia czatów (JSON)
tasks:{userId} – kolejka zadań dla pluginu
sess:{sessionToken} – mapowanie token → userId
Przepływ

Użytkownik loguje się na stronie (Google via Netlify Identity)
Strona tworzy sessionToken dla Roblox Studio: /session-create
Użytkownik wklei ten token w plugin (raz na zawsze)
Plugin po prostu polluje /queue-dequeue z tym tokenem
Gdy user wysyła prompt:
backend sprawdza kredyty i je zużywa
zapisuje zadania do tasks:{userId}
Plugin pobiera zadania i robi create/update/delete (nie tworzy duplikatów)
B) Potrzebne zmienne w Netlify (Env Vars)
W Netlify → Site configuration → Environment variables dodaj:

Obowiązkowe

GROQ_API_KEY (albo Gemini, ale teraz masz Groq)
UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_URL (musisz mieć https://...)
UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_TOKEN
Admin

ADMIN_PASSWORD = SIGMAOHIO ✅ (serwerowo, nie w JS)
Stripe (opcjonalnie — jak chcesz prawdziwe kupowanie)

STRIPE_SECRET_KEY
STRIPE_WEBHOOK_SECRET
STRIPE_PRICE_ID_50
STRIPE_PRICE_ID_100
C) Backend (Netlify Functions) – pliki
1) netlify/functions/session-create.js
Tworzy token sesji dla zalogowanego usera.

JavaScript

const headers = {
  "Access-Control-Allow-Origin": "*",
  "Access-Control-Allow-Headers": "Content-Type",
  "Access-Control-Allow-Methods": "GET, POST, OPTIONS",
  "Content-Type": "application/json"
};

function redisCmd(redisUrl, redisToken, cmd) {
  return fetch(redisUrl, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: {
      "Authorization": `Bearer ${redisToken}`,
      "Content-Type": "application/json"
    },
    body: JSON.stringify(cmd)
  }).then(r => r.json());
}

exports.handler = async (event) => {
  if (event.httpMethod === "OPTIONS") return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: "" };
  if (event.httpMethod !== "POST") return { statusCode: 405, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "POST only" }) };

  const body = JSON.parse(event.body || "{}");
  const userId = body.userId;
  if (!userId) return { statusCode: 400, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "userId required" }) };

  const redisUrl = process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_URL;
  const redisToken = process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_TOKEN;

  // session token
  const token = "sess_" + require("crypto").randomBytes(12).toString("hex");
  const ttl = 60 * 60 * 24 * 30; // 30 dni

  // sess:{token} = userId
  await redisCmd(redisUrl, redisToken, ["SET", `sess:${token}`, userId, "EX", String(ttl)]);

  return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ sessionToken: token }) };
};
2) netlify/functions/queue-dequeue.js
Plugin pobiera tasks.

JavaScript

const headers = {
  "Access-Control-Allow-Origin": "*",
  "Access-Control-Allow-Headers": "Content-Type",
  "Access-Control-Allow-Methods": "GET, POST, OPTIONS",
  "Content-Type": "application/json"
};

function redisCmd(redisUrl, redisToken, cmd) {
  return fetch(redisUrl, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: {
      "Authorization": `Bearer ${redisToken}`,
      "Content-Type": "application/json"
    },
    body: JSON.stringify(cmd)
  }).then(r => r.json());
}

exports.handler = async (event) => {
  if (event.httpMethod === "OPTIONS") return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: "" };

  const method = event.httpMethod;

  const redisUrl = process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_URL;
  const redisToken = process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_TOKEN;

  if (!redisUrl || !redisToken) {
    return { statusCode: 500, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "Redis not configured" }) };
  }

  if (method === "GET") {
    const qs = event.queryStringParameters || {};
    const sessionToken = qs.sessionToken;
    if (!sessionToken) return { statusCode: 400, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "sessionToken required" }) };

    const sess = await redisCmd(redisUrl, redisToken, ["GET", `sess:${sessionToken}`]);
    const userId = sess?.result;
    if (!userId) return { statusCode: 401, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "INVALID_SESSION" }) };

    const getTasks = await redisCmd(redisUrl, redisToken, ["GET", `tasks:${userId}`]);
    let tasks = [];
    if (getTasks?.result) {
      try { tasks = JSON.parse(getTasks.result); } catch { tasks = []; }
    }

    if (tasks.length > 0) await redisCmd(redisUrl, redisToken, ["DEL", `tasks:${userId}`]);

    return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ tasks, count: tasks.length, userId }) };
  }

  return { statusCode: 405, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "Not allowed" }) };
};
3) netlify/functions/queue-enqueue.js
Backend wrzuca tasks (po wygenerowaniu kodu i zużyciu kredytów).

JavaScript

const headers = {
  "Access-Control-Allow-Origin": "*",
  "Access-Control-Allow-Headers": "Content-Type",
  "Access-Control-Allow-Methods": "GET, POST, OPTIONS",
  "Content-Type": "application/json"
};

function redisCmd(redisUrl, redisToken, cmd) {
  return fetch(redisUrl, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: {
      "Authorization": `Bearer ${redisToken}`,
      "Content-Type": "application/json"
    },
    body: JSON.stringify(cmd)
  }).then(r => r.json());
}

exports.handler = async (event) => {
  if (event.httpMethod === "OPTIONS") return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: "" };
  if (event.httpMethod !== "POST") return { statusCode: 405, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "POST only" }) };

  const body = JSON.parse(event.body || "{}");
  const userId = body.userId;
  const tasks = body.tasks || [];

  if (!userId) return { statusCode: 400, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "userId required" }) };
  if (!Array.isArray(tasks) || tasks.length === 0) return { statusCode: 400, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "tasks required" }) };

  const redisUrl = process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_URL;
  const redisToken = process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_TOKEN;

  const current = await redisCmd(redisUrl, redisToken, ["GET", `tasks:${userId}`]);
  let all = [];
  if (current?.result) {
    try { all = JSON.parse(current.result); } catch { all = []; }
  }

  all = all.concat(tasks);

  await redisCmd(redisUrl, redisToken, ["SET", `tasks:${userId}`, JSON.stringify(all), "EX", "3600"]);

  return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ ok: true, added: tasks.length, total: all.length }) };
};

JavaScript

const headers = {
  "Access-Control-Allow-Origin": "*",
  "Access-Control-Allow-Headers": "Content-Type",
  "Access-Control-Allow-Methods": "POST, OPTIONS",
  "Content-Type": "application/json"
};

function redisCmd(redisUrl, redisToken, cmd) {
  return fetch(redisUrl, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: { "Authorization": `Bearer ${redisToken}`, "Content-Type": "application/json" },
    body: JSON.stringify(cmd)
  }).then(r => r.json());
}

exports.handler = async (event) => {
  if (event.httpMethod === "OPTIONS") return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: "" };
  if (event.httpMethod !== "POST") return { statusCode: 405, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "POST only" }) };

  const body = JSON.parse(event.body || "{}");
  const password = body.password;
  const targetUserId = body.userId;
  const amount = Number(body.amount);

  if (!password || password !== process.env.ADMIN_PASSWORD) {
    return { statusCode: 403, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "FORBIDDEN" }) };
  }
  if (!targetUserId) return { statusCode: 400, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "userId required" }) };
  if (!Number.isFinite(amount) || amount <= 0) return { statusCode: 400, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "amount invalid" }) };

  const redisUrl = process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_URL;
  const redisToken = process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_TOKEN;

  await redisCmd(redisUrl, redisToken, ["INCRBY", `credits:${targetUserId}`, String(amount)]);

  return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ ok: true, userId: targetUserId, added: amount }) };
};
D) Plugin – “automatycznie łączy osobno”
Twój plugin musi pollować queue-dequeue po sessionToken, a nie po pluginKey.

Wersja “Lemonade style”:

po pierwszym połączeniu plugin zapisuje sessionToken przez plugin:SetSetting.
potem nie pyta — tylko działa.
✅ Przerobię Ci plugin, ale potrzebuję 1 rzeczy: wklej obecny RoboAI.lua, którego używasz.

4) Backend: Netlify Functions (kredyty + Groq + zasilanie zadań)
4.1 netlify/functions/chat.js (ZAMIEŃ CAŁY)
To jest kluczowe: w tej funkcji:

action: addTasks => zapis zadań do pluginu (bez kredytów)
normalny chat => zużywa kredyt i dopiero odpala Groq
Wklej jako cały plik netlify/functions/chat.js:

JavaScript

const headers = {
  "Access-Control-Allow-Origin": "*",
  "Access-Control-Allow-Headers": "Content-Type",
  "Access-Control-Allow-Methods": "GET, POST, OPTIONS",
  "Content-Type": "application/json"
};

function upstashCmd(redisUrl, redisToken, arr) {
  return fetch(redisUrl, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: {
      "Authorization": `Bearer ${redisToken}`,
      "Content-Type": "application/json"
    },
    body: JSON.stringify(arr)
  }).then(r => r.json());
}

async function ensureCredits(redisUrl, redisToken, userId) {
  const creditsKey = `credits:${userId}`;
  const usageKey = `usage:${userId}`;

  const got = await upstashCmd(redisUrl, redisToken, ["GET", creditsKey]);
  const gotCredits = got?.result ? parseInt(got.result, 10) : 0;
  if (!Number.isFinite(gotCredits) || gotCredits <= 0) {
    // start kredytów demo: 20
    await upstashCmd(redisUrl, redisToken, ["SET", creditsKey, "20", "EX", String(60 * 60 * 24 * 30)]);
  }

  const gotU = await upstashCmd(redisUrl, redisToken, ["GET", usageKey]);
  const gotUsage = gotU?.result ? parseInt(gotU.result, 10) : 0;
  if (!Number.isFinite(gotUsage)) {
    await upstashCmd(redisUrl, redisToken, ["SET", usageKey, "0", "EX", String(60 * 60 * 24 * 30)]);
  }
}

exports.handler = async (event) => {
  if (event.httpMethod === "OPTIONS") {
    return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: "" };
  }

  if (event.httpMethod !== "POST") {
    return { statusCode: 405, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "POST only" }) };
  }

  try {
    const body = JSON.parse(event.body || "{}");

    // ---- 1) PLUGIN TASK ENQUEUE (bez kredytów)
    if (body.action === "addTasks" || body.action === "addTask") {
      const pluginKey = body.pluginKey;
      if (!pluginKey) return { statusCode: 400, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "pluginKey required" }) };

      const tasks = body.tasks || (body.task ? [body.task] : []);
      const redisUrl = process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_URL;
      const redisToken = process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_TOKEN;

      const get = await upstashCmd(redisUrl, redisToken, ["GET", pluginKey]);
      let existing = [];
      if (get?.result) {
        try { existing = JSON.parse(get.result); } catch { existing = []; }
      }

      const all = existing.concat(tasks);
      await upstashCmd(redisUrl, redisToken, ["SET", pluginKey, JSON.stringify(all), "EX", "3600"]);

      return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ success: true, count: tasks.length }) };
    }

    // ---- 2) AI CHAT (zużywa kredyt)
    const userId = body.userId;
    const model = body.model || "llama-3.3-70b-versatile";
    const messages = body.messages || [];

    if (!userId) {
      return { statusCode: 401, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "LOGIN_REQUIRED" }) };
    }

    const cost = Number(body.cost || 1);

    const redisUrl = process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_URL;
    const redisToken = process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_TOKEN;

    await ensureCredits(redisUrl, redisToken, userId);

    const creditsKey = `credits:${userId}`;
    const usageKey = `usage:${userId}`;

    const lua = `
      local cur = tonumber(redis.call("GET", KEYS[1]) or "0")
      local cost = tonumber(ARGV[1])
      if cur <= 0 then return -1 end
      if cur < cost then return -2 end
      redis.call("DECRBY", KEYS[1], cost)
      redis.call("INCRBY", KEYS[2], 1)
      local after = tonumber(redis.call("GET", KEYS[1]) or "0")
      return after
    `.trim();

    const evalRes = await upstashCmd(redisUrl, redisToken, [
      "EVAL",
      lua,
      "2",
      creditsKey,
      usageKey,
      String(cost)
    ]);

    const remaining = evalRes?.result;

    if (remaining === -1) {
      return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "NO_CREDITS" }) };
    }
    if (remaining === -2) {
      return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "NOT_ENOUGH" }) };
    }

    // Call Groq
    const groqApiKey = process.env.GROQ_API_KEY;
    if (!groqApiKey) {
      return { statusCode: 500, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "GROQ_API_KEY missing" }) };
    }

    const aiRes = await fetch("https://api.groq.com/openai/v1/chat/completions", {
      method: "POST",
      headers: {
        "Content-Type": "application/json",
        "Authorization": `Bearer ${groqApiKey}`
      },
      body: JSON.stringify({
        model,
        messages,
        temperature: 0.4,
        max_tokens: 6000
      })
    });

    const aiData = await aiRes.json();
    if (!aiRes.ok) {
      return { statusCode: aiRes.status, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: aiData?.error?.message || "GROQ_ERROR" }) };
    }

    const content =
      aiData?.choices?.[0]?.message?.content ||
      "";

    // fetch usage for UI
    const usageGet = await upstashCmd(redisUrl, redisToken, ["GET", usageKey]);
    const usage = usageGet?.result ? parseInt(usageGet.result, 10) : 0;

    return {
      statusCode: 200,
      headers,
      body: JSON.stringify({
        content,
        remainingCredits: remaining,
        usage
      })
    };

  } catch (err) {
    return { statusCode: 500, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: err.message }) };
  }
};
Ten chat.js już obsługuje: AI chat + enqueue zadań do pluginu.

4.2 netlify/functions/credits-get.js (NOWY)
Utwórz plik: netlify/functions/credits-get.js

JavaScript

const headers = {
  "Access-Control-Allow-Origin": "*",
  "Access-Control-Allow-Headers": "Content-Type",
  "Access-Control-Allow-Methods": "GET, POST, OPTIONS",
  "Content-Type": "application/json"
};

function upstashCmd(redisUrl, redisToken, arr) {
  return fetch(redisUrl, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: { "Authorization": `Bearer ${redisToken}`, "Content-Type": "application/json" },
    body: JSON.stringify(arr)
  }).then(r => r.json());
}

exports.handler = async (event) => {
  if (event.httpMethod === "OPTIONS") return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: "" };
  if (event.httpMethod !== "GET") return { statusCode: 405, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "GET only" }) };

  const qs = event.queryStringParameters || {};
  const userId = qs.userId;
  if (!userId) return { statusCode: 400, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "userId required" }) };

  const redisUrl = process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_URL;
  const redisToken = process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_TOKEN;

  const creditsKey = `credits:${userId}`;
  const usageKey = `usage:${userId}`;

  const got = await upstashCmd(redisUrl, redisToken, ["GET", creditsKey]);
  let credits = got?.result ? parseInt(got.result, 10) : 0;
  if (!Number.isFinite(credits) || credits <= 0) {
    await upstashCmd(redisUrl, redisToken, ["SET", creditsKey, "20", "EX", String(60 * 60 * 24 * 30)]);
    credits = 20;
  }

  const usageGet = await upstashCmd(redisUrl, redisToken, ["GET", usageKey]);
  const usage = usageGet?.result ? parseInt(usageGet.result, 10) : 0;

  return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ credits, usage }) };
};

netlify/functions/stripe-create-checkout.js (NOWY)
JavaScript

const Stripe = require("stripe");

const headers = {
  "Access-Control-Allow-Origin": "*",
  "Access-Control-Allow-Headers": "Content-Type",
  "Access-Control-Allow-Methods": "GET, POST, OPTIONS",
  "Content-Type": "application/json"
};

exports.handler = async (event) => {
  if (event.httpMethod === "OPTIONS") return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: "" };
  if (event.httpMethod !== "POST") return { statusCode: 405, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "POST only" }) };

  try {
    const body = JSON.parse(event.body || "{}");
    const userId = body.userId;
    const credits = Number(body.credits);

    if (!userId) return { statusCode: 401, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "LOGIN_REQUIRED" }) };
    if (![50,100].includes(credits)) return { statusCode: 400, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "credits must be 50 or 100" }) };

    const priceId = credits === 50 ? process.env.STRIPE_PRICE_ID_50 : process.env.STRIPE_PRICE_ID_100;
    if (!priceId) return { statusCode: 500, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "Stripe Price not configured" }) };

    const stripe = new Stripe(process.env.STRIPE_SECRET_KEY);

    // success/cancel z frontu (polecam)
    const successUrl = body.successUrl || process.env.STRIPE_SUCCESS_URL || "https://fleetyai.netlify.app/";
    const cancelUrl = body.cancelUrl || process.env.STRIPE_CANCEL_URL || "https://fleetyai.netlify.app/";

    const session = await stripe.checkout.sessions.create({
      mode: "payment",
      line_items: [{ price: priceId, quantity: 1 }],
      success_url: successUrl + "?checkout=success",
      cancel_url: cancelUrl + "?checkout=cancel",
      metadata: {
        userId,
        credits: String(credits)
      }
    });

    return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ url: session.url }) };
  } catch (err) {
    return { statusCode: 500, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: err.message }) };
  }
};
netlify/functions/stripe-webhook.js (NOWY)
JavaScript

const Stripe = require("stripe");

const headers = {
  "Access-Control-Allow-Origin": "*",
  "Access-Control-Allow-Headers": "*",
  "Access-Control-Allow-Methods": "POST, OPTIONS",
  "Content-Type": "application/json"
};

exports.handler = async (event) => {
  if (event.httpMethod === "OPTIONS") return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: "" };
  if (event.httpMethod !== "POST") return { statusCode: 405, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "POST only" }) };

  try {
    const stripe = new Stripe(process.env.STRIPE_SECRET_KEY);
    const signature = event.headers["stripe-signature"];

    // Zostaw event.body jako string (Netlify zwykle daje body string)
    const rawBody = event.body || "";

    const evt = stripe.webhooks.constructEvent(
      rawBody,
      signature,
      process.env.STRIPE_WEBHOOK_SECRET
    );

    if (evt.type === "checkout.session.completed") {
      const session = evt.data.object;

      const userId = session.metadata?.userId;
      const credits = Number(session.metadata?.credits || "0");

      if (userId && [50,100].includes(credits)) {
        const redisUrl = process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_URL;
        const redisToken = process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_TOKEN;

        const cmd = (arr) => fetch(redisUrl, {
          method: "POST",
          headers: { "Authorization": `Bearer ${redisToken}`, "Content-Type": "application/json" },
          body: JSON.stringify(arr)
        }).then(r => r.json());

        // idempotencja
        const processedKey = `stripe:processed:${session.id}`;
        const already = await cmd(["GET", processedKey]);

        if (!already?.result) {
          await cmd(["SET", processedKey, "1", "EX", "86400"]);
          await cmd(["INCRBY", `credits:${userId}`, String(credits)]);
        }
      }
    }

    return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ received: true }) };
  } catch (err) {
    return { statusCode: 400, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: err.message }) };
  }
};

A) netlify/functions/credits-get.js
Utwórz plik:

JavaScript

exports.handler = async (event) => {
  const headers = {
    "Access-Control-Allow-Origin": "*",
    "Access-Control-Allow-Headers": "Content-Type",
    "Access-Control-Allow-Methods": "GET, POST, OPTIONS",
    "Content-Type": "application/json"
  };

  if (event.httpMethod === "OPTIONS") return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: "" };

  const qs = event.queryStringParameters || {};
  const userId = qs.userId;
  if (!userId) return { statusCode: 400, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "userId required" }) };

  const redisUrl = process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_URL;
  const redisToken = process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_TOKEN;
  const key = `credits:${userId}`;

  // Zwróć 0 jeśli brak
  const res = await fetch(redisUrl, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: { "Authorization": `Bearer ${redisToken}`, "Content-Type": "application/json" },
    body: JSON.stringify(["GET", key])
  });
  const data = await res.json();

  let credits = 0;
  if (data?.result) {
    credits = parseInt(data.result, 10);
    if (Number.isNaN(credits)) credits = 0;
  }

  // Ustaw pierwsze kredyty (demo)
  if (credits <= 0) {
    await fetch(redisUrl, {
      method: "POST",
      headers: { "Authorization": `Bearer ${redisToken}`, "Content-Type": "application/json" },
      body: JSON.stringify(["SET", key, "20", "EX", "2592000"]) // 30 dni
    });
    credits = 20;
  }

  return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ credits }) };
};
B) netlify/functions/credits-consume.js
JavaScript

exports.handler = async (event) => {
  const headers = {
    "Access-Control-Allow-Origin": "*",
    "Access-Control-Allow-Headers": "Content-Type",
    "Access-Control-Allow-Methods": "GET, POST, OPTIONS",
    "Content-Type": "application/json"
  };

  if (event.httpMethod === "OPTIONS") return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: "" };

  if (event.httpMethod !== "POST") return { statusCode: 405, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "POST only" }) };

  const body = JSON.parse(event.body || "{}");
  const userId = body.userId;
  const cost = Number(body.cost || 1);
  if (!userId) return { statusCode: 400, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "userId required" }) };

  const redisUrl = process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_URL;
  const redisToken = process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_TOKEN;
  const key = `credits:${userId}`;

  // Atomic check+decrement (EVAL)
  const lua = `
    local current = tonumber(redis.call("GET", KEYS[1]) or "0")
    local cost = tonumber(ARGV[1])
    if current <= 0 then return -1 end
    if current < cost then return -2 end
    redis.call("DECRBY", KEYS[1], cost)
    local after = tonumber(redis.call("GET", KEYS[1]) or "0")
    return after
  `.trim();

  const res = await fetch(redisUrl, {
    method: "POST",
    headers: { "Authorization": `Bearer ${redisToken}`, "Content-Type": "application/json" },
    body: JSON.stringify(["EVAL", lua, "1", key, String(cost)])
  });

  const data = await res.json();
  const after = data?.result;

  if (after === -1) return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ ok:false, code:"NO_CREDITS" }) };
  if (after === -2) return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ ok:false, code:"NOT_ENOUGH" }) };

  return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ ok:true, credits: after }) };
};
