JavaScript

var App = {
    apiKey: localStorage.getItem('roboai_key') || '',
    pluginKey: localStorage.getItem('roboai_pkey') || '',
    messages: [],
    generating: false,
    msgCount: 0,
    codeCount: 0,
    files: [],
    currentFile: null,

    init: function() {
        if (!this.pluginKey) {
            this.pluginKey = 'rk_' + Date.now() + '_' + Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 10);
            localStorage.setItem('roboai_pkey', this.pluginKey);
        }
        this.cacheDom();
        this.bindEvents();
        this.loadKey();
        this.showPluginKey();
        this.consolePrint('System gotowy', 'info');
        this.consolePrint('Polacz sie z AI aby zaczac', 'info');
    },

    cacheDom: function() {
        this.dom = {
            sidebar: document.getElementById('panelLeft'),
            menuBtn: document.getElementById('menuBtn'),
            statusDot: document.getElementById('statusDot'),
            statusText: document.getElementById('statusText'),
            apiKeyInput: document.getElementById('apiKeyInput'),
            toggleKey: document.getElementById('toggleKey'),
            connectBtn: document.getElementById('connectBtn'),
            pluginKeyDisplay: document.getElementById('pluginKeyDisplay'),
            copyPluginKey: document.getElementById('copyPluginKey'),
            fileTree: document.getElementById('fileTree'),
            refreshExplorer: document.getElementById('refreshExplorer'),
            consoleOutput: document.getElementById('consoleOutput'),
            clearConsole: document.getElementById('clearConsole'),
            chat: document.getElementById('chat'),
            welcome: document.getElementById('welcome'),
            messages: document.getElementById('messages'),
            typing: document.getElementById('typing'),
            typingLabel: document.getElementById('typingLabel'),
            msgInput: document.getElementById('msgInput'),
            sendBtn: document.getElementById('sendBtn'),
            autoInsert: document.getElementById('autoInsert'),
            modelSelect: document.getElementById('modelSelect'),
            msgCount: document.getElementById('msgCount'),
            codeCount: document.getElementById('codeCount'),
            clearBtn: document.getElementById('clearBtn'),
            exportBtn: document.getElementById('exportBtn'),
            notifs: document.getElementById('notifs'),
            tabChat: document.getElementById('tabChat'),
            tabEditor: document.getElementById('tabEditor'),
            viewChat: document.getElementById('viewChat'),
            viewEditor: document.getElementById('viewEditor'),
            editorFileName: document.getElementById('editorFileName'),
            editorName: document.getElementById('editorName'),
            editorType: document.getElementById('editorType'),
            editorParent: document.getElementById('editorParent'),
            editorCode: document.getElementById('editorCode'),
            editorSave: document.getElementById('editorSave'),
            editorDelete: document.getElementById('editorDelete')
        };
    },

    bindEvents: function() {
        var self = this;

        this.dom.menuBtn.addEventListener('click', function() {
            self.dom.sidebar.classList.toggle('open');
        });

        document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
            if (window.innerWidth <= 768 && !self.dom.sidebar.contains(e.target) && !self.dom.menuBtn.contains(e.target)) {
                self.dom.sidebar.classList.remove('open');
            }
        });

        this.dom.toggleKey.addEventListener('click', function() {
            var inp = self.dom.apiKeyInput;
            var ico = self.dom.toggleKey.querySelector('i');
            if (inp.type === 'password') { inp.type = 'text'; ico.className = 'fas fa-eye-slash'; }
            else { inp.type = 'password'; ico.className = 'fas fa-eye'; }
        });

        this.dom.connectBtn.addEventListener('click', function() { self.connect(); });

        this.dom.copyPluginKey.addEventListener('click', function() {
            navigator.clipboard.writeText(self.pluginKey);
            self.notify('Klucz skopiowany!', 'success');
        });

        this.dom.sendBtn.addEventListener('click', function() { self.send(); });
        this.dom.msgInput.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
            if (e.key === 'Enter' && !e.shiftKey) { e.preventDefault(); self.send(); }
        });
        this.dom.msgInput.addEventListener('input', function() {
            self.dom.sendBtn.disabled = !self.dom.msgInput.value.trim() || self.generating;
            self.autoResize();
        });

        document.querySelectorAll('.action-card, .chip').forEach(function(btn) {
            btn.addEventListener('click', function() {
                var p = btn.dataset.prompt;
                if (p) { self.dom.msgInput.value = p; self.dom.sendBtn.disabled = false; self.send(); }
            });
        });

        this.dom.clearBtn.addEventListener('click', function() { self.clearChat(); });
        this.dom.exportBtn.addEventListener('click', function() { self.exportChat(); });
        this.dom.clearConsole.addEventListener('click', function() {
            self.dom.consoleOutput.innerHTML = '';
            self.consolePrint('Konsola wyczyszczona', 'info');
        });

        // Tabs
        this.dom.tabChat.addEventListener('click', function() { self.switchTab('chat'); });
        this.dom.tabEditor.addEventListener('click', function() { self.switchTab('editor'); });

        // Editor
        this.dom.editorSave.addEventListener('click', function() { self.saveFromEditor(); });
        this.dom.editorDelete.addEventListener('click', function() { self.deleteFromEditor(); });
        this.dom.refreshExplorer.addEventListener('click', function() { self.renderFileTree(); });

        // Tab key in editor
        this.dom.editorCode.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
            if (e.key === 'Tab') {
                e.preventDefault();
                var start = this.selectionStart;
                var end = this.selectionEnd;
                this.value = this.value.substring(0, start) + '    ' + this.value.substring(end);
                this.selectionStart = this.selectionEnd = start + 4;
            }
        });
    },

    // === TABS ===
    switchTab: function(tab) {
        this.dom.tabChat.className = 'tab' + (tab === 'chat' ? ' active' : '');
        this.dom.tabEditor.className = 'tab' + (tab === 'editor' ? ' active' : '');
        this.dom.viewChat.className = 'view-container' + (tab === 'chat' ? '' : ' hidden');
        this.dom.viewEditor.className = 'view-container' + (tab === 'editor' ? '' : ' hidden');
    },

    // === CONSOLE ===
    consolePrint: function(msg, type) {
        type = type || 'info';
        var time = new Date().toLocaleTimeString('pl-PL', { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit', second: '2-digit' });
        var div = document.createElement('div');
        div.className = 'console-line ' + type;
        div.innerHTML = '<span class="console-time">' + time + '</span> ' + msg;
        this.dom.consoleOutput.appendChild(div);
        this.dom.consoleOutput.scrollTop = this.dom.consoleOutput.scrollHeight;
    },

    // === CONNECTION ===
    loadKey: function() {
        if (this.apiKey) this.dom.apiKeyInput.value = this.apiKey;
    },

    showPluginKey: function() {
        this.dom.pluginKeyDisplay.textContent = this.pluginKey;
    },

    connect: function() {
        var self = this;
        var key = this.dom.apiKeyInput.value.trim();
        if (!key) return this.notify('Wpisz klucz API Groq!', 'error');

        this.apiKey = key;
        localStorage.setItem('roboai_key', key);
        this.setStatus('connecting', 'Laczenie...');
        this.consolePrint('Laczenie z Groq AI...', 'action');

        fetch('/.netlify/functions/chat', {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
            body: JSON.stringify({ apiKey: key, testMode: true })
        })
        .then(function(res) { return res.json().then(function(d) { return { ok: res.ok, data: d }; }); })
        .then(function(r) {
            if (r.ok && r.data.success) {
                self.setStatus('online', 'Polaczono');
                self.notify('Polaczono z AI!', 'success');
                self.consolePrint('Polaczono z Groq AI', 'success');
            } else {
                throw new Error(r.data.error || 'Blad');
            }
        })
        .catch(function(err) {
            self.setStatus('offline', 'Blad');
            self.notify(err.message, 'error');
            self.consolePrint('Blad: ' + err.message, 'error');
        });
    },

    setStatus: function(state, text) {
        this.dom.statusDot.className = 'status-dot ' + state;
        this.dom.statusText.textContent = text;
    },

    // === SEND ===
    send: function() {
        var self = this;
        var text = this.dom.msgInput.value.trim();
        if (!text || this.generating) return;
        if (!this.apiKey) return this.notify('Najpierw polacz sie z AI!', 'warn');

        this.dom.welcome.style.display = 'none';
        this.addMsg('user', text);
        this.dom.msgInput.value = '';
        this.dom.sendBtn.disabled = true;
        this.autoResize();

        this.generating = true;
        this.dom.typing.classList.add('active');
        this.dom.typingLabel.textContent = 'AI planuje...';
        this.scrollDown();
        this.consolePrint('Wysylanie zapytania do AI...', 'action');

        // Build context with existing files
        var fileContext = '';
        if (this.files.length > 0) {
            fileContext = '\n\nAKTUALNE PLIKI W PROJEKCIE:\n';
            for (var i = 0; i < this.files.length; i++) {
                var f = this.files[i];
                fileContext += '- ' + f.name + ' (' + f.type + ' w ' + f.parent + ') - ' + f.code.split('\n').length + ' linii\n';
            }
            fileContext += '\nJesli uzytkownik chce ZMIENIC istniejacy plik, uzyj akcji "update" z ta sama nazwa.\n';
            fileContext += 'Jesli chce USUNAC plik, uzyj akcji "delete".\n';
        }

        var sysPrompt = this.getSystemPrompt() + fileContext;
        var apiMsgs = [{ role: 'system', content: sysPrompt }];
        for (var j = 0; j < this.messages.length; j++) {
            apiMsgs.push({ role: this.messages[j].role, content: this.messages[j].text });
        }

        setTimeout(function() {
            self.dom.typingLabel.textContent = 'AI generuje kod...';
        }, 1500);

        fetch('/.netlify/functions/chat', {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
            body: JSON.stringify({
                apiKey: this.apiKey,
                messages: apiMsgs,
                model: this.dom.modelSelect.value
            })
        })
        .then(function(res) {
            if (!res.ok) return res.json().then(function(d) { throw new Error(d.error || 'Blad API'); });
            return res.json();
        })
        .then(function(data) {
            self.dom.typingLabel.textContent = 'Przetwarzanie...';
            self.addMsg('bot', data.content);
            self.consolePrint('Odpowiedz otrzymana', 'success');

            if (self.dom.autoInsert.checked) {
                var blocks = self.extractCode(data.content);
                if (blocks.length > 0) {
                    self.consolePrint('Znaleziono ' + blocks.length + ' blokow kodu', 'action');
                    self.processBlocks(blocks);
                }
            }
        })
        .catch(function(err) {
            self.addMsg('bot', 'Blad: ' + err.message);
            self.notify(err.message, 'error');
            self.consolePrint('Blad: ' + err.message, 'error');
        })
        .finally(function() {
            self.generating = false;
            self.dom.typing.classList.remove('active');
            self.dom.sendBtn.disabled = !self.dom.msgInput.value.trim();
        });
    },

    getSystemPrompt: function() {
        return 'Jestes profesjonalnym developerem Roblox Studio i Luau. Tworzysz kompletne, dzialajace systemy.\n\n' +
        'FORMAT KODU - KRYTYCZNIE WAZNE:\n' +
        'Kazdy blok kodu MUSI miec na PIERWSZEJ LINII konfiguracje w DOKLADNIE takim formacie:\n' +
        '-- @NAME: NazwaPliku | @TYPE: TypSkryptu | @PARENT: Lokalizacja | @ACTION: create\n\n' +
        'Dozwolone @TYPE: LocalScript, Script, ModuleScript\n' +
        'Dozwolone @PARENT: StarterGui, ServerScriptService, ReplicatedStorage, StarterPlayerScripts, ServerStorage\n' +
        'Dozwolone @ACTION: create (nowy plik), update (zmien istniejacy), delete (usun plik)\n\n' +
        'PRZYKLAD:\n' +
        '```lua\n' +
        '-- @NAME: MainMenuGUI | @TYPE: LocalScript | @PARENT: StarterGui | @ACTION: create\n' +
        'local Players = game:GetService("Players")\n' +
        '-- kod...\n' +
        '```\n\n' +
        'ZASADY PLANOWANIA:\n' +
        '1. ZAWSZE zacznij odpowiedz od PLANU - opisz jakie pliki stworzysz/zmienisz i dlaczego\n' +
        '2. Uzyj formatowania: **Plan:** nastepnie lista krokow\n' +
        '3. Opisz architekture i zaleznosci miedzy plikami\n' +
        '4. Kazdy plik nazywaj opisowo: MainMenuGUI, CombatSystem, ItemDatabase\n\n' +
        'ZASADY KODU:\n' +
        '1. Pisz WYLACZNIE w Luau\n' +
        '2. Kod musi dzialac natychmiast\n' +
        '3. GUI twórz z Instance.new() - ScreenGui, Frame, TextButton, UICorner, UIGradient, UIListLayout itd.\n' +
        '4. ZAWSZE dodawaj animacje TweenService\n' +
        '5. Uzywaj ladnych kolorow, gradientow, zaokraglen\n' +
        '6. Pisz DLUGI, SZCZEGOLOWY kod - minimum 100 linii na skrypt GUI\n' +
        '7. Dodawaj komentarze po polsku\n' +
        '8. Unikaj magic numbers - zmienne config na gorze\n' +
        '9. Obsluguj bledy z pcall\n' +
        '10. Mozesz generowac WIELE plikow w jednej odpowiedzi\n\n' +
        'JESLI UZYTKOWNIK CHCE ZMIENIC ISTNIEJACY PLIK:\n' +
        '- Uzyj @ACTION: update i tej samej @NAME\n' +
        '- Wygeneruj CALY nowy kod pliku (nie fragmenty)\n\n' +
        'JESLI UZYTKOWNIK CHCE USUNAC PLIK:\n' +
        '- Uzyj @ACTION: delete i @NAME pliku do usuniecia\n' +
        '- Kod moze byc pusty lub komentarz\n\n' +
        'Odpowiadaj po polsku. Badz profesjonalny i szczegolowy.';
    },

    // === PROCESS BLOCKS ===
    processBlocks: function(blocks) {
        var self = this;
        var tasks = [];

        for (var i = 0; i < blocks.length; i++) {
            var code = blocks[i].code;
            var info = this.parseScriptInfo(code);

            if (info.action === 'delete') {
                this.consolePrint('Usuwanie: ' + info.name, 'warn');
                this.removeFile(info.name);
                tasks.push({
                    id: 'task_' + Date.now() + '_' + i,
                    code: '',
                    scriptName: info.name,
                    scriptType: info.type,
                    parent: info.parent,
                    action: 'delete',
                    order: i + 1,
                    total: blocks.length,
                    timestamp: Date.now()
                });
            } else if (info.action === 'update') {
                this.consolePrint('Aktualizacja: ' + info.name, 'action');
                this.updateFile(info.name, code, info.type, info.parent);
                tasks.push({
                    id: 'task_' + Date.now() + '_' + i,
                    code: code,
                    scriptName: info.name,
                    scriptType: info.type,
                    parent: info.parent,
                    action: 'update',
                    order: i + 1,
                    total: blocks.length,
                    timestamp: Date.now()
                });
            } else {
                this.consolePrint('Tworzenie: ' + info.name + ' (' + info.type + ' w ' + info.parent + ')', 'success');
                this.addFile(info.name, code, info.type, info.parent);
                tasks.push({
                    id: 'task_' + Date.now() + '_' + i,
                    code: code,
                    scriptName: info.name,
                    scriptType: info.type,
                    parent: info.parent,
                    action: 'create',
                    order: i + 1,
                    total: blocks.length,
                    timestamp: Date.now()
                });
            }
        }

        // Send all tasks to plugin
        if (tasks.length > 0) {
            this.sendTasksToPlugin(tasks);
        }

        this.renderFileTree();
    },

    parseScriptInfo: function(code) {
        var name = 'GeneratedScript';
        var type = 'LocalScript';
        var parent = 'StarterGui';
        var action = 'create';

        var nm = code.match(/@NAME:\s*([^|@\n]+)/i);
        if (nm) name = nm[1].trim();

        var tp = code.match(/@TYPE:\s*(\w+)/i);
        if (tp) type = tp[1].trim();

        var pr = code.match(/@PARENT:\s*(\w+)/i);
        if (pr) parent = pr[1].trim();

        var ac = code.match(/@ACTION:\s*(\w+)/i);
        if (ac) action = ac[1].trim().toLowerCase();

        // Fallback
        if (!nm) {
            var ot = code.match(/SCRIPT_TYPE:\s*(\w+)/i);
            var op = code.match(/PARENT:\s*(\w+)/i);
            if (ot) type = ot[1];
            if (op) parent = op[1];
        }

        return { name: name, type: type, parent: parent, action: action };
    },

    extractCode: function(text) {
        var blocks = [];
        var re = /```(\w+)?\n([\s\S]*?)```/g;
        var m;
        while ((m = re.exec(text)) !== null) {
            blocks.push({ lang: m[1] || 'lua', code: m[2].trim() });
        }
        return blocks;
    },

    // === FILE MANAGEMENT ===
    addFile: function(name, code, type, parent) {
        // Remove existing with same name
        this.files = this.files.filter(function(f) { return f.name !== name; });
        this.files.push({ name: name, code: code, type: type, parent: parent });
    },

    updateFile: function(name, code, type, parent) {
        var found = false;
        for (var i = 0; i < this.files.length; i++) {
            if (this.files[i].name === name) {
                this.files[i].code = code;
                this.files[i].type = type || this.files[i].type;
                this.files[i].parent = parent || this.files[i].parent;
                found = true;
                break;
            }
        }
        if (!found) this.addFile(name, code, type, parent);
    },

    removeFile: function(name) {
        this.files = this.files.filter(function(f) { return f.name !== name; });
        if (this.currentFile && this.currentFile.name === name) {
            this.currentFile = null;
            this.dom.editorFileName.textContent = 'Plik usuniety';
            this.dom.editorCode.value = '';
        }
    },

    renderFileTree: function() {
        var self = this;
        if (this.files.length === 0) {
            this.dom.fileTree.innerHTML = '<div class="tree-empty"><i class="fas fa-inbox"></i><p>Brak skryptow</p><p class="hint">Wyslij polecenie do AI</p></div>';
            return;
        }

        // Group by parent
        var groups = {};
        for (var i = 0; i < this.files.length; i++) {
            var f = this.files[i];
            if (!groups[f.parent]) groups[f.parent] = [];
            groups[f.parent].push(f);
        }

        var html = '';
        var parentIcons = {
            StarterGui: 'fa-display',
            ServerScriptService: 'fa-server',
            ReplicatedStorage: 'fa-database',
            StarterPlayerScripts: 'fa-user',
            ServerStorage: 'fa-box'
        };

        var typeIcons = {
            LocalScript: 'file-icon-local',
            Script: 'file-icon-server',
            ModuleScript: 'file-icon-module',
            ScreenGui: 'file-icon-gui'
        };

        for (var parentName in groups) {
            var icon = parentIcons[parentName] || 'fa-folder';
            html += '<div class="tree-folder">';
            html += '<div class="tree-folder-name"><i class="fas ' + icon + '"></i> ' + parentName + '</div>';
            var items = groups[parentName];
            for (var j = 0; j < items.length; j++) {
                var file = items[j];
                var fIcon = typeIcons[file.type] || 'file-icon-local';
                var isActive = self.currentFile && self.currentFile.name === file.name ? ' active' : '';
                html += '<div class="tree-file' + isActive + '" data-file="' + file.name + '">';
                html += '<i class="fas fa-file-code ' + fIcon + '"></i> ' + file.name;
                html += '</div>';
            }
            html += '</div>';
        }

        this.dom.fileTree.innerHTML = html;

        // Bind click events
        this.dom.fileTree.querySelectorAll('.tree-file').forEach(function(el) {
            el.addEventListener('click', function() {
                var fileName = el.dataset.file;
                self.openFileInEditor(fileName);
            });
        });
    },

    openFileInEditor: function(name) {
        var file = null;
        for (var i = 0; i < this.files.length; i++) {
            if (this.files[i].name === name) { file = this.files[i]; break; }
        }
        if (!file) return;

        this.currentFile = file;
        this.dom.editorFileName.textContent = file.name;
        this.dom.editorName.value = file.name;
        this.dom.editorType.value = file.type;
        this.dom.editorParent.value = file.parent;
        this.dom.editorCode.value = file.code;
        this.switchTab('editor');
        this.renderFileTree();
        this.consolePrint('Otwarty: ' + file.name, 'info');
    },

    // === EDITOR ACTIONS ===
    saveFromEditor: function() {
        var name = this.dom.editorName.value.trim();
        var type = this.dom.editorType.value;
        var parent = this.dom.editorParent.value;
        var code = this.dom.editorCode.value;

        if (!name) return this.notify('Wpisz nazwe pliku!', 'warn');
        if (!code.trim()) return this.notify('Kod jest pusty!', 'warn');

        this.updateFile(name, code, type, parent);
        this.renderFileTree();

        // Send to plugin as update
        this.sendTasksToPlugin([{
            id: 'task_' + Date.now(),
            code: code,
            scriptName: name,
            scriptType: type,
            parent: parent,
            action: this.currentFile ? 'update' : 'create',
            order: 1,
            total: 1,
            timestamp: Date.now()
        }]);

        this.consolePrint('Zapisano i wyslano: ' + name, 'success');
        this.notify(name + ' zapisano i wyslano!', 'success');
    },

    deleteFromEditor: function() {
        if (!this.currentFile) return;
        var name = this.currentFile.name;

        this.sendTasksToPlugin([{
            id: 'task_' + Date.now(),
            code: '',
            scriptName: name,
            scriptType: this.currentFile.type,
            parent: this.currentFile.parent,
            action: 'delete',
            order: 1,
            total: 1,
            timestamp: Date.now()
        }]);

        this.removeFile(name);
        this.renderFileTree();
        this.dom.editorFileName.textContent = 'Wybierz plik';
        this.dom.editorCode.value = '';
        this.dom.editorName.value = '';
        this.currentFile = null;

        this.consolePrint('Usuniety: ' + name, 'warn');
        this.notify(name + ' usuniety!', 'info');
    },

    // === PLUGIN COMMUNICATION ===
    sendTasksToPlugin: function(tasks) {
        var self = this;

        fetch('/.netlify/functions/chat', {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
            body: JSON.stringify({
                action: 'addTasks',
                pluginKey: this.pluginKey,
                tasks: tasks
            })
        })
        .then(function(res) { return res.json(); })
        .then(function(data) {
            if (data.success) {
                self.consolePrint(tasks.length + ' operacji wyslanych do Studio', 'success');
            } else {
                self.consolePrint('Blad Redis: ' + (data.error || ''), 'error');
            }
        })
        .catch(function(e) {
            self.consolePrint('Blad sieci: ' + e.message, 'error');
        });
    },

    // === MESSAGES ===
    addMsg: function(role, text) {
        this.messages.push({ role: role === 'bot' ? 'assistant' : role, text: text });
        this.msgCount++;
        this.dom.msgCount.textContent = this.msgCount;

        var time = new Date().toLocaleTimeString('pl-PL', { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit' });
        var div = document.createElement('div');
        div.className = 'msg ' + role;

        var icon = role === 'bot' ? 'fa-robot' : 'fa-user';
        var content = role === 'bot' ? this.renderContent(text) : this.esc(text);

        div.innerHTML = '<div class="msg-avatar"><i class="fas ' + icon + '"></i></div>' +
            '<div class="msg-body"><div class="msg-bubble">' + content + '</div>' +
            '<div class="msg-time">' + time + '</div></div>';

        this.dom.messages.appendChild(div);
        this.scrollDown();
    },

    renderContent: function(text) {
        var self = this;
        var html = text;

        html = html.replace(/```(\w+)?\n([\s\S]*?)```/g, function(_, lang, code) {
            self.codeCount++;
            self.dom.codeCount.textContent = self.codeCount;
            var id = 'c' + Date.now() + Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 7);
            var info = self.parseScriptInfo(code);

            var actionLabel = '';
            if (info.action === 'update') actionLabel = ' <span style="color:#f59e0b">UPDATE</span>';
            else if (info.action === 'delete') actionLabel = ' <span style="color:#ef4444">DELETE</span>';

            return '<div class="code-wrap" id="' + id + '">' +
                '<div class="code-top">' +
                '<span class="code-lang"><i class="fas fa-file-code"></i> ' + info.name + actionLabel + ' <span class="code-meta">' + info.type + ' → ' + info.parent + '</span></span>' +
                '<div class="code-btns">' +
                '<button class="code-btn edit-btn" onclick="App.editCodeBlock(\'' + id + '\')"><i class="fas fa-pen"></i> Edytuj</button>' +
                '<button class="code-btn" onclick="App.copyCode(\'' + id + '\')"><i class="fas fa-copy"></i></button>' +
                '<button class="code-btn run" id="btn_' + id + '" onclick="App.runCode(\'' + id + '\')"><i class="fas fa-play"></i> Wstaw</button>' +
                '</div></div>' +
                '<pre><code>' + self.esc(code.trim()) + '</code></pre></div>';
        });

        html = html.replace(/`([^`]+)`/g, '<code>$1</code>');
        html = html.replace(/\*\*(.*?)\*\*/g, '<strong>$1</strong>');
        html = html.replace(/\n/g, '<br>');
        return html;
    },

    editCodeBlock: function(id) {
        var el = document.getElementById(id);
        if (!el) return;
        var code = el.querySelector('code').textContent;
        var info = this.parseScriptInfo(code);

        this.addFile(info.name, code, info.type, info.parent);
        this.openFileInEditor(info.name);
    },

    esc: function(t) {
        var d = document.createElement('div');
        d.textContent = t;
        return d.innerHTML;
    },

    copyCode: function(id) {
        var el = document.getElementById(id);
        if (!el) return;
        navigator.clipboard.writeText(el.querySelector('code').textContent);
        this.notify('Skopiowano!', 'success');
    },

    runCode: function(id) {
        var el = document.getElementById(id);
        if (!el) return;
        var code = el.querySelector('code').textContent;
        var info = this.parseScriptInfo(code);

        this.addFile(info.name, code, info.type, info.parent);
        this.renderFileTree();

        this.sendTasksToPlugin([{
            id: 'task_' + Date.now(),
            code: code,
            scriptName: info.name,
            scriptType: info.type,
            parent: info.parent,
            action: info.action,
            order: 1,
            total: 1,
            timestamp: Date.now()
        }]);

        var btn = document.getElementById('btn_' + id);
        if (btn) { btn.className = 'code-btn sent'; btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-check"></i> OK'; }
    },

    // === HELPERS ===
    autoResize: function() {
        var ta = this.dom.msgInput;
        ta.style.height = 'auto';
        ta.style.height = Math.min(ta.scrollHeight, 120) + 'px';
    },

    scrollDown: function() {
        var chat = this.dom.chat;
        requestAnimationFrame(function() { chat.scrollTop = chat.scrollHeight; });
    },

    clearChat: function() {
        this.messages = [];
        this.msgCount = 0;
        this.codeCount = 0;
        this.files = [];
        this.currentFile = null;
        this.dom.msgCount.textContent = '0';
        this.dom.codeCount.textContent = '0';
        this.dom.messages.innerHTML = '';
        this.dom.welcome.style.display = '';
        this.renderFileTree();
        this.consolePrint('Czat i pliki wyczyszczone', 'info');
        this.notify('Wyczyszczono', 'info');
    },

    exportChat: function() {
        if (!this.messages.length) return this.notify('Brak wiadomosci', 'warn');
        var t = '=== RoboAI Export ===\n\n';
        for (var i = 0; i < this.messages.length; i++) {
            var m = this.messages[i];
            t += (m.role === 'user' ? 'Ty' : 'AI') + ':\n' + m.text + '\n\n---\n\n';
        }
        var a = document.createElement('a');
        a.href = URL.createObjectURL(new Blob([t]));
        a.download = 'roboai-' + Date.now() + '.txt';
        a.click();
    },

    notify: function(msg, type) {
        type = type || 'info';
        var icons = { success: 'fa-check-circle', error: 'fa-times-circle', warn: 'fa-exclamation-triangle', info: 'fa-info-circle' };
        var n = document.createElement('div');
        n.className = 'notif ' + type;
        n.innerHTML = '<i class="fas ' + icons[type] + ' notif-icon"></i><span class="notif-text">' + msg + '</span><button class="notif-close" onclick="this.parentElement.remove()"><i class="fas fa-times"></i></button>';
        this.dom.notifs.appendChild(n);
        setTimeout(function() { if (n.parentElement) n.remove(); }, 4000);
    }
};

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() { App.init(); });

Lua

local SERVER = "https://fleetyai.netlify.app"
local PLUGIN_KEY = "rk_fb008f90a40e4eb2b5c2dd5eb0d92fec"
local DELAY = 2

local Http = game:GetService("HttpService")
local Sel = game:GetService("Selection")
local CHS = game:GetService("ChangeHistoryService")

local bar = plugin:CreateToolbar("RoboAI")
local mainBtn = bar:CreateButton("RoboAI", "AI Assistant", "rbxassetid://4458901886")
local wInfo = DockWidgetPluginGuiInfo.new(Enum.InitialDockState.Right, false, false, 300, 450, 260, 300)
local w = plugin:CreateDockWidgetPluginGui("RoboAI_v5", wInfo)
w.Title = "RoboAI Studio"

local function make(c, p)
    local i = Instance.new(c)
    for k,v in pairs(p) do if k ~= "Parent" then i[k] = v end end
    if p.Parent then i.Parent = p.Parent end
    return i
end

local bg = make("Frame", {Size=UDim2.new(1,0,1,0), BackgroundColor3=Color3.fromRGB(8,12,24), BorderSizePixel=0, Parent=w})
make("UIListLayout", {Padding=UDim.new(0,4), SortOrder=Enum.SortOrder.LayoutOrder, Parent=bg})
make("UIPadding", {PaddingLeft=UDim.new(0,8), PaddingRight=UDim.new(0,8), PaddingTop=UDim.new(0,8), PaddingBottom=UDim.new(0,8), Parent=bg})

make("TextLabel", {Size=UDim2.new(1,0,0,24), BackgroundTransparency=1, Text="🤖 RoboAI Studio v5", TextColor3=Color3.fromRGB(96,165,250), Font=Enum.Font.GothamBold, TextSize=14, TextXAlignment=Enum.TextXAlignment.Left, LayoutOrder=1, Parent=bg})

local sBar = make("Frame", {Size=UDim2.new(1,0,0,24), BackgroundColor3=Color3.fromRGB(14,20,38), BorderSizePixel=0, LayoutOrder=2, Parent=bg})
make("UICorner", {CornerRadius=UDim.new(0,5), Parent=sBar})
local sDot = make("Frame", {Size=UDim2.new(0,7,0,7), Position=UDim2.new(0,8,0.5,-3), BackgroundColor3=Color3.fromRGB(239,68,68), BorderSizePixel=0, Parent=sBar})
make("UICorner", {CornerRadius=UDim.new(1,0), Parent=sDot})
local sTxt = make("TextLabel", {Size=UDim2.new(1,-22,1,0), Position=UDim2.new(0,20,0,0), BackgroundTransparency=1, Text="Oczekuje", TextColor3=Color3.fromRGB(120,140,180), Font=Enum.Font.Gotham, TextSize=10, TextXAlignment=Enum.TextXAlignment.Left, Parent=sBar})

local statsLbl = make("TextLabel", {Size=UDim2.new(1,0,0,14), BackgroundTransparency=1, Text="0 operacji", TextColor3=Color3.fromRGB(60,80,120), Font=Enum.Font.RobotoMono, TextSize=9, TextXAlignment=Enum.TextXAlignment.Left, LayoutOrder=3, Parent=bg})

local logBox = make("ScrollingFrame", {
    Size=UDim2.new(1,0,1,-110), BackgroundColor3=Color3.fromRGB(5,8,16), BorderSizePixel=0,
    ScrollBarThickness=3, ScrollBarImageColor3=Color3.fromRGB(59,130,246),
    AutomaticCanvasSize=Enum.AutomaticSize.Y, CanvasSize=UDim2.new(0,0,0,0), LayoutOrder=4, Parent=bg
})
make("UICorner", {CornerRadius=UDim.new(0,5), Parent=logBox})
make("UIListLayout", {Padding=UDim.new(0,1), SortOrder=Enum.SortOrder.LayoutOrder, Parent=logBox})
make("UIPadding", {PaddingLeft=UDim.new(0,5), PaddingRight=UDim.new(0,5), PaddingTop=UDim.new(0,3), PaddingBottom=UDim.new(0,3), Parent=logBox})

local goBtn = make("TextButton", {Size=UDim2.new(1,0,0,32), BackgroundColor3=Color3.fromRGB(59,130,246), Text="▶ URUCHOM", TextColor3=Color3.fromRGB(255,255,255), Font=Enum.Font.GothamBold, TextSize=12, BorderSizePixel=0, LayoutOrder=5, Parent=bg})
make("UICorner", {CornerRadius=UDim.new(0,6), Parent=goBtn})

local active = false
local logN = 0
local totalOps = 0

local function log(msg, col)
    logN = logN + 1
    make("TextLabel", {
        Size=UDim2.new(1,0,0,0), AutomaticSize=Enum.AutomaticSize.Y, BackgroundTransparency=1,
        RichText=true, Text='<font color="#4a6090">['..os.date("%H:%M:%S")..']</font> '..msg,
        TextColor3=col or Color3.fromRGB(140,155,190), Font=Enum.Font.RobotoMono, TextSize=9,
        TextXAlignment=Enum.TextXAlignment.Left, TextWrapped=true, LayoutOrder=logN, Parent=logBox
    })
    task.defer(function() logBox.CanvasPosition = Vector2.new(0, logBox.AbsoluteCanvasSize.Y) end)
end

local function getParent(n)
    local m = {
        ServerScriptService = game:GetService("ServerScriptService"),
        ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"),
        ServerStorage = game:GetService("ServerStorage"),
        Workspace = workspace,
        StarterPlayerScripts = game:GetService("StarterPlayer"):FindFirstChild("StarterPlayerScripts"),
    }
    return m[n] or game:GetService("StarterGui")
end

local function findScript(name, parent)
    local p = getParent(parent)
    for _, child in ipairs(p:GetChildren()) do
        if child.Name == name and (child:IsA("BaseScript") or child:IsA("ModuleScript")) then
            return child
        end
    end
    return nil
end

local function executeTask(t, idx, total)
    local name = t.scriptName or "GeneratedScript"
    local stype = t.scriptType or "LocalScript"
    local parent = t.parent or "StarterGui"
    local action = t.action or "create"

    local prefix = ""
    if total > 1 then prefix = "[" .. idx .. "/" .. total .. "] " end

    if action == "delete" then
        log('<font color="#f59e0b">🗑 ' .. prefix .. 'Usuwanie: ' .. name .. '</font>')
        task.wait(0.3)
        local existing = findScript(name, parent)
        if existing then
            existing:Destroy()
            log('<font color="#10b981">✅ Usunieto: ' .. name .. '</font>')
        else
            log('<font color="#f59e0b">⚠ Nie znaleziono: ' .. name .. '</font>')
        end
        totalOps = totalOps + 1
        statsLbl.Text = totalOps .. " operacji"
        return
    end

    if action == "update" then
        log('<font color="#60a5fa">✏️ ' .. prefix .. 'Aktualizacja: ' .. name .. '</font>')
        task.wait(0.3)
        local existing = findScript(name, parent)
        if existing then
            existing.Source = t.code
            Sel:Set({existing})
            CHS:SetWaypoint("RoboAI: Updated " .. name)
            log('<font color="#10b981">✅ Zaktualizowano: ' .. name .. '</font>')
        else
            log('<font color="#f59e0b">⚠ Nie znaleziono, tworze nowy: ' .. name .. '</font>')
            action = "create"
        end
    end

    if action == "create" then
        log('<font color="#60a5fa">📝 ' .. prefix .. 'Tworzenie: ' .. name .. '</font>')
        task.wait(0.5)

        local ok, err = pcall(function()
            -- Remove old if exists
            local old = findScript(name, parent)
            if old then old:Destroy() end

            local inst
            if stype == "ModuleScript" then inst = Instance.new("ModuleScript")
            elseif stype == "Script" then inst = Instance.new("Script")
            else inst = Instance.new("LocalScript") end

            inst.Source = t.code
            inst.Name = name
            inst.Parent = getParent(parent)
            Sel:Set({inst})
            CHS:SetWaypoint("RoboAI: " .. name)
        end)

        if ok then
            log('<font color="#10b981">✅ ' .. name .. ' (' .. stype .. ') → ' .. parent .. '</font>')
        else
            log('<font color="#ef4444">❌ ' .. tostring(err) .. '</font>')
        end
    end

    totalOps = totalOps + 1
    statsLbl.Text = totalOps .. " operacji"
end

local function poll()
    local ok = pcall(function()
        local url = SERVER .. "/.netlify/functions/get-task?pluginKey=" .. PLUGIN_KEY
        local resp = Http:GetAsync(url, true)
        local data = Http:JSONDecode(resp)

        if data.tasks and #data.tasks > 0 then
            log('<font color="#60a5fa">📦 ' .. #data.tasks .. ' operacji</font>')
            table.sort(data.tasks, function(a,b) return (a.order or 0) < (b.order or 0) end)
            for i, t in ipairs(data.tasks) do
                executeTask(t, i, #data.tasks)
                if i < #data.tasks then task.wait(0.5) end
            end
            log('<font color="#10b981">✅ Gotowe!</font>')
        end
    end)

    if ok then
        sDot.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(16,185,129)
        sTxt.Text = "Polaczono"
        sTxt.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(16,185,129)
    else
        sDot.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(245,158,11)
        sTxt.Text = "Blad"
    end
end

local function start()
    if active then return end
    active = true
    goBtn.Text = "⏸ ZATRZYMAJ"
    goBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(239,68,68)
    log('<font color="#10b981">🚀 Start!</font>')
    task.spawn(function() while active do poll() task.wait(DELAY) end end)
end

local function stop()
    active = false
    goBtn.Text = "▶ URUCHOM"
    goBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(59,130,246)
    sDot.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(245,158,11)
    sTxt.Text = "Stop"
    sTxt.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(245,158,11)
    log('<font color="#f59e0b">⏸ Stop</font>')
end

goBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function() if active then stop() else start() end end)
mainBtn.Click:Connect(function() w.Enabled = not w.Enabled end)
log('<font color="#60a5fa">🤖 RoboAI v5 zaladowany</font>')

#msgInput::placeholder{color:var(--text3)}

Kontynuuję z script.js i pluginem - to jest za duże na jedną wiadomość. Wypchnij te 2 pliki (html + css) i napisz "gotowe" - dam ci resztę! 🚀

claude-opus-4-6
Rozumiem! Robimy profesjonalny system
Chcesz żeby AI:

✅ Sam decydował o nazwie pliku (np. "MainMenuGUI", "CombatSystem")
✅ Sam wybierał typ (Script/LocalScript/ModuleScript)
✅ Sam wybierał gdzie wstawić (StarterGui/ServerScriptService itd.)
✅ Planował kolejność skryptów
✅ Generował dłuższy, lepszy kod
✅ Plugin nazywał pliki normalnie
Krok 1: Zmień script.js
Otwórz script.js, usuń wszystko, wklej:

JavaScript

var App = {
    apiKey: localStorage.getItem('roboai_key') || '',
    pluginKey: localStorage.getItem('roboai_pkey') || '',
    messages: [],
    generating: false,
    msgCount: 0,
    codeCount: 0,
    sentTasks: [],

    init: function() {
        if (!this.pluginKey) {
            this.pluginKey = 'rk_' + Date.now() + '_' + Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 10);
            localStorage.setItem('roboai_pkey', this.pluginKey);
        }
        this.cacheDom();
        this.bindEvents();
        this.loadKey();
        this.showPluginKey();
    },

    cacheDom: function() {
        this.dom = {
            sidebar: document.getElementById('sidebar'),
            menuBtn: document.getElementById('menuBtn'),
            statusDot: document.getElementById('statusDot'),
            statusText: document.getElementById('statusText'),
            apiKeyInput: document.getElementById('apiKeyInput'),
            toggleKey: document.getElementById('toggleKey'),
            connectBtn: document.getElementById('connectBtn'),
            pluginKeyDisplay: document.getElementById('pluginKeyDisplay'),
            copyPluginKey: document.getElementById('copyPluginKey'),
            pluginDot: document.getElementById('pluginDot'),
            pluginStatusText: document.getElementById('pluginStatusText'),
            taskQueue: document.getElementById('taskQueue'),
            chat: document.getElementById('chat'),
            welcome: document.getElementById('welcome'),
            messages: document.getElementById('messages'),
            typing: document.getElementById('typing'),
            msgInput: document.getElementById('msgInput'),
            sendBtn: document.getElementById('sendBtn'),
            autoInsert: document.getElementById('autoInsert'),
            modelSelect: document.getElementById('modelSelect'),
            chatTitle: document.getElementById('chatTitle'),
            msgCount: document.getElementById('msgCount'),
            codeCount: document.getElementById('codeCount'),
            insertedCount: document.getElementById('insertedCount'),
            clearBtn: document.getElementById('clearBtn'),
            exportBtn: document.getElementById('exportBtn'),
            notifs: document.getElementById('notifs')
        };
    },

    bindEvents: function() {
        var self = this;

        this.dom.menuBtn.addEventListener('click', function() {
            self.dom.sidebar.classList.toggle('open');
        });

        document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
            if (window.innerWidth <= 768 && !self.dom.sidebar.contains(e.target) && !self.dom.menuBtn.contains(e.target)) {
                self.dom.sidebar.classList.remove('open');
            }
        });

        this.dom.toggleKey.addEventListener('click', function() {
            var inp = self.dom.apiKeyInput;
            var ico = self.dom.toggleKey.querySelector('i');
            if (inp.type === 'password') { inp.type = 'text'; ico.className = 'fas fa-eye-slash'; }
            else { inp.type = 'password'; ico.className = 'fas fa-eye'; }
        });

        this.dom.connectBtn.addEventListener('click', function() { self.connect(); });

        this.dom.copyPluginKey.addEventListener('click', function() {
            navigator.clipboard.writeText(self.pluginKey);
            self.notify('Klucz skopiowany!', 'success');
        });

        this.dom.sendBtn.addEventListener('click', function() { self.send(); });
        this.dom.msgInput.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
            if (e.key === 'Enter' && !e.shiftKey) { e.preventDefault(); self.send(); }
        });
        this.dom.msgInput.addEventListener('input', function() {
            self.dom.sendBtn.disabled = !self.dom.msgInput.value.trim() || self.generating;
            self.autoResize();
        });

        document.querySelectorAll('.action-btn, .chip').forEach(function(btn) {
            btn.addEventListener('click', function() {
                var p = btn.dataset.prompt;
                if (p) { self.dom.msgInput.value = p; self.dom.sendBtn.disabled = false; self.send(); }
            });
        });

        this.dom.clearBtn.addEventListener('click', function() { self.clearChat(); });
        this.dom.exportBtn.addEventListener('click', function() { self.exportChat(); });
    },

    loadKey: function() {
        if (this.apiKey) this.dom.apiKeyInput.value = this.apiKey;
    },

    showPluginKey: function() {
        this.dom.pluginKeyDisplay.textContent = this.pluginKey;
    },

    connect: function() {
        var self = this;
        var key = this.dom.apiKeyInput.value.trim();
        if (!key) return this.notify('Wpisz klucz API Groq!', 'error');

        this.apiKey = key;
        localStorage.setItem('roboai_key', key);
        this.setStatus('connecting', 'Laczenie...');

        fetch('/.netlify/functions/chat', {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
            body: JSON.stringify({ apiKey: key, testMode: true })
        })
        .then(function(res) { return res.json().then(function(d) { return { ok: res.ok, data: d }; }); })
        .then(function(r) {
            if (r.ok && r.data.success) {
                self.setStatus('online', 'Polaczono z AI');
                self.notify('Polaczono z AI!', 'success');
            } else {
                throw new Error(r.data.error || 'Blad polaczenia');
            }
        })
        .catch(function(err) {
            self.setStatus('offline', 'Blad polaczenia');
            self.notify(err.message, 'error');
        });
    },

    setStatus: function(state, text) {
        this.dom.statusDot.className = 'status-dot ' + state;
        this.dom.statusText.textContent = text;
    },

    send: function() {
        var self = this;
        var text = this.dom.msgInput.value.trim();
        if (!text || this.generating) return;
        if (!this.apiKey) return this.notify('Najpierw polacz sie z AI!', 'warn');

        this.dom.welcome.style.display = 'none';
        this.addMsg('user', text);
        this.dom.msgInput.value = '';
        this.dom.sendBtn.disabled = true;
        this.autoResize();

        if (this.messages.length === 1) {
            this.dom.chatTitle.textContent = text.length > 45 ? text.slice(0, 45) + '...' : text;
        }

        this.generating = true;
        this.dom.typing.classList.add('active');
        this.scrollDown();

        var sysPrompt = this.getSystemPrompt();
        var apiMsgs = [{ role: 'system', content: sysPrompt }];
        for (var i = 0; i < this.messages.length; i++) {
            apiMsgs.push({ role: this.messages[i].role, content: this.messages[i].text });
        }

        fetch('/.netlify/functions/chat', {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
            body: JSON.stringify({
                apiKey: this.apiKey,
                messages: apiMsgs,
                model: this.dom.modelSelect.value
            })
        })
        .then(function(res) {
            if (!res.ok) return res.json().then(function(d) { throw new Error(d.error || 'Blad API'); });
            return res.json();
        })
        .then(function(data) {
            self.addMsg('bot', data.content);

            if (self.dom.autoInsert.checked) {
                var blocks = self.extractCode(data.content);
                if (blocks.length > 0) {
                    self.notify('Planuje ' + blocks.length + ' skryptow...', 'info');
                    self.sendAllToPlugin(blocks);
                }
            }
        })
        .catch(function(err) {
            self.addMsg('bot', 'Blad: ' + err.message);
            self.notify(err.message, 'error');
        })
        .finally(function() {
            self.generating = false;
            self.dom.typing.classList.remove('active');
            self.dom.sendBtn.disabled = !self.dom.msgInput.value.trim();
        });
    },

    getSystemPrompt: function() {
        return 'Jestes ekspertem Roblox Studio i Luau. Tworzysz profesjonalne, kompletne systemy do gier.\n\n' +
        'KRYTYCZNE ZASADY FORMATU:\n' +
        'Kazdy blok kodu MUSI miec na PIERWSZEJ LINII specjalny komentarz konfiguracyjny w DOKLADNIE takim formacie:\n' +
        '-- @NAME: NazwaSkryptu | @TYPE: LocalScript | @PARENT: StarterGui\n\n' +
        'Dozwolone @TYPE: LocalScript, Script, ModuleScript\n' +
        'Dozwolone @PARENT: StarterGui, ServerScriptService, ReplicatedStorage, StarterPlayerScripts, ServerStorage\n\n' +
        'PRZYKLAD poprawnego bloku:\n' +
        '```lua\n' +
        '-- @NAME: MainMenuGUI | @TYPE: LocalScript | @PARENT: StarterGui\n' +
        'local Players = game:GetService("Players")\n' +
        '-- reszta kodu...\n' +
        '```\n\n' +
        'ZASADY PROGRAMOWANIA:\n' +
        '1. Pisz WYLACZNIE w Luau (Roblox Lua)\n' +
        '2. Kod musi dzialac natychmiast po wklejeniu\n' +
        '3. Dla GUI tworz pelne drzewa z Instance.new() - ScreenGui, Frame, TextButton, TextLabel, ImageLabel, UICorner, UIStroke, UIGradient, UIListLayout, UIPadding itp.\n' +
        '4. ZAWSZE dodawaj animacje TweenService - hover efekty, fade in/out, slide animacje\n' +
        '5. Uzywaj ladnych kolorow, gradientow, cieni i zaokraglen\n' +
        '6. Kazdy skrypt MUSI byc kompletny i niezalezny\n' +
        '7. Dodawaj szczegolowe komentarze po polsku\n' +
        '8. Generuj WIELE skryptow jesli to potrzebne (GUI + logika + dane + serwer)\n\n' +
        'ZASADY PLANOWANIA:\n' +
        '1. Przed kodem ZAWSZE napisz plan: jakie skrypty stworzysz, gdzie je umiescisc i dlaczego\n' +
        '2. Opisz architekture: co robi kazdy skrypt i jak wspolpracuja\n' +
        '3. Wymien zaleznosci miedzy skryptami\n' +
        '4. Kazdy skrypt nazywaj opisowo np: MainMenuGUI, CombatSystem, ItemDatabase, ShopHandler\n\n' +
        'ZASADY JAKOSCI:\n' +
        '1. Pisz profesjonalny, czytelny kod z wcienciami\n' +
        '2. Unikaj magic numbers - uzywaj zmiennych konfiguracyjnych na gorze skryptu\n' +
        '3. Obsluguj bledy (pcall gdzie potrzeba)\n' +
        '4. Dla GUI: tworz co najmniej 200+ linii kodu z pelnym UI\n' +
        '5. Odpowiadaj po polsku\n' +
        '6. Pisz DLUGE, SZCZEGOLOWE skrypty - nie skracaj!';
    },

    addMsg: function(role, text) {
        this.messages.push({ role: role === 'bot' ? 'assistant' : role, text: text });
        this.msgCount++;
        this.dom.msgCount.textContent = this.msgCount;

        var time = new Date().toLocaleTimeString('pl-PL', { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit' });
        var div = document.createElement('div');
        div.className = 'msg ' + role;

        var icon = role === 'bot' ? 'fa-robot' : 'fa-user';
        var content = role === 'bot' ? this.renderContent(text) : this.esc(text);

        div.innerHTML = '<div class="msg-avatar"><i class="fas ' + icon + '"></i></div>' +
            '<div class="msg-body"><div class="msg-bubble">' + content + '</div>' +
            '<div class="msg-time">' + time + '</div></div>';

        this.dom.messages.appendChild(div);
        this.scrollDown();
    },

    renderContent: function(text) {
        var self = this;
        var html = text;

        html = html.replace(/```(\w+)?\n([\s\S]*?)```/g, function(_, lang, code) {
            self.codeCount++;
            self.dom.codeCount.textContent = self.codeCount;
            var id = 'c' + Date.now() + Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 7);

            // Parse the config comment
            var info = self.parseScriptInfo(code);

            return '<div class="code-wrap" id="' + id + '">' +
                '<div class="code-top">' +
                '<span class="code-lang"><i class="fas fa-file-code"></i> ' + info.name + ' <span class="code-meta">' + info.type + ' → ' + info.parent + '</span></span>' +
                '<div class="code-btns">' +
                '<button class="code-btn" onclick="App.copyCode(\'' + id + '\')"><i class="fas fa-copy"></i> Kopiuj</button>' +
                '<button class="code-btn run" id="btn_' + id + '" onclick="App.runCode(\'' + id + '\')"><i class="fas fa-play"></i> Wstaw</button>' +
                '</div></div>' +
                '<pre><code>' + self.esc(code.trim()) + '</code></pre></div>';
        });

        html = html.replace(/`([^`]+)`/g, '<code>$1</code>');
        html = html.replace(/\*\*(.*?)\*\*/g, '<strong>$1</strong>');
        html = html.replace(/\n/g, '<br>');
        return html;
    },

    parseScriptInfo: function(code) {
        var name = 'Script';
        var type = 'LocalScript';
        var parent = 'StarterGui';

        // Try new format: -- @NAME: xxx | @TYPE: xxx | @PARENT: xxx
        var configMatch = code.match(/--\s*@NAME:\s*([^|]+)/i);
        if (configMatch) name = configMatch[1].trim();

        var typeMatch = code.match(/@TYPE:\s*(\w+)/i);
        if (typeMatch) type = typeMatch[1].trim();

        var parentMatch = code.match(/@PARENT:\s*(\w+)/i);
        if (parentMatch) parent = parentMatch[1].trim();

        // Fallback to old format
        if (!configMatch) {
            var oldType = code.match(/--\s*SCRIPT_TYPE:\s*(\w+)/i);
            var oldParent = code.match(/--\s*PARENT:\s*(\w+)/i);
            if (oldType) type = oldType[1];
            if (oldParent) parent = oldParent[1];
        }

        return { name: name, type: type, parent: parent };
    },

    esc: function(t) {
        var d = document.createElement('div');
        d.textContent = t;
        return d.innerHTML;
    },

    copyCode: function(id) {
        var el = document.getElementById(id);
        if (!el) return;
        var code = el.querySelector('code').textContent;
        navigator.clipboard.writeText(code);
        this.notify('Kod skopiowany!', 'success');
    },

    runCode: function(id) {
        var el = document.getElementById(id);
        if (!el) return;
        var code = el.querySelector('code').textContent;
        this.sendOneToPlugin(code, id);
    },

    extractCode: function(text) {
        var blocks = [];
        var re = /```(\w+)?\n([\s\S]*?)```/g;
        var m;
        while ((m = re.exec(text)) !== null) {
            blocks.push({ lang: m[1] || 'lua', code: m[2].trim() });
        }
        return blocks;
    },

    sendAllToPlugin: function(blocks) {
        var self = this;
        var tasks = [];

        for (var i = 0; i < blocks.length; i++) {
            var code = blocks[i].code;
            var info = this.parseScriptInfo(code);

            tasks.push({
                id: 'task_' + Date.now() + '_' + i,
                code: code,
                scriptName: info.name,
                scriptType: info.type,
                parent: info.parent,
                order: i + 1,
                total: blocks.length,
                timestamp: Date.now()
            });
        }

        fetch('/.netlify/functions/chat', {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
            body: JSON.stringify({
                action: 'addTasks',
                pluginKey: this.pluginKey,
                tasks: tasks
            })
        })
        .then(function(res) { return res.json(); })
        .then(function(data) {
            if (data.success) {
                self.sentTasks = self.sentTasks.concat(tasks);
                self.updateTaskQueue();
                self.notify(tasks.length + ' skryptow wyslanych do Studio!', 'success');
            }
        })
        .catch(function() {
            self.notify('Blad wysylania - skopiuj recznie', 'warn');
        });
    },

    sendOneToPlugin: function(code, btnId) {
        var self = this;
        var info = this.parseScriptInfo(code);

        var task = {
            id: 'task_' + Date.now(),
            code: code,
            scriptName: info.name,
            scriptType: info.type,
            parent: info.parent,
            order: 1,
            total: 1,
            timestamp: Date.now()
        };

        fetch('/.netlify/functions/chat', {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
            body: JSON.stringify({
                action: 'addTasks',
                pluginKey: this.pluginKey,
                tasks: [task]
            })
        })
        .then(function(res) { return res.json(); })
        .then(function(data) {
            if (data.success) {
                var btn = document.getElementById('btn_' + btnId);
                if (btn) {
                    btn.className = 'code-btn sent';
                    btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-check"></i> Wyslano';
                }
                self.sentTasks.push(task);
                self.updateTaskQueue();
                self.notify(info.name + ' wyslano do Studio!', 'success');
            }
        })
        .catch(function() {
            self.notify('Blad - skopiuj recznie', 'warn');
        });
    },

    updateTaskQueue: function() {
        var html = '';
        var recent = this.sentTasks.slice(-5);
        for (var i = 0; i < recent.length; i++) {
            var t = recent[i];
            html += '<div class="task-item"><i class="fas fa-circle-check task-done"></i> ' + (t.scriptName || t.scriptType) + ' → ' + t.parent + '</div>';
        }
        this.dom.taskQueue.innerHTML = html;
    },

    autoResize: function() {
        var ta = this.dom.msgInput;
        ta.style.height = 'auto';
        ta.style.height = Math.min(ta.scrollHeight, 140) + 'px';
    },

    scrollDown: function() {
        var chat = this.dom.chat;
        requestAnimationFrame(function() { chat.scrollTop = chat.scrollHeight; });
    },

    clearChat: function() {
        this.messages = [];
        this.msgCount = 0;
        this.codeCount = 0;
        this.sentTasks = [];
        this.dom.msgCount.textContent = '0';
        this.dom.codeCount.textContent = '0';
        this.dom.insertedCount.textContent = '0';
        this.dom.messages.innerHTML = '';
        this.dom.taskQueue.innerHTML = '';
        this.dom.chatTitle.textContent = 'Nowa Rozmowa';
        this.dom.welcome.style.display = '';
        this.notify('Czat wyczyszczony', 'info');
    },

    exportChat: function() {
        if (!this.messages.length) return this.notify('Brak wiadomosci', 'warn');
        var t = '=== RoboAI Export ===\n\n';
        for (var i = 0; i < this.messages.length; i++) {
            var m = this.messages[i];
            t += (m.role === 'user' ? 'Ty' : 'AI') + ': ' + m.text + '\n\n---\n\n';
        }
        var a = document.createElement('a');
        a.href = URL.createObjectURL(new Blob([t]));
        a.download = 'roboai-' + Date.now() + '.txt';
        a.click();
        this.notify('Wyeksportowano!', 'success');
    },

    notify: function(msg, type) {
        type = type || 'info';
        var icons = { success: 'fa-check-circle', error: 'fa-times-circle', warn: 'fa-exclamation-triangle', info: 'fa-info-circle' };
        var n = document.createElement('div');
        n.className = 'notif ' + type;
        n.innerHTML = '<i class="fas ' + icons[type] + ' notif-icon"></i><span class="notif-text">' + msg + '</span><button class="notif-close" onclick="this.parentElement.remove()"><i class="fas fa-times"></i></button>';
        this.dom.notifs.appendChild(n);
        setTimeout(function() { if (n.parentElement) n.remove(); }, 4500);
    }
};

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() { App.init(); });

local function make(class, props)
    local inst = Instance.new(class)
    for k, v in pairs(props) do
        if k ~= "Parent" then inst[k] = v end
    end
    if props.Parent then inst.Parent = props.Parent end
    return inst
end

-- LOGIC
local active = false
local logN = 0
local totalScripts = 0
local pollN = 0

local function log(msg, col)
    logN = logN + 1
    make("TextLabel", {
        Size = UDim2.new(1,0,0,0), AutomaticSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.Y,
        BackgroundTransparency = 1, RichText = true,
        Text = '<font color="#5570a0">[' .. os.date("%H:%M:%S") .. ']</font> ' .. msg,
        TextColor3 = col or Color3.fromRGB(150,165,200),
        Font = Enum.Font.RobotoMono, TextSize = 10,
        TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left, TextWrapped = true,
        LayoutOrder = logN, Parent = logScroll
    })
    task.defer(function()
        logScroll.CanvasPosition = Vector2.new(0, logScroll.AbsoluteCanvasSize.Y)
    end)
end

local function getParent(name)
    local map = {
        ServerScriptService = game:GetService("ServerScriptService"),
        ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"),
        ServerStorage = game:GetService("ServerStorage"),
        Workspace = workspace,
        StarterPlayerScripts = game:GetService("StarterPlayer"):FindFirstChild("StarterPlayerScripts"),
    }
    return map[name] or game:GetService("StarterGui")
end

local function parseConfig(code)
    local name = "GeneratedScript"
    local stype = "LocalScript"
    local parent = "StarterGui"

    -- New format: -- @NAME: xxx | @TYPE: xxx | @PARENT: xxx
    local nm = code:match("@NAME:%s*([^|]+)")
    if nm then name = nm:match("^%s*(.-)%s*$") end

    local tp = code:match("@TYPE:%s*(%w+)")
    if tp then stype = tp end

    local pr = code:match("@PARENT:%s*(%w+)")
    if pr then parent = pr end

    -- Fallback old format
    if not nm then
        local ot = code:match("SCRIPT_TYPE:%s*(%w+)")
        local op = code:match("PARENT:%s*(%w+)")
        if ot then stype = ot end
        if op then parent = op end
    end

    return name, stype, parent
end

local function executeTask(t, index, total)
    local name = t.scriptName or "GeneratedScript"
    local stype = t.scriptType or "LocalScript"
    local parent = t.parent or "StarterGui"

    -- Also parse from code in case AI put config there
    local codeName, codeType, codeParent = parseConfig(t.code)
    if t.scriptName == nil or t.scriptName == "Script" then
        name = codeName
    end
    if codeName ~= "GeneratedScript" then name = codeName end
    if codeType ~= "LocalScript" then stype = codeType end
    if codeParent ~= "StarterGui" then parent = codeParent end

    local prefix = ""
    if total > 1 then
        prefix = "[" .. index .. "/" .. total .. "] "
    end

    log('<font color="#60a5fa">⏳ ' .. prefix .. 'Tworzenie: ' .. name .. '</font>')
    task.wait(0.5) -- Slow down for visual effect

    local ok, err = pcall(function()
        local inst
        if stype == "ModuleScript" then
            inst = Instance.new("ModuleScript")
        elseif stype == "Script" then
            inst = Instance.new("Script")
        else
            inst = Instance.new("LocalScript")
        end

        inst.Source = t.code
        inst.Name = name
        inst.Parent = getParent(parent)

        Sel:Set({inst})
        CHS:SetWaypoint("RoboAI: " .. name)

        totalScripts = totalScripts + 1
        statsLbl.Text = "Skryptow: " .. totalScripts .. " | Sprawdzen: " .. pollN
    end)

    if ok then
        log('<font color="#10b981">✅ ' .. prefix .. name .. ' (' .. stype .. ') → ' .. parent .. '</font>')
    else
        log('<font color="#ef4444">❌ Blad: ' .. tostring(err) .. '</font>')
    end
end

local function poll()
    local ok, result = pcall(function()
        local url = SERVER .. "/.netlify/functions/get-task?pluginKey=" .. PLUGIN_KEY
        local resp = Http:GetAsync(url, true)
        local data = Http:JSONDecode(resp)

        pollN = pollN + 1
        statsLbl.Text = "Skryptow: " .. totalScripts .. " | Sprawdzen: " .. pollN

        if data.tasks and #data.tasks > 0 then
            local count = #data.tasks
            log('<font color="#60a5fa">📦 Otrzymano ' .. count .. ' skryptow!</font>')

            -- Sort by order if available
            table.sort(data.tasks, function(a, b)
                return (a.order or 0) < (b.order or 0)
            end)

            for i, taskData in ipairs(data.tasks) do
                executeTask(taskData, i, count)
                if i < count then
                    task.wait(0.8) -- Delay between scripts
                end
            end

            log('<font color="#10b981">✅ Wszystkie ' .. count .. ' skrypty wstawione!</font>')
        end
    end)

    if ok then
        sDot.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(16,185,129)
        sText.Text = "Polaczono - nasluchuje..."
        sText.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(16,185,129)
    else
        sDot.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(245,158,11)
        sText.Text = "Blad polaczenia"
        sText.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200,150,50)
    end
end

local function start()
    if active then return end
    active = true
    goBtn.Text = "⏸  ZATRZYMAJ"
    goBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(239,68,68)

    log('<font color="#10b981">🚀 Plugin uruchomiony!</font>')
    log('<font color="#60a5fa">🔗 ' .. SERVER .. '</font>')
    log('<font color="#8a9bc0">⏱ Sprawdzam co ' .. DELAY .. 's</font>')

    sDot.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(16,185,129)
    sText.Text = "Aktywny"
    sText.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(16,185,129)

    task.spawn(function()
        while active do
            poll()
            task.wait(DELAY)
        end
    end)
end

local function stop()
    active = false
    goBtn.Text = "▶  URUCHOM"
    goBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(59,130,246)
    sDot.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(245,158,11)
    sText.Text = "Zatrzymany"
    sText.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(245,158,11)
    log('<font color="#f59e0b">⏸ Zatrzymano</font>')
end

goBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
    if active then stop() else start() end
end)

mainBtn.Click:Connect(function()
    w.Enabled = not w.Enabled
end)

log('<font color="#60a5fa">🤖 RoboAI v4</font>')
log('<font color="#8a9bc0">Kliknij URUCHOM</font>')

Naprawiam oba pliki
Krok 1: Zmień chat.js
Otwórz netlify/functions/chat.js, usuń wszystko, wklej:

JavaScript

exports.handler = async (event) => {
    const headers = {
        "Access-Control-Allow-Origin": "*",
        "Access-Control-Allow-Headers": "Content-Type",
        "Access-Control-Allow-Methods": "GET, POST, OPTIONS",
        "Content-Type": "application/json"
    };

    if (event.httpMethod === "OPTIONS") {
        return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: "" };
    }

    if (event.httpMethod !== "POST") {
        return { statusCode: 405, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "POST only" }) };
    }

    var redisUrl = process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_URL;
    var redisToken = process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_TOKEN;

    try {
        var body = JSON.parse(event.body);

        // STORE TASKS
        if (body.action === "addTasks" || body.action === "addTask") {
            if (!redisUrl || !redisToken) {
                return { statusCode: 500, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ success: false, error: "Redis not configured" }) };
            }

            var pluginKey = body.pluginKey;
            var newTasks = body.tasks || [body.task];

            // Get existing
            var getRes = await fetch(redisUrl + "/get/" + pluginKey, {
                headers: { "Authorization": "Bearer " + redisToken }
            });
            var getData = await getRes.json();

            var allTasks = [];
            if (getData.result && getData.result !== null) {
                try {
                    allTasks = JSON.parse(getData.result);
                } catch(e) {
                    allTasks = [];
                }
            }

            for (var i = 0; i < newTasks.length; i++) {
                allTasks.push(newTasks[i]);
            }

            // Save as string using SET with POST body
            var saveRes = await fetch(redisUrl, {
                method: "POST",
                headers: {
                    "Authorization": "Bearer " + redisToken,
                    "Content-Type": "application/json"
                },
                body: JSON.stringify(["SET", pluginKey, JSON.stringify(allTasks), "EX", "3600"])
            });
            var saveData = await saveRes.json();

            return {
                statusCode: 200,
                headers,
                body: JSON.stringify({ success: true, count: newTasks.length, total: allTasks.length, redis: saveData })
            };
        }

        // AI CHAT
        var apiKey = body.apiKey;
        var messages = body.messages;
        var model = body.model;
        var testMode = body.testMode;

        if (!apiKey) {
            return { statusCode: 400, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "Brak klucza API" }) };
        }

        if (testMode) {
            var test = await fetch("https://api.groq.com/openai/v1/models", {
                headers: { "Authorization": "Bearer " + apiKey }
            });
            return {
                statusCode: test.ok ? 200 : 401,
                headers,
                body: JSON.stringify(test.ok ? { success: true } : { error: "Zly klucz API Groq" })
            };
        }

        var aiRes = await fetch("https://api.groq.com/openai/v1/chat/completions", {
            method: "POST",
            headers: {
                "Content-Type": "application/json",
                "Authorization": "Bearer " + apiKey
            },
            body: JSON.stringify({
                model: model || "llama-3.3-70b-versatile",
                messages: messages,
                max_tokens: 8000,
                temperature: 0.7
            })
        });

        if (!aiRes.ok) {
            var errData = await aiRes.json();
            return {
                statusCode: aiRes.status,
                headers,
                body: JSON.stringify({ error: errData.error ? errData.error.message : "Blad Groq" })
            };
        }

        var data = await aiRes.json();
        var content = "Brak odpowiedzi";
        if (data.choices && data.choices[0] && data.choices[0].message) {
            content = data.choices[0].message.content;
        }

        return {
            statusCode: 200,
            headers,
            body: JSON.stringify({ content: content })
        };

    } catch (err) {
        return {
            statusCode: 500,
            headers,
            body: JSON.stringify({ error: "Server error: " + err.message })
        };
    }
};
Krok 2: Zmień get-task.js
Otwórz netlify/functions/get-task.js, usuń wszystko, wklej:

JavaScript

exports.handler = async (event) => {
    var headers = {
        "Access-Control-Allow-Origin": "*",
        "Access-Control-Allow-Headers": "Content-Type",
        "Access-Control-Allow-Methods": "GET, POST, OPTIONS",
        "Content-Type": "application/json"
    };

    if (event.httpMethod === "OPTIONS") {
        return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: "" };
    }

    var redisUrl = process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_URL;
    var redisToken = process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_TOKEN;

    if (!redisUrl || !redisToken) {
        return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ tasks: [], error: "Redis not configured" }) };
    }

    // POST = clear tasks
    if (event.httpMethod === "POST") {
        try {
            var postBody = JSON.parse(event.body);
            if (postBody.pluginKey) {
                await fetch(redisUrl, {
                    method: "POST",
                    headers: {
                        "Authorization": "Bearer " + redisToken,
                        "Content-Type": "application/json"
                    },
                    body: JSON.stringify(["DEL", postBody.pluginKey])
                });
            }
        } catch (e) {}
        return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ success: true }) };
    }

    // GET = fetch tasks
    var pluginKey = null;
    if (event.queryStringParameters) {
        pluginKey = event.queryStringParameters.pluginKey;
    }

    if (!pluginKey) {
        return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ tasks: [], error: "no key" }) };
    }

    try {
        // GET from Redis using POST command format
        var getRes = await fetch(redisUrl, {
            method: "POST",
            headers: {
                "Authorization": "Bearer " + redisToken,
                "Content-Type": "application/json"
            },
            body: JSON.stringify(["GET", pluginKey])
        });
        var getData = await getRes.json();

        var tasks = [];
        if (getData.result && getData.result !== null) {
            try {
                tasks = JSON.parse(getData.result);
            } catch(e) {
                tasks = [];
            }
        }

        // Delete after fetching
        if (tasks.length > 0) {
            await fetch(redisUrl, {
                method: "POST",
                headers: {
                    "Authorization": "Bearer " + redisToken,
                    "Content-Type": "application/json"
                },
                body: JSON.stringify(["DEL", pluginKey])
            });
        }

        return {
            statusCode: 200,
            headers,
            body: JSON.stringify({ tasks: tasks, count: tasks.length })
        };

    } catch (err) {
        return {
            statusCode: 200,
            headers,
            body: JSON.stringify({ tasks: [], error: err.message })
        };
    }
};
