[build]
  command = "npm install"
  functions = "netlify/functions"
  publish = "."

[functions]
  node_bundler = "esbuild"
  external_node_modules = ["@upstash/redis"]

[[headers]]
  for = "/*"
  [headers.values]
    Access-Control-Allow-Origin = "*"
    Access-Control-Allow-Headers = "Content-Type"
    Access-Control-Allow-Methods = "GET, POST, OPTIONS"
Krok 3: Zmień chat.js
Otwórz netlify/functions/chat.js, usuń wszystko, wklej:

JavaScript

exports.handler = async (event) => {
    const headers = {
        "Access-Control-Allow-Origin": "*",
        "Access-Control-Allow-Headers": "Content-Type",
        "Access-Control-Allow-Methods": "GET, POST, OPTIONS",
        "Content-Type": "application/json"
    };

    if (event.httpMethod === "OPTIONS") {
        return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: "" };
    }

    if (event.httpMethod !== "POST") {
        return { statusCode: 405, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "POST only" }) };
    }

    try {
        const body = JSON.parse(event.body);

        // STORE TASKS - using Upstash REST API directly (no SDK issues)
        if (body.action === "addTasks" || body.action === "addTask") {
            const redisUrl = process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_URL;
            const redisToken = process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_TOKEN;

            if (!redisUrl || !redisToken) {
                return {
                    statusCode: 500,
                    headers,
                    body: JSON.stringify({ success: false, error: "Redis not configured" })
                };
            }

            const pluginKey = body.pluginKey;
            const newTasks = body.tasks || [body.task];
            const taskData = JSON.stringify(newTasks);

            // GET existing tasks
            const getRes = await fetch(redisUrl + "/get/" + pluginKey, {
                headers: { "Authorization": "Bearer " + redisToken }
            });
            const getData = await getRes.json();

            let allTasks = [];
            if (getData.result) {
                try {
                    allTasks = JSON.parse(getData.result);
                } catch(e) {
                    allTasks = [];
                }
            }

            allTasks = allTasks.concat(newTasks);

            // SET tasks with 1 hour expiry
            const setRes = await fetch(redisUrl + "/set/" + pluginKey + "/ex/3600", {
                method: "POST",
                headers: {
                    "Authorization": "Bearer " + redisToken,
                    "Content-Type": "application/json"
                },
                body: JSON.stringify(allTasks)
            });

            return {
                statusCode: 200,
                headers,
                body: JSON.stringify({ success: true, count: newTasks.length, total: allTasks.length })
            };
        }

        // AI CHAT
        const { apiKey, messages, model, testMode } = body;

        if (!apiKey) {
            return { statusCode: 400, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "Brak klucza API" }) };
        }

        if (testMode) {
            const test = await fetch("https://api.groq.com/openai/v1/models", {
                headers: { "Authorization": "Bearer " + apiKey }
            });
            return {
                statusCode: test.ok ? 200 : 401,
                headers,
                body: JSON.stringify(test.ok ? { success: true } : { error: "Zly klucz API Groq" })
            };
        }

        const aiRes = await fetch("https://api.groq.com/openai/v1/chat/completions", {
            method: "POST",
            headers: {
                "Content-Type": "application/json",
                "Authorization": "Bearer " + apiKey
            },
            body: JSON.stringify({
                model: model || "llama-3.3-70b-versatile",
                messages: messages,
                max_tokens: 8000,
                temperature: 0.7
            })
        });

        if (!aiRes.ok) {
            const err = await aiRes.json();
            return {
                statusCode: aiRes.status,
                headers,
                body: JSON.stringify({ error: err.error?.message || "Blad Groq" })
            };
        }

        const data = await aiRes.json();
        const content = data.choices && data.choices[0] ? data.choices[0].message.content : "Brak odpowiedzi";

        return {
            statusCode: 200,
            headers,
            body: JSON.stringify({ content: content })
        };

    } catch (err) {
        return {
            statusCode: 500,
            headers,
            body: JSON.stringify({ error: "Server error: " + err.message })
        };
    }
};
Krok 4: Zmień get-task.js
Otwórz netlify/functions/get-task.js, usuń wszystko, wklej:

JavaScript

exports.handler = async (event) => {
    const headers = {
        "Access-Control-Allow-Origin": "*",
        "Access-Control-Allow-Headers": "Content-Type",
        "Access-Control-Allow-Methods": "GET, POST, OPTIONS",
        "Content-Type": "application/json"
    };

    if (event.httpMethod === "OPTIONS") {
        return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: "" };
    }

    const redisUrl = process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_URL;
    const redisToken = process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_TOKEN;

    if (!redisUrl || !redisToken) {
        return {
            statusCode: 200,
            headers,
            body: JSON.stringify({ tasks: [], error: "Redis not configured" })
        };
    }

    // POST = plugin confirms done
    if (event.httpMethod === "POST") {
        try {
            const body = JSON.parse(event.body);
            if (body.pluginKey) {
                await fetch(redisUrl + "/del/" + body.pluginKey, {
                    headers: { "Authorization": "Bearer " + redisToken }
                });
            }
        } catch (e) {}
        return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ success: true }) };
    }

    // GET = plugin fetches tasks
    const pluginKey = event.queryStringParameters && event.queryStringParameters.pluginKey;
    if (!pluginKey) {
        return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ tasks: [], error: "no key" }) };
    }

    try {
        // GET tasks from Redis
        const getRes = await fetch(redisUrl + "/get/" + pluginKey, {
            headers: { "Authorization": "Bearer " + redisToken }
        });
        const getData = await getRes.json();

        let tasks = [];
        if (getData.result) {
            try {
                tasks = JSON.parse(getData.result);
            } catch(e) {
                tasks = [];
            }
        }

        // DELETE tasks after fetching (so plugin doesn't get them twice)
        if (tasks.length > 0) {
            await fetch(redisUrl + "/del/" + pluginKey, {
                headers: { "Authorization": "Bearer " + redisToken }
            });
        }

        return {
            statusCode: 200,
            headers,
            body: JSON.stringify({ tasks: tasks, count: tasks.length })
        };

    } catch (err) {
        return {
            statusCode: 200,
            headers,
            body: JSON.stringify({ tasks: [], error: err.message })
        };
    }
};

Krok 3: Zmień chat.js
Otwórz netlify/functions/chat.js, usuń wszystko, wklej:

JavaScript

const { getStore } = require("@netlify/blobs");

exports.handler = async (event) => {
    const headers = {
        "Access-Control-Allow-Origin": "*",
        "Access-Control-Allow-Headers": "Content-Type",
        "Access-Control-Allow-Methods": "GET, POST, OPTIONS",
        "Content-Type": "application/json"
    };

    if (event.httpMethod === "OPTIONS") {
        return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: "" };
    }

    if (event.httpMethod !== "POST") {
        return { statusCode: 405, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "POST only" }) };
    }

    try {
        const body = JSON.parse(event.body);

        // STORE TASKS FOR PLUGIN
        if (body.action === "addTasks" || body.action === "addTask") {
            const store = getStore("roboai-tasks");
            const pluginKey = body.pluginKey;
            const newTasks = body.tasks || [body.task];

            // Get existing tasks
            let existing = [];
            try {
                const data = await store.get(pluginKey);
                if (data) {
                    existing = JSON.parse(data);
                }
            } catch (e) {
                existing = [];
            }

            // Add new tasks
            existing = existing.concat(newTasks);
            await store.set(pluginKey, JSON.stringify(existing));

            return {
                statusCode: 200,
                headers,
                body: JSON.stringify({ success: true, count: newTasks.length, total: existing.length })
            };
        }

        // AI CHAT
        const { apiKey, messages, model, testMode } = body;

        if (!apiKey) {
            return { statusCode: 400, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "Brak klucza API" }) };
        }

        if (testMode) {
            const test = await fetch("https://api.groq.com/openai/v1/models", {
                headers: { "Authorization": "Bearer " + apiKey }
            });
            return {
                statusCode: test.ok ? 200 : 401,
                headers,
                body: JSON.stringify(test.ok ? { success: true } : { error: "Zly klucz API Groq" })
            };
        }

        const aiRes = await fetch("https://api.groq.com/openai/v1/chat/completions", {
            method: "POST",
            headers: {
                "Content-Type": "application/json",
                "Authorization": "Bearer " + apiKey
            },
            body: JSON.stringify({
                model: model || "llama-3.3-70b-versatile",
                messages: messages,
                max_tokens: 8000,
                temperature: 0.7
            })
        });

        if (!aiRes.ok) {
            const err = await aiRes.json();
            return {
                statusCode: aiRes.status,
                headers,
                body: JSON.stringify({ error: err.error?.message || "Blad Groq" })
            };
        }

        const data = await aiRes.json();
        const content = data.choices && data.choices[0] ? data.choices[0].message.content : "Brak odpowiedzi";

        return {
            statusCode: 200,
            headers,
            body: JSON.stringify({ content: content })
        };

    } catch (err) {
        return {
            statusCode: 500,
            headers,
            body: JSON.stringify({ error: "Server error: " + err.message })
        };
    }
};
Krok 4: Zmień get-task.js
Otwórz netlify/functions/get-task.js, usuń wszystko, wklej:

JavaScript

const { getStore } = require("@netlify/blobs");

exports.handler = async (event) => {
    const headers = {
        "Access-Control-Allow-Origin": "*",
        "Access-Control-Allow-Headers": "Content-Type",
        "Access-Control-Allow-Methods": "GET, POST, OPTIONS",
        "Content-Type": "application/json"
    };

    if (event.httpMethod === "OPTIONS") {
        return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: "" };
    }

    // POST = plugin potwierdza wykonanie
    if (event.httpMethod === "POST") {
        try {
            const body = JSON.parse(event.body);
            if (body.pluginKey && body.action === "confirm") {
                const store = getStore("roboai-tasks");
                // Clear tasks after plugin confirms
                await store.set(body.pluginKey, JSON.stringify([]));
            }
        } catch (e) {}
        return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ success: true }) };
    }

    // GET = plugin pobiera taski
    const pluginKey = event.queryStringParameters && event.queryStringParameters.pluginKey;
    if (!pluginKey) {
        return { statusCode: 400, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: "pluginKey required", tasks: [] }) };
    }

    try {
        const store = getStore("roboai-tasks");
        let tasks = [];

        try {
            const data = await store.get(pluginKey);
            if (data) {
                tasks = JSON.parse(data);
            }
        } catch (e) {
            tasks = [];
        }

        // Clear tasks after sending to plugin
        if (tasks.length > 0) {
            await store.set(pluginKey, JSON.stringify([]));
        }

        return {
            statusCode: 200,
            headers,
            body: JSON.stringify({ tasks: tasks, count: tasks.length })
        };

    } catch (err) {
        return {
            statusCode: 200,
            headers,
            body: JSON.stringify({ tasks: [], error: err.message })
        };
    }
};

local function create(class, props)
    local inst = Instance.new(class)
    for k, v in pairs(props) do
        if k ~= "Parent" and k ~= "Children" then
            inst[k] = v
        end
    end
    if props.Children then
        for _, child in ipairs(props.Children) do
            child.Parent = inst
        end
    end
    if props.Parent then
        inst.Parent = props.Parent
    end
    return inst
end

---------------------------------------------
-- LOGIC
---------------------------------------------
local active = false
local logCount = 0
local totalScripts = 0
local pollCount = 0

local function addLog(msg, color)
    logCount = logCount + 1
    local lbl = create("TextLabel", {
        Size = UDim2.new(1,0,0,0),
        AutomaticSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.Y,
        BackgroundTransparency = 1,
        RichText = true,
        Text = '<font color="#5570a0">[' .. os.date("%H:%M:%S") .. ']</font> ' .. msg,
        TextColor3 = color or Color3.fromRGB(150,165,200),
        Font = Enum.Font.RobotoMono,
        TextSize = 10,
        TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left,
        TextWrapped = true,
        LayoutOrder = logCount,
        Parent = logScroll
    })
    task.defer(function()
        logScroll.CanvasPosition = Vector2.new(0, logScroll.AbsoluteCanvasSize.Y)
    end)
end

local function setConnected(yes)
    if yes then
        connDot.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(16,185,129)
        connText.Text = "Polaczono - nasluchuje..."
        connText.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(16,185,129)
    else
        connDot.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(239,68,68)
        connText.Text = "Rozlaczono"
        connText.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200,100,100)
    end
end

local function updateStats()
    statsText.Text = "Skryptow: " .. totalScripts .. "  |  Sprawdzen: " .. pollCount
end

local function getParent(name)
    if name == "ServerScriptService" then return SSS
    elseif name == "ReplicatedStorage" then return RS
    elseif name == "StarterPlayerScripts" then
        local sps = SP:FindFirstChild("StarterPlayerScripts")
        if sps then return sps end
        return StarterGui
    elseif name == "Workspace" then return workspace
    else return StarterGui
    end
end

local function executeTask(taskData)
    local success, err = pcall(function()
        local sType = taskData.scriptType or "LocalScript"
        local pName = taskData.parent or "StarterGui"

        local scriptInst
        if sType == "ModuleScript" then
            scriptInst = Instance.new("ModuleScript")
        elseif sType == "Script" then
            scriptInst = Instance.new("Script")
        else
            scriptInst = Instance.new("LocalScript")
        end

        scriptInst.Source = taskData.code
        scriptInst.Name = "RoboAI_" .. sType .. "_" .. tostring(os.time()) .. math.random(100,999)

        local parentInst = getParent(pName)
        scriptInst.Parent = parentInst

        Selection:Set({scriptInst})
        ChangeHistory:SetWaypoint("RoboAI: Created " .. sType)

        totalScripts = totalScripts + 1
        updateStats()

        addLog('<font color="#10b981">✅ ' .. sType .. ' → ' .. pName .. '</font>', Color3.fromRGB(16,185,129))
    end)

    if not success then
        addLog('<font color="#ef4444">❌ Blad: ' .. tostring(err) .. '</font>', Color3.fromRGB(239,68,68))
    end
end

local function pollServer()
    local success, result = pcall(function()
        local url = SERVER .. "/.netlify/functions/get-task?pluginKey=" .. PLUGIN_KEY
        local response = HttpService:GetAsync(url, true)
        local data = HttpService:JSONDecode(response)

        pollCount = pollCount + 1
        updateStats()

        if data.tasks and #data.tasks > 0 then
            addLog('<font color="#60a5fa">📦 Otrzymano ' .. #data.tasks .. ' skryptow!</font>', Color3.fromRGB(96,165,250))

            for i, taskData in ipairs(data.tasks) do
                addLog('<font color="#8a9bc0">⏳ Wstawiam skrypt ' .. i .. '/' .. #data.tasks .. '...</font>')
                executeTask(taskData)
                if i < #data.tasks then
                    task.wait(0.3)
                end
            end

            -- Potwierdz wykonanie
            pcall(function()
                HttpService:PostAsync(
                    SERVER .. "/.netlify/functions/get-task",
                    HttpService:JSONEncode({ pluginKey = PLUGIN_KEY, action = "confirm" }),
                    Enum.HttpContentType.ApplicationJson
                )
            end)

            addLog('<font color="#10b981">✅ Wszystkie skrypty wstawione!</font>', Color3.fromRGB(16,185,129))
        end
    end)

    if not success then
        addLog('<font color="#f59e0b">⚠ Blad polaczenia</font>', Color3.fromRGB(200,150,50))
        setConnected(false)
    else
        setConnected(true)
    end
end

local function startPlugin()
    if active then return end
    active = true

    startBtn.Text = "⏸  ZATRZYMAJ PLUGIN"
    -- Change gradient to red
    local grad = startBtn:FindFirstChildOfClass("UIGradient")
    if grad then
        grad.Color = ColorSequence.new(Color3.fromRGB(239,68,68), Color3.fromRGB(200,50,50))
    end

    addLog('<font color="#10b981">🚀 Plugin uruchomiony!</font>', Color3.fromRGB(16,185,129))
    addLog('<font color="#60a5fa">🔗 ' .. SERVER .. '</font>', Color3.fromRGB(96,165,250))
    addLog('<font color="#60a5fa">🔑 ' .. string.sub(PLUGIN_KEY, 1, 15) .. '...</font>', Color3.fromRGB(96,165,250))
    addLog('<font color="#8a9bc0">⏱ Sprawdzam co ' .. DELAY .. 's</font>')

    setConnected(true)

    task.spawn(function()
        while active do
            pollServer()
            task.wait(DELAY)
        end
    end)
end

local function stopPlugin()
    active = false

    startBtn.Text = "▶  URUCHOM PLUGIN"
    local grad = startBtn:FindFirstChildOfClass("UIGradient")
    if grad then
        grad.Color = ColorSequence.new(Color3.fromRGB(59,130,246), Color3.fromRGB(99,102,241))
    end

    setConnected(false)
    connText.Text = "Zatrzymany"
    connDot.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(245,158,11)
    connText.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(245,158,11)

    addLog('<font color="#f59e0b">⏸ Plugin zatrzymany</font>', Color3.fromRGB(245,158,11))
end

-- Events
startBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
    if active then
        stopPlugin()
    else
        startPlugin()
    end
end)

mainBtn.Click:Connect(function()
    w.Enabled = not w.Enabled
end)

-- Init
addLog('<font color="#60a5fa">🤖 RoboAI Studio v3</font>', Color3.fromRGB(96,165,250))
addLog('<font color="#8a9bc0">Kliknij URUCHOM aby polaczyc ze strona</font>')
addLog('<font color="#5570a0">Upewnij sie ze HttpService jest wlaczony!</font>')
Krok 8: Zmień PLUGIN_KEY w pluginie
W pliku RoboAI.lua zmień:

Lua

local PLUGIN_KEY = "WKLEJ_SWOJ_KLUCZ"
Na klucz ze strony (ten rk_... widoczny w sidebarze).

Krok 9: W Roblox Studio
Zrestartuj Studio
Home → Game Settings → Security → Allow HTTP Requests → ON
Kliknij RoboAI w toolbarze
Kliknij URUCHOM PLUGIN
Krok 10: Testuj!
Na stronie fleetyai.netlify.app wpisz: "Stwórz prosty przycisk GUI"
Poczekaj na odpowiedź
W Roblox Studio plugin powinien automatycznie odebrać i wstawić skrypt
Wypchnij pliki (git add, commit, push), poczekaj 2 min i napisz mi co się dzieje! 🚀

Krok 1: Najpierw sprawdź - czy AI w ogóle odpowiada?
Otwórz https://fleetyai.netlify.app
Wklej klucz Groq (gsk_...)
Kliknij Połącz z AI
Wpisz: "powiedz cześć"
Co się dzieje? Napisz mi:

A) AI odpowiada ✅
B) Błąd ❌ (jaki?)
C) Ładuje się bez końca
Najpierw muszę wiedzieć czy AI działa, potem naprawię plugin. Napisz A, B lub C! 👍

Pełna naprawa - WSZYSTKIE pliki od zera
Daję ci kompletnie nowe pliki. Usuń wszystko z folderu projektu i stwórz od nowa.

Struktura plików - upewnij się że masz DOKŁADNIE to:
text

C:\Users\Janus\Desktop\roblox-ai-assistant\
├── index.html
├── style.css
├── script.js
├── package.json
├── netlify.toml
└── netlify\
    └── functions\
        ├── chat.js
        └── get-task.js
Usuń plik complete-task.js jeśli istnieje!

    Access-Control-Allow-Origin = "*"
    Access-Control-Allow-Headers = "Content-Type"
    Access-Control-Allow-Methods = "GET, POST, OPTIONS"

📄 script.js
JavaScript

var App = {
    apiKey: localStorage.getItem('roboai_key') || '',
    pluginKey: localStorage.getItem('roboai_pkey') || '',
    messages: [],
    generating: false,
    msgCount: 0,
    codeCount: 0,
    insertedCount: 0,
    sentTasks: [],

    init: function() {
        if (!this.pluginKey) {
            this.pluginKey = 'rk_' + Date.now() + '_' + Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 10);
            localStorage.setItem('roboai_pkey', this.pluginKey);
        }
        this.cacheDom();
        this.bindEvents();
        this.loadKey();
        this.showPluginKey();
        this.startTaskMonitor();
    },

    cacheDom: function() {
        this.dom = {
            sidebar: document.getElementById('sidebar'),
            menuBtn: document.getElementById('menuBtn'),
            statusDot: document.getElementById('statusDot'),
            statusText: document.getElementById('statusText'),
            apiKeyInput: document.getElementById('apiKeyInput'),
            toggleKey: document.getElementById('toggleKey'),
            connectBtn: document.getElementById('connectBtn'),
            pluginKeyDisplay: document.getElementById('pluginKeyDisplay'),
            copyPluginKey: document.getElementById('copyPluginKey'),
            pluginDot: document.getElementById('pluginDot'),
            pluginStatusText: document.getElementById('pluginStatusText'),
            taskQueue: document.getElementById('taskQueue'),
            chat: document.getElementById('chat'),
            welcome: document.getElementById('welcome'),
            messages: document.getElementById('messages'),
            typing: document.getElementById('typing'),
            msgInput: document.getElementById('msgInput'),
            sendBtn: document.getElementById('sendBtn'),
            autoInsert: document.getElementById('autoInsert'),
            modelSelect: document.getElementById('modelSelect'),
            chatTitle: document.getElementById('chatTitle'),
            msgCount: document.getElementById('msgCount'),
            codeCount: document.getElementById('codeCount'),
            insertedCount: document.getElementById('insertedCount'),
            clearBtn: document.getElementById('clearBtn'),
            exportBtn: document.getElementById('exportBtn'),
            notifs: document.getElementById('notifs')
        };
    },

    bindEvents: function() {
        var self = this;

        this.dom.menuBtn.addEventListener('click', function() {
            self.dom.sidebar.classList.toggle('open');
        });

        document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
            if (window.innerWidth <= 768 && !self.dom.sidebar.contains(e.target) && !self.dom.menuBtn.contains(e.target)) {
                self.dom.sidebar.classList.remove('open');
            }
        });

        this.dom.toggleKey.addEventListener('click', function() {
            var inp = self.dom.apiKeyInput;
            var ico = self.dom.toggleKey.querySelector('i');
            if (inp.type === 'password') { inp.type = 'text'; ico.className = 'fas fa-eye-slash'; }
            else { inp.type = 'password'; ico.className = 'fas fa-eye'; }
        });

        this.dom.connectBtn.addEventListener('click', function() { self.connect(); });

        this.dom.copyPluginKey.addEventListener('click', function() {
            navigator.clipboard.writeText(self.pluginKey);
            self.notify('Klucz skopiowany!', 'success');
        });

        this.dom.sendBtn.addEventListener('click', function() { self.send(); });
        this.dom.msgInput.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
            if (e.key === 'Enter' && !e.shiftKey) { e.preventDefault(); self.send(); }
        });
        this.dom.msgInput.addEventListener('input', function() {
            self.dom.sendBtn.disabled = !self.dom.msgInput.value.trim() || self.generating;
            self.autoResize();
        });

        document.querySelectorAll('.action-btn, .chip').forEach(function(btn) {
            btn.addEventListener('click', function() {
                var p = btn.dataset.prompt;
                if (p) { self.dom.msgInput.value = p; self.dom.sendBtn.disabled = false; self.send(); }
            });
        });

        this.dom.clearBtn.addEventListener('click', function() { self.clearChat(); });
        this.dom.exportBtn.addEventListener('click', function() { self.exportChat(); });
    },

    loadKey: function() {
        if (this.apiKey) this.dom.apiKeyInput.value = this.apiKey;
    },

    showPluginKey: function() {
        this.dom.pluginKeyDisplay.textContent = this.pluginKey;
    },

    connect: function() {
        var self = this;
        var key = this.dom.apiKeyInput.value.trim();
        if (!key) return this.notify('Wpisz klucz API Groq!', 'error');

        this.apiKey = key;
        localStorage.setItem('roboai_key', key);
        this.setStatus('connecting', 'Laczenie...');

        fetch('/.netlify/functions/chat', {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
            body: JSON.stringify({ apiKey: key, testMode: true })
        })
        .then(function(res) { return res.json().then(function(d) { return { ok: res.ok, data: d }; }); })
        .then(function(r) {
            if (r.ok && r.data.success) {
                self.setStatus('online', 'Polaczono z Groq AI');
                self.notify('Polaczono z AI!', 'success');
            } else {
                throw new Error(r.data.error || 'Blad polaczenia');
            }
        })
        .catch(function(err) {
            self.setStatus('offline', 'Blad polaczenia');
            self.notify(err.message, 'error');
        });
    },

    setStatus: function(state, text) {
        this.dom.statusDot.className = 'status-dot ' + state;
        this.dom.statusText.textContent = text;
    },

    send: function() {
        var self = this;
        var text = this.dom.msgInput.value.trim();
        if (!text || this.generating) return;
        if (!this.apiKey) return this.notify('Najpierw polacz sie z AI!', 'warn');

        this.dom.welcome.style.display = 'none';
        this.addMsg('user', text);
        this.dom.msgInput.value = '';
        this.dom.sendBtn.disabled = true;
        this.autoResize();

        if (this.messages.length === 1) {
            this.dom.chatTitle.textContent = text.length > 45 ? text.slice(0, 45) + '...' : text;
        }

        this.generating = true;
        this.dom.typing.classList.add('active');
        this.scrollDown();

        var sysPrompt = this.getSystemPrompt();
        var apiMsgs = [{ role: 'system', content: sysPrompt }];
        for (var i = 0; i < this.messages.length; i++) {
            apiMsgs.push({ role: this.messages[i].role, content: this.messages[i].text });
        }

        fetch('/.netlify/functions/chat', {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
            body: JSON.stringify({
                apiKey: this.apiKey,
                messages: apiMsgs,
                model: this.dom.modelSelect.value
            })
        })
        .then(function(res) {
            if (!res.ok) return res.json().then(function(d) { throw new Error(d.error || 'Blad API'); });
            return res.json();
        })
        .then(function(data) {
            self.addMsg('bot', data.content);

            // Auto wysylanie WSZYSTKICH blokow kodu do pluginu
            if (self.dom.autoInsert.checked) {
                var blocks = self.extractCode(data.content);
                if (blocks.length > 0) {
                    self.notify('Znaleziono ' + blocks.length + ' skryptow - wysylam do Studio...', 'info');
                    self.sendAllToPlugin(blocks);
                }
            }
        })
        .catch(function(err) {
            self.addMsg('bot', 'Blad: ' + err.message);
            self.notify(err.message, 'error');
        })
        .finally(function() {
            self.generating = false;
            self.dom.typing.classList.remove('active');
            self.dom.sendBtn.disabled = !self.dom.msgInput.value.trim();
        });
    },

    getSystemPrompt: function() {
        return 'Jestes ekspertem od Roblox Studio i Luau. Generujesz gotowy kod do wklejenia.\n\n' +
        'ZASADY:\n' +
        '1. Pisz WYLACZNIE w Luau (Roblox Lua)\n' +
        '2. Kod musi dzialac natychmiast po wklejeniu do Roblox Studio\n' +
        '3. Dla GUI tworz pelne drzewa z Instance.new() - ScreenGui, Frame, TextButton, UICorner, UIStroke, UIGradient, UIListLayout itp.\n' +
        '4. Dodawaj animacje TweenService\n' +
        '5. KAZDY blok kodu MUSI byc oznaczony jako ```lua\n' +
        '6. KAZDY skrypt MUSI miec na SAMYM KONCU te dwa komentarze:\n' +
        '   -- SCRIPT_TYPE: LocalScript\n' +
        '   -- PARENT: StarterGui\n' +
        '   Dozwolone SCRIPT_TYPE: LocalScript, Script, ModuleScript\n' +
        '   Dozwolone PARENT: StarterGui, ServerScriptService, ReplicatedStorage, StarterPlayerScripts\n' +
        '7. Mozesz generowac WIELE skryptow w jednej odpowiedzi - kazdy w osobnym bloku ```lua\n' +
        '8. Odpowiadaj po polsku\n' +
        '9. Badz szczegolowy - dodawaj komentarze w kodzie\n' +
        '10. Tworzac GUI uzywaj ladnych kolorow, gradientow, zaokraglen i animacji\n' +
        '11. Kazdy skrypt powinien byc kompletny i niezalezny';
    },

    addMsg: function(role, text) {
        this.messages.push({ role: role === 'bot' ? 'assistant' : role, text: text });
        this.msgCount++;
        this.dom.msgCount.textContent = this.msgCount;

        var time = new Date().toLocaleTimeString('pl-PL', { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit' });
        var div = document.createElement('div');
        div.className = 'msg ' + role;

        var icon = role === 'bot' ? 'fa-robot' : 'fa-user';
        var content = role === 'bot' ? this.renderContent(text) : this.esc(text);

        div.innerHTML = '<div class="msg-avatar"><i class="fas ' + icon + '"></i></div>' +
            '<div class="msg-body"><div class="msg-bubble">' + content + '</div>' +
            '<div class="msg-time">' + time + '</div></div>';

        this.dom.messages.appendChild(div);
        this.scrollDown();
    },

    renderContent: function(text) {
        var self = this;
        var html = text;

        html = html.replace(/```(\w+)?\n([\s\S]*?)```/g, function(_, lang, code) {
            self.codeCount++;
            self.dom.codeCount.textContent = self.codeCount;
            var id = 'c' + Date.now() + Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 7);

            var scriptType = 'LocalScript';
            var parent = 'StarterGui';
            var tm = code.match(/--\s*SCRIPT_TYPE:\s*(\w+)/i);
            var pm = code.match(/--\s*PARENT:\s*(\w+)/i);
            if (tm) scriptType = tm[1];
            if (pm) parent = pm[1];

            return '<div class="code-wrap" id="' + id + '">' +
                '<div class="code-top">' +
                '<span class="code-lang"><i class="fas fa-code"></i> ' + (lang || 'lua') + ' | ' + scriptType + ' → ' + parent + '</span>' +
                '<div class="code-btns">' +
                '<button class="code-btn" onclick="App.copyCode(\'' + id + '\')"><i class="fas fa-copy"></i> Kopiuj</button>' +
                '<button class="code-btn run" id="btn_' + id + '" onclick="App.runCode(\'' + id + '\')"><i class="fas fa-play"></i> Wstaw do Studio</button>' +
                '</div></div>' +
                '<pre><code>' + self.esc(code.trim()) + '</code></pre></div>';
        });

        html = html.replace(/`([^`]+)`/g, '<code>$1</code>');
        html = html.replace(/\*\*(.*?)\*\*/g, '<strong>$1</strong>');
        html = html.replace(/\n/g, '<br>');
        return html;
    },

    esc: function(t) {
        var d = document.createElement('div');
        d.textContent = t;
        return d.innerHTML;
    },

    copyCode: function(id) {
        var el = document.getElementById(id);
        if (!el) return;
        var code = el.querySelector('code').textContent;
        navigator.clipboard.writeText(code);
        this.notify('Kod skopiowany!', 'success');
    },

    runCode: function(id) {
        var el = document.getElementById(id);
        if (!el) return;
        var code = el.querySelector('code').textContent;
        this.sendOneToPlugin(code, id);
    },

    extractCode: function(text) {
        var blocks = [];
        var re = /```(\w+)?\n([\s\S]*?)```/g;
        var m;
        while ((m = re.exec(text)) !== null) {
            blocks.push({ lang: m[1] || 'lua', code: m[2].trim() });
        }
        return blocks;
    },

    sendAllToPlugin: function(blocks) {
        var self = this;
        var tasks = [];

        for (var i = 0; i < blocks.length; i++) {
            var code = blocks[i].code;
            var scriptType = 'LocalScript';
            var parent = 'StarterGui';

            var tm = code.match(/--\s*SCRIPT_TYPE:\s*(\w+)/i);
            var pm = code.match(/--\s*PARENT:\s*(\w+)/i);
            if (tm) scriptType = tm[1];
            if (pm) parent = pm[1];

            tasks.push({
                id: 'task_' + Date.now() + '_' + i,
                code: code,
                scriptType: scriptType,
                parent: parent,
                timestamp: Date.now()
            });
        }

        fetch('/.netlify/functions/chat', {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
            body: JSON.stringify({
                action: 'addTasks',
                pluginKey: this.pluginKey,
                tasks: tasks
            })
        })
        .then(function(res) { return res.json(); })
        .then(function(data) {
            if (data.success) {
                self.sentTasks = self.sentTasks.concat(tasks);
                self.updateTaskQueue();
                self.notify(tasks.length + ' skryptow wyslanych do Studio!', 'success');
            }
        })
        .catch(function() {
            self.notify('Blad wysylania - skopiuj kod recznie', 'warn');
        });
    },

    sendOneToPlugin: function(code, btnId) {
        var self = this;
        var scriptType = 'LocalScript';
        var parent = 'StarterGui';

        var tm = code.match(/--\s*SCRIPT_TYPE:\s*(\w+)/i);
        var pm = code.match(/--\s*PARENT:\s*(\w+)/i);
        if (tm) scriptType = tm[1];
        if (pm) parent = pm[1];

        var task = {
            id: 'task_' + Date.now(),
            code: code,
            scriptType: scriptType,
            parent: parent,
            timestamp: Date.now()
        };

        fetch('/.netlify/functions/chat', {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
            body: JSON.stringify({
                action: 'addTasks',
                pluginKey: this.pluginKey,
                tasks: [task]
            })
        })
        .then(function(res) { return res.json(); })
        .then(function(data) {
            if (data.success) {
                var btn = document.getElementById('btn_' + btnId);
                if (btn) {
                    btn.className = 'code-btn sent';
                    btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-check"></i> Wyslano';
                }
                self.sentTasks.push(task);
                self.updateTaskQueue();
                self.notify('Wyslano ' + scriptType + ' do Studio!', 'success');
            }
        })
        .catch(function() {
            self.notify('Blad - skopiuj recznie', 'warn');
        });
    },

    updateTaskQueue: function() {
        var html = '';
        var recent = this.sentTasks.slice(-5);
        for (var i = 0; i < recent.length; i++) {
            var t = recent[i];
            html += '<div class="task-item"><i class="fas fa-circle-check task-done"></i> ' + t.scriptType + ' → ' + t.parent + '</div>';
        }
        if (this.sentTasks.length > 5) {
            html = '<div class="task-item">...i ' + (this.sentTasks.length - 5) + ' wiecej</div>' + html;
        }
        this.dom.taskQueue.innerHTML = html;
    },

    startTaskMonitor: function() {
        var self = this;
        setInterval(function() {
            if (!self.pluginKey) return;
            // Update plugin status indicator
            if (self.sentTasks.length > 0) {
                self.dom.pluginDot.className = 'plugin-status-dot active';
                self.dom.pluginStatusText.textContent = self.sentTasks.length + ' skryptow wyslanych';
            }
        }, 3000);
    },

    autoResize: function() {
        var ta = this.dom.msgInput;
        ta.style.height = 'auto';
        ta.style.height = Math.min(ta.scrollHeight, 140) + 'px';
    },

    scrollDown: function() {
        var chat = this.dom.chat;
        requestAnimationFrame(function() { chat.scrollTop = chat.scrollHeight; });
    },

    clearChat: function() {
        this.messages = [];
        this.msgCount = 0;
        this.codeCount = 0;
        this.insertedCount = 0;
        this.sentTasks = [];
        this.dom.msgCount.textContent = '0';
        this.dom.codeCount.textContent = '0';
        this.dom.insertedCount.textContent = '0';
        this.dom.messages.innerHTML = '';
        this.dom.taskQueue.innerHTML = '';
        this.dom.chatTitle.textContent = 'Nowa Rozmowa';
        this.dom.welcome.style.display = '';
        this.notify('Czat wyczyszczony', 'info');
    },

    exportChat: function() {
        if (!this.messages.length) return this.notify('Brak wiadomosci', 'warn');
        var t = '=== RoboAI Export ===\n\n';
        for (var i = 0; i < this.messages.length; i++) {
            var m = this.messages[i];
            t += (m.role === 'user' ? 'Ty' : 'AI') + ': ' + m.text + '\n\n---\n\n';
        }
        var a = document.createElement('a');
        a.href = URL.createObjectURL(new Blob([t]));
        a.download = 'roboai-' + Date.now() + '.txt';
        a.click();
        this.notify('Wyeksportowano!', 'success');
    },

    notify: function(msg, type) {
        type = type || 'info';
        var icons = { success: 'fa-check-circle', error: 'fa-times-circle', warn: 'fa-exclamation-triangle', info: 'fa-info-circle' };
        var n = document.createElement('div');
        n.className = 'notif ' + type;
        n.innerHTML = '<i class="fas ' + icons[type] + ' notif-icon"></i><span class="notif-text">' + msg + '</span><button class="notif-close" onclick="this.parentElement.remove()"><i class="fas fa-times"></i></button>';
        this.dom.notifs.appendChild(n);
        setTimeout(function() { if (n.parentElement) n.remove(); }, 4500);
    }
};

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() { App.init(); });
📄 netlify/functions/chat.js
JavaScript

const { Redis } = require('@upstash/redis');

let redis = null;
try {
    if (process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_URL) {
        redis = new Redis({
            url: process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_URL,
            token: process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_TOKEN,
        });
    }
} catch (e) {}

async function storeTasks(pluginKey, tasks) {
    const key = 'tasks:' + pluginKey;
    if (redis) {
        let existing = (await redis.get(key)) || [];
        existing = existing.concat(tasks);
        await redis.set(key, existing, { ex: 3600 });
        return true;
    }
    return false;
}

exports.handler = async (event) => {
    const headers = {
        'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*',
        'Access-Control-Allow-Headers': 'Content-Type',
        'Access-Control-Allow-Methods': 'GET, POST, OPTIONS',
        'Content-Type': 'application/json'
    };

    if (event.httpMethod === 'OPTIONS') {
        return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: '' };
    }

    if (event.httpMethod !== 'POST') {
        return { statusCode: 405, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: 'POST only' }) };
    }

    try {
        const body = JSON.parse(event.body);

        // Store multiple tasks at once
        if (body.action === 'addTasks') {
            const ok = await storeTasks(body.pluginKey, body.tasks);
            return {
                statusCode: 200,
                headers,
                body: JSON.stringify({ success: ok, count: body.tasks.length })
            };
        }

        // Legacy single task support
        if (body.action === 'addTask') {
            const ok = await storeTasks(body.pluginKey, [body.task]);
            return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ success: ok }) };
        }

        const { apiKey, messages, model, testMode } = body;

        if (!apiKey) {
            return { statusCode: 400, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: 'Brak klucza API' }) };
        }

        // Test connection
        if (testMode) {
            const test = await fetch('https://api.groq.com/openai/v1/models', {
                headers: { 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + apiKey }
            });
            return {
                statusCode: test.ok ? 200 : 401,
                headers,
                body: JSON.stringify(test.ok
                    ? { success: true }
                    : { error: 'Nieprawidlowy klucz API Groq. Wejdz na https://console.groq.com i stwórz nowy klucz.' })
            };
        }

        // Chat with Groq
        const aiRes = await fetch('https://api.groq.com/openai/v1/chat/completions', {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: {
                'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + apiKey
            },
            body: JSON.stringify({
                model: model || 'llama-3.3-70b-versatile',
                messages: messages,
                max_tokens: 8000,
                temperature: 0.7
            })
        });

        if (!aiRes.ok) {
            const err = await aiRes.json();
            return {
                statusCode: aiRes.status,
                headers,
                body: JSON.stringify({ error: err.error?.message || 'Blad Groq API' })
            };
        }

        const data = await aiRes.json();
        const content = data.choices && data.choices[0] && data.choices[0].message
            ? data.choices[0].message.content
            : 'Brak odpowiedzi';

        return {
            statusCode: 200,
            headers,
            body: JSON.stringify({ content: content })
        };

    } catch (err) {
        return {
            statusCode: 500,
            headers,
            body: JSON.stringify({ error: err.message })
        };
    }
};
📄 netlify/functions/get-task.js
JavaScript

const { Redis } = require('@upstash/redis');

let redis = null;
try {
    if (process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_URL) {
        redis = new Redis({
            url: process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_URL,
            token: process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_TOKEN,
        });
    }
} catch (e) {}

exports.handler = async (event) => {
    const headers = {
        'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*',
        'Access-Control-Allow-Headers': 'Content-Type',
        'Access-Control-Allow-Methods': 'GET, POST, OPTIONS',
        'Content-Type': 'application/json'
    };

    if (event.httpMethod === 'OPTIONS') {
        return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: '' };
    }

    // POST = plugin confirms task done
    if (event.httpMethod === 'POST') {
        return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ success: true }) };
    }

    // GET = plugin fetches tasks
    const pluginKey = event.queryStringParameters && event.queryStringParameters.pluginKey;
    if (!pluginKey) {
        return { statusCode: 400, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: 'pluginKey required' }) };
    }

    try {
        const key = 'tasks:' + pluginKey;
        let tasks = [];

        if (redis) {
            tasks = (await redis.get(key)) || [];
            if (tasks.length > 0) {
                await redis.del(key);
            }
        }

        return {
            statusCode: 200,
            headers,
            body: JSON.stringify({ tasks: tasks })
        };

    } catch (err) {
        return {
            statusCode: 500,
            headers,
            body: JSON.stringify({ error: err.message, tasks: [] })
        };
    }
};

local running = false
local logN = 0
local totalInserted = 0

local function log(msg, col)
    logN = logN + 1
    local l = Instance.new("TextLabel")
    l.Size = UDim2.new(1,0,0,0)
    l.AutomaticSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.Y
    l.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    l.Text = "[" .. os.date("%H:%M:%S") .. "] " .. msg
    l.TextColor3 = col or Color3.fromRGB(138,155,192)
    l.Font = Enum.Font.RobotoMono
    l.TextSize = 10
    l.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
    l.TextWrapped = true
    l.LayoutOrder = logN
    l.Parent = logScroll
    task.defer(function()
        logScroll.CanvasPosition = Vector2.new(0, logScroll.AbsoluteCanvasSize.Y)
    end)
end

local function getParent(name)
    if name == "ServerScriptService" then return game:GetService("ServerScriptService")
    elseif name == "ReplicatedStorage" then return game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
    elseif name == "StarterPlayerScripts" then
        local sp = game:GetService("StarterPlayer"):FindFirstChild("StarterPlayerScripts")
        return sp or game:GetService("StarterGui")
    elseif name == "Workspace" then return workspace
    else return game:GetService("StarterGui")
    end
end

local function runTask(t)
    local ok, err = pcall(function()
        local sType = t.scriptType or "LocalScript"
        local pName = t.parent or "StarterGui"
        local inst
        if sType == "LocalScript" then inst = Instance.new("LocalScript")
        elseif sType == "ModuleScript" then inst = Instance.new("ModuleScript")
        else inst = Instance.new("Script")
        end
        inst.Source = t.code
        inst.Name = "AI_" .. sType .. "_" .. tostring(os.time()) .. "_" .. tostring(math.random(100,999))
        inst.Parent = getParent(pName)
        Sel:Set({inst})
        CHS:SetWaypoint("RoboAI: " .. sType)
        totalInserted = totalInserted + 1
        countLbl.Text = "Wstawionych: " .. totalInserted
        log("Stworzono " .. sType .. " w " .. pName, Color3.fromRGB(16,185,129))
    end)
    if not ok then
        log("BLAD: " .. tostring(err), Color3.fromRGB(239,68,68))
    end
end

local function poll()
    local ok, result = pcall(function()
        local url = SERVER_URL .. "/.netlify/functions/get-task?pluginKey=" .. PLUGIN_KEY
        local resp = Http:GetAsync(url)
        local data = Http:JSONDecode(resp)
        if data.tasks and #data.tasks > 0 then
            log("Otrzymano " .. #data.tasks .. " skryptow!", Color3.fromRGB(96,165,250))
            for _, t in ipairs(data.tasks) do
                runTask(t)
                task.wait(0.2)
            end
        end
    end)
    if not ok then
        -- cichy blad
    end
end

local function start()
    if running then return end
    running = true
    statDot.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(16,185,129)
    statLbl.Text = "Aktywny"
    statLbl.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(16,185,129)
    togBtn.Text = "ZATRZYMAJ"
    togBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(239,68,68)
    log("Uruchomiono!", Color3.fromRGB(16,185,129))
    log("Serwer: " .. SERVER_URL, Color3.fromRGB(96,165,250))
    log("Klucz: " .. string.sub(PLUGIN_KEY, 1, 12) .. "...", Color3.fromRGB(96,165,250))
    log("Sprawdzam co " .. POLL_DELAY .. "s", Color3.fromRGB(138,155,192))
    task.spawn(function()
        while running do
            poll()
            task.wait(POLL_DELAY)
        end
    end)
end

local function stop()
    running = false
    statDot.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(245,158,11)
    statLbl.Text = "Zatrzymany"
    statLbl.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(245,158,11)
    togBtn.Text = "URUCHOM"
    togBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(59,130,246)
    log("Zatrzymano", Color3.fromRGB(245,158,11))
end

togBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
    if running then stop() else start() end
end)

btn.Click:Connect(function()
    widget.Enabled = not widget.Enabled
end)

log("RoboAI Plugin v2 zaladowany", Color3.fromRGB(96,165,250))
log("Kliknij URUCHOM", Color3.fromRGB(138,155,192))

claude-opus-4-6
OK, musimy to naprawić inaczej
Twoje konto Google ma zablokowany darmowy tier. Użyjmy innego darmowego AI.

Użyjemy Groq - 100% za darmo, bez limitu!
Krok 1: Zdobądź klucz Groq
Wejdź na https://console.groq.com
Załóż konto (przez Google najłatwiej)
Po zalogowaniu kliknij "API Keys" po lewej
Kliknij "Create API Key"
Nazwa: roboai
Kliknij "Submit"
Skopiuj klucz (zaczyna się od gsk_...)
Groq jest DARMOWY - 30 zapytań na minutę! ✅

Krok 2: Zmień chat.js
Otwórz netlify/functions/chat.js w Notatniku, usuń wszystko i wklej:

JavaScript

const { Redis } = require('@upstash/redis');

let redis = null;
try {
    if (process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_URL) {
        redis = new Redis({
            url: process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_URL,
            token: process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_TOKEN,
        });
    }
} catch (e) {}

async function storeTask(pluginKey, task) {
    const key = 'tasks:' + pluginKey;
    if (redis) {
        let tasks = (await redis.get(key)) || [];
        tasks.push(task);
        await redis.set(key, tasks, { ex: 3600 });
    }
}

exports.handler = async (event) => {
    const headers = {
        'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*',
        'Access-Control-Allow-Headers': 'Content-Type',
        'Access-Control-Allow-Methods': 'GET, POST, OPTIONS',
        'Content-Type': 'application/json'
    };

    if (event.httpMethod === 'OPTIONS') {
        return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: '' };
    }

    if (event.httpMethod !== 'POST') {
        return { statusCode: 405, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: 'POST only' }) };
    }

    try {
        const body = JSON.parse(event.body);

        if (body.action === 'addTask') {
            await storeTask(body.pluginKey, body.task);
            return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ success: true }) };
        }

        const { apiKey, messages, model, testMode } = body;

        if (!apiKey) {
            return { statusCode: 400, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: 'Brak klucza API' }) };
        }

        if (testMode) {
            const test = await fetch('https://api.groq.com/openai/v1/models', {
                headers: { 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + apiKey }
            });
            return {
                statusCode: test.ok ? 200 : 401,
                headers,
                body: JSON.stringify(test.ok ? { success: true } : { error: 'Nieprawidlowy klucz API. Wejdz na https://console.groq.com i stwórz nowy klucz.' })
            };
        }

        const aiRes = await fetch('https://api.groq.com/openai/v1/chat/completions', {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: {
                'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + apiKey
            },
            body: JSON.stringify({
                model: model || 'llama-3.3-70b-versatile',
                messages: messages,
                max_tokens: 8000,
                temperature: 0.7
            })
        });

        if (!aiRes.ok) {
            const err = await aiRes.json();
            return {
                statusCode: aiRes.status,
                headers,
                body: JSON.stringify({ error: err.error?.message || 'Blad Groq API' })
            };
        }

        const data = await aiRes.json();
        const content = data.choices?.[0]?.message?.content || 'Brak odpowiedzi';

        return {
            statusCode: 200,
            headers,
            body: JSON.stringify({ content: content })
        };

    } catch (err) {
        return {
            statusCode: 500,
            headers,
            body: JSON.stringify({ error: err.message })
        };
    }
};
Zapisz (Ctrl+S)

2. Na stronie

text

Czasem trzeba:

Wejść na https://console.cloud.google.com
Zaakceptować regulamin
Wtedy darmowy tier się odblokuje
Nie musisz podawać karty ani płacić!

text

text

Limity darmowego Gemini
text

Gemini 1.5 Pro:     2 zapytania / minutę (darmowy)

Poczekaj 30 sekund

.notif-close { background:none; border:none; color:var(--text3); cursor:pointer; padding:2px; font-size:.75rem; }
.notif-close:hover { color:var(--text); }

@media(max-width:768px){
    .sidebar { position:fixed; left:0; top:0; bottom:0; transform:translateX(-100%); box-shadow:6px 0 30px rgba(0,0,0,.5); z-index:200; }
    .sidebar.open { transform:translateX(0); }

}

claude-opus-4-6
Problem znaleziony! Brakuje instalacji paczek
Netlify nie zainstalował @upstash/redis. Musimy dodać komendę build. Też musisz usunąć plik complete-task.js którego już nie używamy.

Krok 1: Zmień netlify.toml
Otwórz netlify.toml w Notatniku, usuń wszystko i wklej:

toml

[build]
  command = "npm install"
  functions = "netlify/functions"
  publish = "."

[functions]
  node_bundler = "esbuild"
  external_node_modules = ["@upstash/redis"]

[[headers]]
  for = "/*"
  [headers.values]
    Access-Control-Allow-Origin = "*"
    Access-Control-Allow-Headers = "Content-Type"
    Access-Control-Allow-Methods = "GET, POST, OPTIONS"
Zapisz (Ctrl+S)

Krok 2: Sprawdź package.json
Otwórz package.json w Notatniku, usuń wszystko i wklej:

JSON

{
  "name": "roblox-ai-assistant",
  "version": "1.0.0",
  "dependencies": {
    "@upstash/redis": "^1.28.0"
  }
}
Zapisz (Ctrl+S)

Krok 3: Usuń complete-task.js
Wejdź do folderu netlify → functions
Znajdź plik complete-task.js
Usuń go (prawy klik → Usuń)
Powinny zostać tylko 2 pliki:

text

netlify/functions/
├── chat.js
└── get-task.js
Krok 4: Wypchnij na GitHub
Otwórz CMD:

Bash

git commit -m "fix build"
Bash

Krok 5: Poczekaj i sprawdź

📄 script.js (CAŁY - podmień)
JavaScript

const App = {
    apiKey: localStorage.getItem('roboai_key') || '',
    pluginKey: localStorage.getItem('roboai_pkey') || '',
    messages: [],
    generating: false,
    msgCount: 0,
    codeCount: 0,

    init() {
        if (!this.pluginKey) {
            this.pluginKey = 'rk_' + crypto.randomUUID().replace(/-/g, '');
            localStorage.setItem('roboai_pkey', this.pluginKey);
        }
        this.cacheDom();
        this.bindEvents();
        this.loadKey();
        this.showPluginKey();
    },

    cacheDom() {
        this.dom = {
            sidebar: document.getElementById('sidebar'),
            menuBtn: document.getElementById('menuBtn'),
            statusDot: document.getElementById('statusDot'),
            statusText: document.getElementById('statusText'),
            apiKeyInput: document.getElementById('apiKeyInput'),
            toggleKey: document.getElementById('toggleKey'),
            connectBtn: document.getElementById('connectBtn'),
            pluginKeyDisplay: document.getElementById('pluginKeyDisplay'),
            copyPluginKey: document.getElementById('copyPluginKey'),
            chat: document.getElementById('chat'),
            welcome: document.getElementById('welcome'),
            messages: document.getElementById('messages'),
            typing: document.getElementById('typing'),
            msgInput: document.getElementById('msgInput'),
            sendBtn: document.getElementById('sendBtn'),
            autoInsert: document.getElementById('autoInsert'),
            modelSelect: document.getElementById('modelSelect'),
            chatTitle: document.getElementById('chatTitle'),
            msgCount: document.getElementById('msgCount'),
            codeCount: document.getElementById('codeCount'),
            clearBtn: document.getElementById('clearBtn'),
            exportBtn: document.getElementById('exportBtn'),
            notifs: document.getElementById('notifs'),
        };
    },

    bindEvents() {
        this.dom.menuBtn.addEventListener('click', () => this.dom.sidebar.classList.toggle('open'));
        document.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
            if (window.innerWidth <= 768 && !this.dom.sidebar.contains(e.target) && !this.dom.menuBtn.contains(e.target)) {
                this.dom.sidebar.classList.remove('open');
            }
        });

        this.dom.toggleKey.addEventListener('click', () => {
            const inp = this.dom.apiKeyInput;
            const ico = this.dom.toggleKey.querySelector('i');
            if (inp.type === 'password') { inp.type = 'text'; ico.className = 'fas fa-eye-slash'; }
            else { inp.type = 'password'; ico.className = 'fas fa-eye'; }
        });

        this.dom.connectBtn.addEventListener('click', () => this.connect());

        this.dom.copyPluginKey.addEventListener('click', () => {
            navigator.clipboard.writeText(this.pluginKey);
            this.notify('Klucz skopiowany!', 'success');
        });

        this.dom.sendBtn.addEventListener('click', () => this.send());
        this.dom.msgInput.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
            if (e.key === 'Enter' && !e.shiftKey) { e.preventDefault(); this.send(); }
        });
        this.dom.msgInput.addEventListener('input', () => {
            this.dom.sendBtn.disabled = !this.dom.msgInput.value.trim() || this.generating;
            this.autoResize();
        });

        document.querySelectorAll('.action-btn, .chip').forEach(btn => {
            btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
                const p = btn.dataset.prompt;
                if (p) { this.dom.msgInput.value = p; this.dom.sendBtn.disabled = false; this.send(); }
            });
        });

        this.dom.clearBtn.addEventListener('click', () => this.clearChat());
        this.dom.exportBtn.addEventListener('click', () => this.exportChat());
    },

    loadKey() {
        if (this.apiKey) this.dom.apiKeyInput.value = this.apiKey;
    },

    showPluginKey() {
        this.dom.pluginKeyDisplay.textContent = this.pluginKey;
    },

    async connect() {
        const key = this.dom.apiKeyInput.value.trim();
        if (!key) return this.notify('Wpisz klucz API Gemini!', 'error');

        this.apiKey = key;
        localStorage.setItem('roboai_key', key);
        this.setStatus('connecting', 'Laczenie...');

        try {
            const res = await fetch('/.netlify/functions/chat', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify({ apiKey: key, testMode: true })
            });

            const d = await res.json();

            if (res.ok && d.success) {
                this.setStatus('online', 'Polaczono z Gemini AI');
                this.notify('Polaczono z Gemini AI!', 'success');
            } else {
                throw new Error(d.error || 'Blad polaczenia');
            }
        } catch (err) {
            this.setStatus('offline', 'Blad polaczenia');
            this.notify(err.message, 'error');
        }
    },

    setStatus(state, text) {
        this.dom.statusDot.className = 'status-dot ' + state;
        this.dom.statusText.textContent = text;
    },

    async send() {
        const text = this.dom.msgInput.value.trim();
        if (!text || this.generating) return;
        if (!this.apiKey) return this.notify('Najpierw polacz sie z AI!', 'warn');

        this.dom.welcome.style.display = 'none';
        this.addMsg('user', text);
        this.dom.msgInput.value = '';
        this.dom.sendBtn.disabled = true;
        this.autoResize();

        if (this.messages.length === 1) {
            this.dom.chatTitle.textContent = text.length > 45 ? text.slice(0, 45) + '...' : text;
        }

        this.generating = true;
        this.dom.typing.classList.add('active');
        this.scrollDown();

        try {
            const sysPrompt = this.getSystemPrompt();
            const apiMsgs = [
                { role: 'system', content: sysPrompt },
                ...this.messages.map(m => ({ role: m.role, content: m.text }))
            ];

            const res = await fetch('/.netlify/functions/chat', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify({
                    apiKey: this.apiKey,
                    messages: apiMsgs,
                    model: this.dom.modelSelect.value
                })
            });

            if (!res.ok) {
                const d = await res.json();
                throw new Error(d.error || 'Blad API');
            }

            const data = await res.json();
            this.addMsg('bot', data.content);

            if (this.dom.autoInsert.checked) {
                const blocks = this.extractCode(data.content);
                for (const b of blocks) {
                    await this.sendToPlugin(b);
                }
            }
        } catch (err) {
            this.addMsg('bot', 'Blad: ' + err.message);
            this.notify(err.message, 'error');
        } finally {
            this.generating = false;
            this.dom.typing.classList.remove('active');
            this.dom.sendBtn.disabled = !this.dom.msgInput.value.trim();
        }
    },

    getSystemPrompt() {
        return 'Jestes ekspertem od Roblox Studio i Luau. Generujesz gotowy kod do wklejenia.\n\nZASADY:\n1. Pisz w Luau (Roblox Lua)\n2. Kod musi dzialac natychmiast po wklejeniu\n3. Dla GUI tworz pelne drzewa z Instance.new() - ScreenGui, Frame, TextButton, UICorner, UIStroke, UIGradient, UIListLayout itp.\n4. Dodawaj animacje TweenService\n5. Oznaczaj bloki kodu jako ```lua\n6. Na koncu KAZDEGO skryptu dodaj komentarz:\n   -- SCRIPT_TYPE: LocalScript  (lub Script albo ModuleScript)\n   -- PARENT: StarterGui  (lub ServerScriptService, ReplicatedStorage, StarterPlayerScripts)\n7. Odpowiadaj po polsku\n8. Badz szczegolowy - dodawaj komentarze w kodzie\n9. Tworzac GUI uzywaj ladnych kolorow, gradientow i zaokraglen';
    },

    addMsg(role, text) {
        this.messages.push({ role: role === 'bot' ? 'assistant' : role, text });
        this.msgCount++;
        this.dom.msgCount.textContent = this.msgCount;

        const time = new Date().toLocaleTimeString('pl-PL', { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit' });
        const div = document.createElement('div');
        div.className = 'msg ' + role;

        const icon = role === 'bot' ? 'fa-robot' : 'fa-user';
        const content = role === 'bot' ? this.renderContent(text) : this.esc(text);

        div.innerHTML = '<div class="msg-avatar"><i class="fas ' + icon + '"></i></div><div class="msg-body"><div class="msg-bubble">' + content + '</div><div class="msg-time">' + time + '</div></div>';

        this.dom.messages.appendChild(div);
        this.scrollDown();
    },

    renderContent(text) {
        let html = text;

        html = html.replace(/```(\w+)?\n([\s\S]*?)```/g, function(_, lang, code) {
            App.codeCount++;
            App.dom.codeCount.textContent = App.codeCount;
            const id = 'c' + Date.now() + Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 7);
            return '<div class="code-wrap" id="' + id + '"><div class="code-top"><span class="code-lang"><i class="fas fa-code"></i> ' + (lang || 'lua') + '</span><div class="code-btns"><button class="code-btn" onclick="App.copyCode(\'' + id + '\')"><i class="fas fa-copy"></i> Kopiuj</button><button class="code-btn run" onclick="App.runCode(\'' + id + '\')"><i class="fas fa-play"></i> Wstaw</button></div></div><pre><code>' + App.esc(code.trim()) + '</code></pre></div>';
        });

        html = html.replace(/`([^`]+)`/g, '<code>$1</code>');
        html = html.replace(/\*\*(.*?)\*\*/g, '<strong>$1</strong>');
        html = html.replace(/\n/g, '<br>');
        return html;
    },

    esc(t) {
        const d = document.createElement('div');
        d.textContent = t;
        return d.innerHTML;
    },

    copyCode(id) {
        const el = document.getElementById(id);
        if (!el) return;
        const code = el.querySelector('code').textContent;
        navigator.clipboard.writeText(code);
        this.notify('Kod skopiowany!', 'success');
    },

    async runCode(id) {
        const el = document.getElementById(id);
        if (!el) return;
        const code = el.querySelector('code').textContent;
        await this.sendToPlugin({ code: code, lang: 'lua' });
    },

    extractCode(text) {
        const blocks = [];
        const re = /```(\w+)?\n([\s\S]*?)```/g;
        let m;
        while ((m = re.exec(text)) !== null) {
            blocks.push({ lang: m[1] || 'lua', code: m[2].trim() });
        }
        return blocks;
    },

    async sendToPlugin(block) {
        let scriptType = 'LocalScript';
        let parent = 'StarterGui';

        const tm = block.code.match(/--\s*SCRIPT_TYPE:\s*(\w+)/i);
        const pm = block.code.match(/--\s*PARENT:\s*(\w+)/i);
        if (tm) scriptType = tm[1];
        if (pm) parent = pm[1];

        try {
            const res = await fetch('/.netlify/functions/chat', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify({
                    action: 'addTask',
                    pluginKey: this.pluginKey,
                    task: {
                        id: crypto.randomUUID(),
                        code: block.code,
                        scriptType: scriptType,
                        parent: parent,
                        timestamp: Date.now()
                    }
                })
            });
            if (res.ok) this.notify('Wyslano do Studio (' + scriptType + ')', 'info');
        } catch (e) {
            this.notify('Nie wyslano - skopiuj recznie', 'warn');
        }
    },

    autoResize() {
        const ta = this.dom.msgInput;
        ta.style.height = 'auto';
        ta.style.height = Math.min(ta.scrollHeight, 140) + 'px';
    },

    scrollDown() {
        requestAnimationFrame(function() { App.dom.chat.scrollTop = App.dom.chat.scrollHeight; });
    },

    clearChat() {
        this.messages = [];
        this.msgCount = 0;
        this.codeCount = 0;
        this.dom.msgCount.textContent = '0';
        this.dom.codeCount.textContent = '0';
        this.dom.messages.innerHTML = '';
        this.dom.chatTitle.textContent = 'Nowa Rozmowa';
        this.dom.welcome.style.display = '';
        this.notify('Czat wyczyszczony', 'info');
    },

    exportChat() {
        if (!this.messages.length) return this.notify('Brak wiadomosci', 'warn');
        let t = '=== RoboAI Export ===\n\n';
        this.messages.forEach(function(m) {
            t += (m.role === 'user' ? 'Ty' : 'AI') + ': ' + m.text + '\n\n---\n\n';
        });
        const a = document.createElement('a');
        a.href = URL.createObjectURL(new Blob([t]));
        a.download = 'roboai-' + Date.now() + '.txt';
        a.click();
        this.notify('Wyeksportowano!', 'success');
    },

    notify(msg, type) {
        type = type || 'info';
        const icons = { success: 'fa-check-circle', error: 'fa-times-circle', warn: 'fa-exclamation-triangle', info: 'fa-info-circle' };
        const n = document.createElement('div');
        n.className = 'notif ' + type;
        n.innerHTML = '<i class="fas ' + icons[type] + ' notif-icon"></i><span class="notif-text">' + msg + '</span><button class="notif-close" onclick="this.parentElement.remove()"><i class="fas fa-times"></i></button>';
        this.dom.notifs.appendChild(n);
        setTimeout(function() { if (n.parentElement) n.remove(); }, 4500);
    }
};

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() { App.init(); });

JavaScript

const { Redis } = require('@upstash/redis');

let redis = null;
try {
    if (process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_URL) {
        redis = new Redis({
            url: process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_URL,
            token: process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_TOKEN,
        });
    }
} catch (e) {}

async function storeTask(pluginKey, task) {
    const key = 'tasks:' + pluginKey;
    if (redis) {
        let tasks = (await redis.get(key)) || [];
        tasks.push(task);
        await redis.set(key, tasks, { ex: 3600 });
    }
}

exports.handler = async (event) => {
    const headers = {
        'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*',
        'Access-Control-Allow-Headers': 'Content-Type',
        'Access-Control-Allow-Methods': 'GET, POST, OPTIONS',
        'Content-Type': 'application/json'
    };

    if (event.httpMethod === 'OPTIONS') {
        return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: '' };
    }

    if (event.httpMethod !== 'POST') {
        return { statusCode: 405, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: 'POST only' }) };
    }

    try {
        const body = JSON.parse(event.body);

        if (body.action === 'addTask') {
            await storeTask(body.pluginKey, body.task);
            return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ success: true }) };
        }

        const { apiKey, messages, model, testMode } = body;

        if (!apiKey) {
            return { statusCode: 400, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: 'Brak klucza API' }) };
        }

        if (testMode) {
            const test = await fetch(
                'https://generativelanguage.googleapis.com/v1beta/models?key=' + apiKey
            );
            return {
                statusCode: test.ok ? 200 : 401,
                headers,
                body: JSON.stringify(test.ok ? { success: true } : { error: 'Nieprawidlowy klucz API Gemini. Wejdz na https://aistudio.google.com/apikey i stwórz nowy klucz.' })
            };
        }

        const systemMsg = messages.find(m => m.role === 'system');
        const chatMsgs = messages.filter(m => m.role !== 'system');

        const geminiContents = chatMsgs.map(m => ({
            role: m.role === 'assistant' ? 'model' : 'user',
            parts: [{ text: m.content }]
        }));

        const geminiBody = {
            contents: geminiContents,
            generationConfig: {
                temperature: 0.7,
                maxOutputTokens: 8192,
            }
        };

        if (systemMsg) {
            geminiBody.systemInstruction = {
                parts: [{ text: systemMsg.content }]
            };
        }

        const selectedModel = model || 'gemini-2.0-flash';

        const aiRes = await fetch(
            'https://generativelanguage.googleapis.com/v1beta/models/' + selectedModel + ':generateContent?key=' + apiKey,
            {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify(geminiBody)
            }
        );

        if (!aiRes.ok) {
            const err = await aiRes.json();
            return {
                statusCode: aiRes.status,
                headers,
                body: JSON.stringify({ error: err.error?.message || 'Blad Gemini API' })
            };
        }

        const data = await aiRes.json();
        const content = data.candidates?.[0]?.content?.parts?.[0]?.text || 'Brak odpowiedzi';

        return {
            statusCode: 200,
            headers,
            body: JSON.stringify({ content: content })
        };

    } catch (err) {
        return {
            statusCode: 500,
            headers,
            body: JSON.stringify({ error: err.message })
        };
    }
};
📄 netlify/functions/get-task.js (CAŁY - podmień)
JavaScript

const { Redis } = require('@upstash/redis');

let redis = null;
try {
    if (process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_URL) {
        redis = new Redis({
            url: process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_URL,
            token: process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_TOKEN,
        });
    }
} catch (e) {}

exports.handler = async (event) => {
    const headers = {
        'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*',
        'Access-Control-Allow-Headers': 'Content-Type',
        'Access-Control-Allow-Methods': 'GET, POST, OPTIONS',
        'Content-Type': 'application/json'
    };

    if (event.httpMethod === 'OPTIONS') {
        return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: '' };
    }

    if (event.httpMethod === 'POST') {
        return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ success: true }) };
    }

    const pluginKey = event.queryStringParameters?.pluginKey;
    if (!pluginKey) {
        return { statusCode: 400, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: 'pluginKey required' }) };
    }

    try {
        const key = 'tasks:' + pluginKey;
        let tasks = [];

        if (redis) {
            tasks = (await redis.get(key)) || [];
            if (tasks.length > 0) await redis.del(key);
        }

        return {
            statusCode: 200,
            headers,
            body: JSON.stringify({ tasks: tasks })
        };

    } catch (err) {
        return {
            statusCode: 500,
            headers,
            body: JSON.stringify({ error: err.message })
        };
    }
};

Plugin Roblox Studio - PRAWIDŁOWY SPOSÓB
Problem z poprzednim pluginem: zapisałeś go źle. Oto jak to zrobić prawidłowo:

Krok 1: Znajdź folder pluginów
Naciśnij Win+R na klawiaturze
Wpisz to i kliknij OK:
text

%LOCALAPPDATA%\Roblox\Plugins
Otworzy się folder - to tutaj zapisujesz plugin
Krok 2: Stwórz plik pluginu
W tym folderze kliknij prawym → Nowy → Dokument tekstowy
Nazwij go: RoboAI.lua
⚠️ WAŻNE: Rozszerzenie musi być .lua a NIE .lua.txt!
Jeśli nie widzisz rozszerzeń plików:

W Eksploratorze kliknij Widok → zaznacz Rozszerzenia nazw plików
Potem zmień nazwę z RoboAI.lua.txt na RoboAI.lua
Krok 3: Wklej kod pluginu
Otwórz RoboAI.lua w Notatniku i wklej:

Lua

--[[
    RoboAI Studio Plugin
    
    PRZED URUCHOMIENIEM:
    1. Zmien SERVER_URL na adres twojej strony
    2. Zmien PLUGIN_KEY na klucz ze strony
    3. Wlacz HttpService: Game Settings > Security > Allow HTTP Requests > ON
--]]

-- ZMIEN TE 2 LINIJKI:
local SERVER_URL = "https://fleetyai.netlify.app"
local PLUGIN_KEY = "TUTAJ_WKLEJ_KLUCZ_ZE_STRONY"

local POLL_DELAY = 3

local HttpService = game:GetService("HttpService")
local Selection = game:GetService("Selection")
local ChangeHistoryService = game:GetService("ChangeHistoryService")

local toolbar = plugin:CreateToolbar("RoboAI Studio")
local mainButton = toolbar:CreateButton("RoboAI", "AI Assistant", "rbxassetid://4458901886")

local widgetInfo = DockWidgetPluginGuiInfo.new(
    Enum.InitialDockState.Right,
    false, false,
    320, 500, 280, 350
)
local widget = plugin:CreateDockWidgetPluginGui("RoboAIWidget", widgetInfo)
widget.Title = "RoboAI Studio"

-- LOGIKA
local isRunning = false
local logCount = 0

local function addLog(msg, color)
    logCount = logCount + 1
    local lbl = Instance.new("TextLabel")
    lbl.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 0)
    lbl.AutomaticSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.Y
    lbl.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    lbl.Text = "[" .. os.date("%H:%M:%S") .. "] " .. msg
    lbl.TextColor3 = color or Color3.fromRGB(138, 155, 192)
    lbl.Font = Enum.Font.RobotoMono
    lbl.TextSize = 10
    lbl.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
    lbl.TextWrapped = true
    lbl.LayoutOrder = logCount
    lbl.Parent = logScroll

    task.defer(function()
        logScroll.CanvasPosition = Vector2.new(0, logScroll.AbsoluteCanvasSize.Y)
    end)
end

local function getParent(name)
    if name == "ServerScriptService" then
        return game:GetService("ServerScriptService")
    elseif name == "ReplicatedStorage" then
        return game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
    elseif name == "StarterPlayerScripts" then
        return game:GetService("StarterPlayer"):FindFirstChild("StarterPlayerScripts")
    elseif name == "Workspace" then
        return workspace
    else
        return game:GetService("StarterGui")
    end
end

local function runTask(taskData)
    addLog("Otrzymano zadanie: " .. (taskData.scriptType or "Script"), Color3.fromRGB(96, 165, 250))

    local ok, err = pcall(function()
        local sType = taskData.scriptType or "LocalScript"
        local inst

        if sType == "LocalScript" then
            inst = Instance.new("LocalScript")
        elseif sType == "ModuleScript" then
            inst = Instance.new("ModuleScript")
        else
            inst = Instance.new("Script")
        end

        inst.Source = taskData.code
        inst.Name = "AI_" .. sType .. "_" .. tostring(os.time())
        inst.Parent = getParent(taskData.parent or "StarterGui")

        Selection:Set({inst})
        ChangeHistoryService:SetWaypoint("RoboAI: " .. sType)

        addLog("Stworzono " .. sType .. " w " .. (taskData.parent or "StarterGui"), Color3.fromRGB(16, 185, 129))
    end)

    if not ok then
        addLog("BLAD: " .. tostring(err), Color3.fromRGB(239, 68, 68))
    end

    pcall(function()
        HttpService:PostAsync(
            SERVER_URL .. "/.netlify/functions/get-task",
            HttpService:JSONEncode({
                pluginKey = PLUGIN_KEY,
                taskId = taskData.id,
                completed = true
            }),
            Enum.HttpContentType.ApplicationJson
        )
    end)
end

local function poll()
    local ok, result = pcall(function()
        local url = SERVER_URL .. "/.netlify/functions/get-task?pluginKey=" .. PLUGIN_KEY
        local response = HttpService:GetAsync(url)
        local data = HttpService:JSONDecode(response)

        if data.tasks and #data.tasks > 0 then
            addLog("Otrzymano " .. #data.tasks .. " zadan!", Color3.fromRGB(96, 165, 250))
            for _, taskData in ipairs(data.tasks) do
                runTask(taskData)
            end
        end
    end)

    if not ok then
        -- cichy blad
    end
end

local function startPlugin()
    if isRunning then return end
    isRunning = true

    statusDot.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(16, 185, 129)
    statusLabel.Text = "Aktywny - nasluchuje..."
    statusLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(16, 185, 129)
    toggleBtn.Text = "ZATRZYMAJ"
    toggleBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(239, 68, 68)

    addLog("Plugin uruchomiony!", Color3.fromRGB(16, 185, 129))
    addLog("Serwer: " .. SERVER_URL, Color3.fromRGB(96, 165, 250))
    addLog("Sprawdzam co " .. POLL_DELAY .. " sekund...", Color3.fromRGB(138, 155, 192))

    task.spawn(function()
        while isRunning do
            poll()
            task.wait(POLL_DELAY)
        end
    end)
end

local function stopPlugin()
    isRunning = false

    statusDot.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(245, 158, 11)
    statusLabel.Text = "Zatrzymany"
    statusLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(245, 158, 11)
    toggleBtn.Text = "URUCHOM"
    toggleBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(59, 130, 246)

    addLog("Plugin zatrzymany", Color3.fromRGB(245, 158, 11))
end

toggleBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
    if isRunning then
        stopPlugin()
    else
        startPlugin()
    end
end)

mainButton.Click:Connect(function()
    widget.Enabled = not widget.Enabled
end)

addLog("RoboAI Plugin zaladowany", Color3.fromRGB(96, 165, 250))
addLog("Kliknij URUCHOM aby polaczyc", Color3.fromRGB(138, 155, 192))
