</div><!-- Settings Modal --><div class="modal-overlay" id="settingsModal"> <div class="modal"> <div class="modal-header"> <h3><i class="fas fa-gear"></i> Ustawienia</h3> <button class="modal-close" id="closeSettings"> <i class="fas fa-times"></i> </button> </div> <div class="modal-body"> <div class="settings-group"> <h4>Generowanie Kodu</h4> <div class="setting-item"> <label>Styl kodu</label> <select id="codeStyle"> <option value="detailed">Szczegółowy (z komentarzami)</option> <option value="compact">Kompaktowy</option> <option value="educational">Edukacyjny (z wyjaśnieniami)</option> </select> </div> <div class="setting-item"> <label>Domyślny typ skryptu</label> <select id="scriptType"> <option value="auto">Automatyczny</option> <option value="server">Server Script</option> <option value="local">Local Script</option> <option value="module">Module Script</option> </select> </div> </div> <div class="settings-group"> <h4>Plugin</h4> <div class="setting-item"> <label>Twój klucz API pluginu</label> <div class="plugin-key-display"> <code id="pluginKeyDisplay">Nie wygenerowano</code> <button class="btn-small" id="generatePluginKey"> <i class="fas fa-refresh"></i> Generuj </button> </div> </div> <div class="setting-item"> <label>URL serwera</label> <code class="server-url" id="serverUrl">https://twoja-strona.netlify.app</code> </div> </div> </div> </div> </div><!-- Notification Container --><div class="notification-container" id="notificationContainer"></div><script src="script.js"></script></body> </html> , napisz mi teraz jak to połączyć z pluginem w roblox bo tamten plugin nie działa wogóle nic się nie wyswietla w roblox studio

Problem jest w stronie - ona sprawdza czy klucz zaczyna się od sk- (OpenAI). Musimy to naprawić.

KROK 1: Napraw script.js
Otwórz folder projektu na pulpicie
Otwórz script.js w Notatniku
Znajdź tę linię (użyj Ctrl+H żeby znaleźć):
Znajdź tekst:

text

<i class="fas fa-key"></i> OpenAI API Key
Zamień na:

text

<i class="fas fa-key"></i> Gemini API Key
Ale to za mało. Łatwiej będzie podmienić cały script.js.

Otwórz script.js
Usuń wszystko
Wklej to:
JavaScript

const App = {
    apiKey: localStorage.getItem('roboai_key') || '',
    pluginKey: localStorage.getItem('roboai_pkey') || '',
    messages: [],
    generating: false,
    msgCount: 0,
    codeCount: 0,

    init() {
        if (!this.pluginKey) {
            this.pluginKey = 'rk_' + crypto.randomUUID().replace(/-/g, '');
            localStorage.setItem('roboai_pkey', this.pluginKey);
        }
        this.cacheDom();
        this.bindEvents();
        this.loadKey();
        this.showPluginKey();
    },

    cacheDom() {
        this.dom = {
            sidebar: document.getElementById('sidebar'),
            menuBtn: document.getElementById('menuBtn'),
            statusDot: document.getElementById('statusDot'),
            statusText: document.getElementById('statusText'),
            apiKeyInput: document.getElementById('apiKeyInput'),
            toggleKey: document.getElementById('toggleKey'),
            connectBtn: document.getElementById('connectBtn'),
            pluginKeyDisplay: document.getElementById('pluginKeyDisplay'),
            copyPluginKey: document.getElementById('copyPluginKey'),
            chat: document.getElementById('chat'),
            welcome: document.getElementById('welcome'),
            messages: document.getElementById('messages'),
            typing: document.getElementById('typing'),
            msgInput: document.getElementById('msgInput'),
            sendBtn: document.getElementById('sendBtn'),
            autoInsert: document.getElementById('autoInsert'),
            modelSelect: document.getElementById('modelSelect'),
            chatTitle: document.getElementById('chatTitle'),
            msgCount: document.getElementById('msgCount'),
            codeCount: document.getElementById('codeCount'),
            clearBtn: document.getElementById('clearBtn'),
            exportBtn: document.getElementById('exportBtn'),
            notifs: document.getElementById('notifs'),
        };
    },

    bindEvents() {
        this.dom.menuBtn.addEventListener('click', () => this.dom.sidebar.classList.toggle('open'));
        document.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
            if (window.innerWidth <= 768 && !this.dom.sidebar.contains(e.target) && !this.dom.menuBtn.contains(e.target)) {
                this.dom.sidebar.classList.remove('open');
            }
        });

        this.dom.toggleKey.addEventListener('click', () => {
            const inp = this.dom.apiKeyInput;
            const ico = this.dom.toggleKey.querySelector('i');
            if (inp.type === 'password') { inp.type = 'text'; ico.className = 'fas fa-eye-slash'; }
            else { inp.type = 'password'; ico.className = 'fas fa-eye'; }
        });

        this.dom.connectBtn.addEventListener('click', () => this.connect());

        this.dom.copyPluginKey.addEventListener('click', () => {
            navigator.clipboard.writeText(this.pluginKey);
            this.notify('Klucz skopiowany!', 'success');
        });

        this.dom.sendBtn.addEventListener('click', () => this.send());
        this.dom.msgInput.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
            if (e.key === 'Enter' && !e.shiftKey) { e.preventDefault(); this.send(); }
        });
        this.dom.msgInput.addEventListener('input', () => {
            this.dom.sendBtn.disabled = !this.dom.msgInput.value.trim() || this.generating;
            this.autoResize();
        });

        document.querySelectorAll('.action-btn, .chip').forEach(btn => {
            btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
                const p = btn.dataset.prompt;
                if (p) { this.dom.msgInput.value = p; this.dom.sendBtn.disabled = false; this.send(); }
            });
        });

        this.dom.clearBtn.addEventListener('click', () => this.clearChat());
        this.dom.exportBtn.addEventListener('click', () => this.exportChat());
    },

    loadKey() {
        if (this.apiKey) this.dom.apiKeyInput.value = this.apiKey;
    },

    showPluginKey() {
        this.dom.pluginKeyDisplay.textContent = this.pluginKey;
    },

    async connect() {
        const key = this.dom.apiKeyInput.value.trim();
        if (!key) return this.notify('Wpisz klucz API Gemini!', 'error');

        this.apiKey = key;
        localStorage.setItem('roboai_key', key);
        this.setStatus('connecting', 'Laczenie...');

        try {
            const res = await fetch('/.netlify/functions/chat', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify({ apiKey: key, testMode: true })
            });

            const d = await res.json();

            if (res.ok && d.success) {
                this.setStatus('online', 'Polaczono z Gemini AI');
                this.notify('Polaczono z Gemini AI! 🎉', 'success');
            } else {
                throw new Error(d.error || 'Blad polaczenia');
            }
        } catch (err) {
            this.setStatus('offline', 'Blad polaczenia');
            this.notify(err.message, 'error');
        }
    },

    setStatus(state, text) {
        this.dom.statusDot.className = `status-dot ${state}`;
        this.dom.statusText.textContent = text;
    },

    async send() {
        const text = this.dom.msgInput.value.trim();
        if (!text || this.generating) return;
        if (!this.apiKey) return this.notify('Najpierw polacz sie z AI!', 'warn');

        this.dom.welcome.style.display = 'none';

        this.addMsg('user', text);
        this.dom.msgInput.value = '';
        this.dom.sendBtn.disabled = true;
        this.autoResize();

        if (this.messages.length === 1) {
            this.dom.chatTitle.textContent = text.length > 45 ? text.slice(0, 45) + '...' : text;
        }

        this.generating = true;
        this.dom.typing.classList.add('active');
        this.scrollDown();

        try {
            const sysPrompt = this.getSystemPrompt();
            const apiMsgs = [
                { role: 'system', content: sysPrompt },
                ...this.messages.map(m => ({ role: m.role, content: m.text }))
            ];

            const res = await fetch('/.netlify/functions/chat', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify({
                    apiKey: this.apiKey,
                    messages: apiMsgs,
                    model: this.dom.modelSelect.value
                })
            });

            if (!res.ok) {
                const d = await res.json();
                throw new Error(d.error || 'Blad API');
            }

            const data = await res.json();
            this.addMsg('bot', data.content);

            if (this.dom.autoInsert.checked) {
                const blocks = this.extractCode(data.content);
                for (const b of blocks) {
                    await this.sendToPlugin(b);
                }
            }
        } catch (err) {
            this.addMsg('bot', '❌ Blad: ' + err.message);
            this.notify(err.message, 'error');
        } finally {
            this.generating = false;
            this.dom.typing.classList.remove('active');
            this.dom.sendBtn.disabled = !this.dom.msgInput.value.trim();
        }
    },

    getSystemPrompt() {
        return `Jestes ekspertem od Roblox Studio i Luau. Generujesz gotowy kod do wklejenia.

ZASADY:
1. Pisz w Luau (Roblox Lua)
2. Kod musi dzialac natychmiast po wklejeniu
3. Dla GUI tworz pelne drzewa z Instance.new() - ScreenGui, Frame, TextButton, UICorner, UIStroke, UIGradient, UIListLayout itp.
4. Dodawaj animacje TweenService
5. Oznaczaj bloki kodu jako \`\`\`lua
6. Na koncu KAZDEGO skryptu dodaj komentarz:
   -- SCRIPT_TYPE: LocalScript  (lub Script albo ModuleScript)
   -- PARENT: StarterGui  (lub ServerScriptService, ReplicatedStorage, StarterPlayerScripts)
7. Odpowiadaj po polsku
8. Badz szczegolowy - dodawaj komentarze w kodzie
9. Tworzac GUI uzywaj ladnych kolorow, gradientow i zaokraglen`;
    },

    addMsg(role, text) {
        this.messages.push({ role: role === 'bot' ? 'assistant' : role, text });
        this.msgCount++;
        this.dom.msgCount.textContent = this.msgCount;

        const time = new Date().toLocaleTimeString('pl-PL', { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit' });
        const div = document.createElement('div');
        div.className = `msg ${role}`;

        const icon = role === 'bot' ? 'fa-robot' : 'fa-user';
        const content = role === 'bot' ? this.renderContent(text) : this.esc(text);

        div.innerHTML = `
            <div class="msg-avatar"><i class="fas ${icon}"></i></div>
            <div class="msg-body">
                <div class="msg-bubble">${content}</div>
                <div class="msg-time">${time}</div>
            </div>`;

        this.dom.messages.appendChild(div);
        this.scrollDown();
    },

    renderContent(text) {
        let html = text;

        html = html.replace(/```(\w+)?\n([\s\S]*?)```/g, (_, lang, code) => {
            this.codeCount++;
            this.dom.codeCount.textContent = this.codeCount;
            const id = 'c' + Date.now() + Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 7);
            return `<div class="code-wrap" id="${id}">
                <div class="code-top">
                    <span class="code-lang"><i class="fas fa-code"></i> ${lang || 'lua'}</span>
                    <div class="code-btns">
                        <button class="code-btn" onclick="App.copyCode('${id}')"><i class="fas fa-copy"></i> Kopiuj</button>
                        <button class="code-btn run" onclick="App.runCode('${id}')"><i class="fas fa-play"></i> Wstaw</button>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <pre><code>${this.esc(code.trim())}</code></pre>
            </div>`;
        });

        html = html.replace(/`([^`]+)`/g, '<code>$1</code>');
        html = html.replace(/\*\*(.*?)\*\*/g, '<strong>$1</strong>');
        html = html.replace(/\n/g, '<br>');
        return html;
    },

    esc(t) {
        const d = document.createElement('div');
        d.textContent = t;
        return d.innerHTML;
    },

    copyCode(id) {
        const code = document.getElementById(id)?.querySelector('code')?.textContent;
        if (code) { navigator.clipboard.writeText(code); this.notify('Kod skopiowany!', 'success'); }
    },

    async runCode(id) {
        const code = document.getElementById(id)?.querySelector('code')?.textContent;
        if (code) await this.sendToPlugin({ code, lang: 'lua' });
    },

    extractCode(text) {
        const blocks = [];
        const re = /```(\w+)?\n([\s\S]*?)```/g;
        let m;
        while ((m = re.exec(text)) !== null) {
            blocks.push({ lang: m[1] || 'lua', code: m[2].trim() });
        }
        return blocks;
    },

    async sendToPlugin(block) {
        let scriptType = 'LocalScript';
        let parent = 'StarterGui';

        const tm = block.code.match(/--\s*SCRIPT_TYPE:\s*(\w+)/i);
        const pm = block.code.match(/--\s*PARENT:\s*(\w+)/i);
        if (tm) scriptType = tm[1];
        if (pm) parent = pm[1];

        try {
            const res = await fetch('/.netlify/functions/chat', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify({
                    action: 'addTask',
                    pluginKey: this.pluginKey,
                    task: {
                        id: crypto.randomUUID(),
                        code: block.code,
                        scriptType,
                        parent,
                        timestamp: Date.now()
                    }
                })
            });
            if (res.ok) this.notify('📤 Wyslano do Studio (' + scriptType + ')', 'info');
        } catch {
            this.notify('Nie wyslano do plugin - skopiuj recznie', 'warn');
        }
    },

    autoResize() {
        const ta = this.dom.msgInput;
        ta.style.height = 'auto';
        ta.style.height = Math.min(ta.scrollHeight, 140) + 'px';
    },

    scrollDown() {
        requestAnimationFrame(() => { this.dom.chat.scrollTop = this.dom.chat.scrollHeight; });
    },

    clearChat() {
        this.messages = [];
        this.msgCount = 0;
        this.codeCount = 0;
        this.dom.msgCount.textContent = '0';
        this.dom.codeCount.textContent = '0';
        this.dom.messages.innerHTML = '';
        this.dom.chatTitle.textContent = 'Nowa Rozmowa';
        this.dom.welcome.style.display = '';
        this.notify('Czat wyczyszczony', 'info');
    },

    exportChat() {
        if (!this.messages.length) return this.notify('Brak wiadomosci', 'warn');
        let t = '=== RoboAI Export ===\n\n';
        this.messages.forEach(m => {
            t += `${m.role === 'user' ? '👤' : '🤖'}: ${m.text}\n\n---\n\n`;
        });
        const a = document.createElement('a');
        a.href = URL.createObjectURL(new Blob([t]));
        a.download = `roboai-${Date.now()}.txt`;
        a.click();
        this.notify('Wyeksportowano!', 'success');
    },

    notify(msg, type = 'info') {
        const icons = { success: 'fa-check-circle', error: 'fa-times-circle', warn: 'fa-exclamation-triangle', info: 'fa-info-circle' };
        const n = document.createElement('div');
        n.className = `notif ${type}`;
        n.innerHTML = `
            <i class="fas ${icons[type]} notif-icon"></i>
            <span class="notif-text">${msg}</span>
            <button class="notif-close" onclick="this.parentElement.remove()"><i class="fas fa-times"></i></button>`;
        this.dom.notifs.appendChild(n);
        setTimeout(() => { if (n.parentElement) n.remove(); }, 4500);
    }
};

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => App.init());

JavaScript

const { Redis } = require('@upstash/redis');

let redis = null;
try {
    if (process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_URL) {
        redis = new Redis({
            url: process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_URL,
            token: process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_TOKEN,
        });
    }
} catch (e) {}

const memStore = {};

async function storeTask(pluginKey, task) {
    const key = `tasks:${pluginKey}`;
    if (redis) {
        let tasks = (await redis.get(key)) || [];
        tasks.push(task);
        await redis.set(key, tasks, { ex: 3600 });
    } else {
        if (!memStore[key]) memStore[key] = [];
        memStore[key].push(task);
    }
}

exports.handler = async (event) => {
    const headers = {
        'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*',
        'Access-Control-Allow-Headers': 'Content-Type',
        'Access-Control-Allow-Methods': 'GET, POST, OPTIONS',
        'Content-Type': 'application/json'
    };

    if (event.httpMethod === 'OPTIONS') {
        return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: '' };
    }

    if (event.httpMethod !== 'POST') {
        return { statusCode: 405, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: 'POST only' }) };
    }

    try {
        const body = JSON.parse(event.body);

        // Task storage for plugin
        if (body.action === 'addTask') {
            await storeTask(body.pluginKey, body.task);
            return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ success: true }) };
        }

        const { apiKey, messages, model, testMode } = body;

        if (!apiKey) {
            return { statusCode: 400, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: 'Brak klucza API' }) };
        }

        // Test connection
        if (testMode) {
            const test = await fetch(
                `https://generativelanguage.googleapis.com/v1beta/models?key=${apiKey}`
            );
            return {
                statusCode: test.ok ? 200 : 401,
                headers,
                body: JSON.stringify(test.ok ? { success: true } : { error: 'Nieprawidlowy klucz API Gemini' })
            };
        }

        // Build Gemini messages
        const systemMsg = messages.find(m => m.role === 'system');
        const chatMsgs = messages.filter(m => m.role !== 'system');

        const geminiContents = chatMsgs.map(m => ({
            role: m.role === 'assistant' ? 'model' : 'user',
            parts: [{ text: m.content }]
        }));

        const geminiBody = {
            contents: geminiContents,
            generationConfig: {
                temperature: 0.7,
                maxOutputTokens: 8192,
            }
        };

        // Add system instruction
        if (systemMsg) {
            geminiBody.systemInstruction = {
                parts: [{ text: systemMsg.content }]
            };
        }

        // Call Gemini API
        const aiRes = await fetch(
            `https://generativelanguage.googleapis.com/v1beta/models/gemini-2.0-flash:generateContent?key=${apiKey}`,
            {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify(geminiBody)
            }
        );

        if (!aiRes.ok) {
            const err = await aiRes.json();
            return {
                statusCode: aiRes.status,
                headers,
                body: JSON.stringify({ error: err.error?.message || 'Blad Gemini API' })
            };
        }

        const data = await aiRes.json();
        const content = data.candidates?.[0]?.content?.parts?.[0]?.text || 'Brak odpowiedzi';

        return {
            statusCode: 200,
            headers,
            body: JSON.stringify({ content })
        };

    } catch (err) {
        return {
            statusCode: 500,
            headers,
            body: JSON.stringify({ error: err.message })
        };
    }
};

Kompletna Instrukcja Krok po Kroku
KROK 1: Stwórz Folder na Komputerze
Otwórz Eksplorator plików i stwórz taki folder gdziekolwiek na dysku (np. na Pulpicie):

text

roblox-ai-assistant/
Wewnątrz stwórz taką strukturę folderów:

text

roblox-ai-assistant/
├── index.html
├── style.css
├── script.js
├── package.json
├── netlify.toml
└── netlify/
    └── functions/
        ├── chat.js
        └── get-task.js
KROK 2: Stwórz Każdy Plik

📄 script.js
JavaScript

// ============================================
// ROBOAI STUDIO - MAIN APP
// ============================================

const App = {
    // State
    apiKey: localStorage.getItem('roboai_key') || '',
    pluginKey: localStorage.getItem('roboai_pkey') || '',
    messages: [],
    generating: false,
    msgCount: 0,
    codeCount: 0,

    // Init
    init() {
        if (!this.pluginKey) {
            this.pluginKey = 'rk_' + crypto.randomUUID().replace(/-/g, '');
            localStorage.setItem('roboai_pkey', this.pluginKey);
        }

        this.cacheDom();
        this.bindEvents();
        this.loadKey();
        this.showPluginKey();
    },

    cacheDom() {
        this.dom = {
            sidebar: document.getElementById('sidebar'),
            menuBtn: document.getElementById('menuBtn'),
            statusDot: document.getElementById('statusDot'),
            statusText: document.getElementById('statusText'),
            apiKeyInput: document.getElementById('apiKeyInput'),
            toggleKey: document.getElementById('toggleKey'),
            connectBtn: document.getElementById('connectBtn'),
            pluginKeyDisplay: document.getElementById('pluginKeyDisplay'),
            copyPluginKey: document.getElementById('copyPluginKey'),
            chat: document.getElementById('chat'),
            welcome: document.getElementById('welcome'),
            messages: document.getElementById('messages'),
            typing: document.getElementById('typing'),
            msgInput: document.getElementById('msgInput'),
            sendBtn: document.getElementById('sendBtn'),
            autoInsert: document.getElementById('autoInsert'),
            modelSelect: document.getElementById('modelSelect'),
            chatTitle: document.getElementById('chatTitle'),
            msgCount: document.getElementById('msgCount'),
            codeCount: document.getElementById('codeCount'),
            clearBtn: document.getElementById('clearBtn'),
            exportBtn: document.getElementById('exportBtn'),
            notifs: document.getElementById('notifs'),
        };
    },

    bindEvents() {
        // Sidebar mobile
        this.dom.menuBtn.addEventListener('click', () => this.dom.sidebar.classList.toggle('open'));
        document.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
            if (window.innerWidth <= 768 && !this.dom.sidebar.contains(e.target) && !this.dom.menuBtn.contains(e.target)) {
                this.dom.sidebar.classList.remove('open');
            }
        });

        // API Key toggle visibility
        this.dom.toggleKey.addEventListener('click', () => {
            const inp = this.dom.apiKeyInput;
            const ico = this.dom.toggleKey.querySelector('i');
            if (inp.type === 'password') { inp.type = 'text'; ico.className = 'fas fa-eye-slash'; }
            else { inp.type = 'password'; ico.className = 'fas fa-eye'; }
        });

        // Connect
        this.dom.connectBtn.addEventListener('click', () => this.connect());

        // Copy plugin key
        this.dom.copyPluginKey.addEventListener('click', () => {
            navigator.clipboard.writeText(this.pluginKey);
            this.notify('Klucz skopiowany!', 'success');
        });

        // Send
        this.dom.sendBtn.addEventListener('click', () => this.send());
        this.dom.msgInput.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
            if (e.key === 'Enter' && !e.shiftKey) { e.preventDefault(); this.send(); }
        });
        this.dom.msgInput.addEventListener('input', () => {
            this.dom.sendBtn.disabled = !this.dom.msgInput.value.trim() || this.generating;
            this.autoResize();
        });

        // Quick actions
        document.querySelectorAll('.action-btn, .chip').forEach(btn => {
            btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
                const p = btn.dataset.prompt;
                if (p) { this.dom.msgInput.value = p; this.dom.sendBtn.disabled = false; this.send(); }
            });
        });

        // Clear & Export
        this.dom.clearBtn.addEventListener('click', () => this.clearChat());
        this.dom.exportBtn.addEventListener('click', () => this.exportChat());
    },

    // ---- CONNECTION ----
    loadKey() {
        if (this.apiKey) this.dom.apiKeyInput.value = this.apiKey;
    },

    showPluginKey() {
        this.dom.pluginKeyDisplay.textContent = this.pluginKey;
    },

    async connect() {
        const key = this.dom.apiKeyInput.value.trim();
        if (!key) return this.notify('Wpisz klucz API OpenAI!', 'error');

        this.apiKey = key;
        localStorage.setItem('roboai_key', key);
        this.setStatus('connecting', 'Łączenie...');

        try {
            const res = await fetch('/.netlify/functions/chat', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify({ apiKey: key, testMode: true })
            });

            if (res.ok) {
                this.setStatus('online', 'Połączono z AI');
                this.notify('Połączono z OpenAI! 🎉', 'success');
            } else {
                const d = await res.json();
                throw new Error(d.error || 'Błąd');
            }
        } catch (err) {
            this.setStatus('offline', 'Błąd połączenia');
            this.notify(err.message, 'error');
        }
    },

    setStatus(state, text) {
        this.dom.statusDot.className = `status-dot ${state}`;
        this.dom.statusText.textContent = text;
    },

    // ---- SEND MESSAGE ----
    async send() {
        const text = this.dom.msgInput.value.trim();
        if (!text || this.generating) return;
        if (!this.apiKey) return this.notify('Najpierw połącz się z AI!', 'warn');

        // Hide welcome
        this.dom.welcome.style.display = 'none';

        // Add user msg
        this.addMsg('user', text);
        this.dom.msgInput.value = '';
        this.dom.sendBtn.disabled = true;
        this.autoResize();

        // Title
        if (this.messages.length === 1) {
            this.dom.chatTitle.textContent = text.length > 45 ? text.slice(0, 45) + '...' : text;
        }

        // Generate
        this.generating = true;
        this.dom.typing.classList.add('active');
        this.scrollDown();

        try {
            const sysPrompt = this.getSystemPrompt();
            const apiMsgs = [
                { role: 'system', content: sysPrompt },
                ...this.messages.map(m => ({ role: m.role, content: m.text }))
            ];

            const res = await fetch('/.netlify/functions/chat', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify({
                    apiKey: this.apiKey,
                    messages: apiMsgs,
                    model: this.dom.modelSelect.value
                })
            });

            if (!res.ok) {
                const d = await res.json();
                throw new Error(d.error || 'Błąd API');
            }

            const data = await res.json();
            this.addMsg('bot', data.content);

            // Auto insert to Studio
            if (this.dom.autoInsert.checked) {
                const blocks = this.extractCode(data.content);
                for (const b of blocks) {
                    await this.sendToPlugin(b);
                }
            }
        } catch (err) {
            this.addMsg('bot', `❌ Błąd: ${err.message}`);
            this.notify(err.message, 'error');
        } finally {
            this.generating = false;
            this.dom.typing.classList.remove('active');
            this.dom.sendBtn.disabled = !this.dom.msgInput.value.trim();
        }
    },

    getSystemPrompt() {
        return `Jesteś ekspertem od Roblox Studio i Luau. Generujesz gotowy kod do wklejenia.

ZASADY:
1. Pisz w Luau (Roblox Lua)
2. Kod musi działać natychmiast po wklejeniu
3. Dla GUI twórz pełne drzewa z Instance.new() - ScreenGui, Frame, TextButton, UICorner, UIStroke, UIGradient, UIListLayout itp.
4. Dodawaj animacje TweenService
5. Oznaczaj bloki kodu jako \`\`\`lua
6. Na końcu KAŻDEGO skryptu dodaj komentarz:
   -- SCRIPT_TYPE: LocalScript  (lub Script albo ModuleScript)
   -- PARENT: StarterGui  (lub ServerScriptService, ReplicatedStorage, StarterPlayerScripts)
7. Odpowiadaj po polsku
8. Bądź szczegółowy - dodawaj komentarze w kodzie`;
    },

    // ---- MESSAGES ----
    addMsg(role, text) {
        this.messages.push({ role: role === 'bot' ? 'assistant' : role, text });
        this.msgCount++;
        this.dom.msgCount.textContent = this.msgCount;

        const time = new Date().toLocaleTimeString('pl-PL', { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit' });
        const div = document.createElement('div');
        div.className = `msg ${role}`;

        const icon = role === 'bot' ? 'fa-robot' : 'fa-user';
        const content = role === 'bot' ? this.renderContent(text) : this.esc(text);

        div.innerHTML = `
            <div class="msg-avatar"><i class="fas ${icon}"></i></div>
            <div class="msg-body">
                <div class="msg-bubble">${content}</div>
                <div class="msg-time">${time}</div>
            </div>`;

        this.dom.messages.appendChild(div);
        this.scrollDown();
    },

    renderContent(text) {
        let html = text;

        // Code blocks
        html = html.replace(/```(\w+)?\n([\s\S]*?)```/g, (_, lang, code) => {
            this.codeCount++;
            this.dom.codeCount.textContent = this.codeCount;
            const id = 'c' + Date.now() + Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 7);
            return `<div class="code-wrap" id="${id}">
                <div class="code-top">
                    <span class="code-lang"><i class="fas fa-code"></i> ${lang || 'lua'}</span>
                    <div class="code-btns">
                        <button class="code-btn" onclick="App.copyCode('${id}')"><i class="fas fa-copy"></i> Kopiuj</button>
                        <button class="code-btn run" onclick="App.runCode('${id}')"><i class="fas fa-play"></i> Wstaw</button>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <pre><code>${this.esc(code.trim())}</code></pre>
            </div>`;
        });

        // Inline code, bold, newlines
        html = html.replace(/`([^`]+)`/g, '<code>$1</code>');
        html = html.replace(/\*\*(.*?)\*\*/g, '<strong>$1</strong>');
        html = html.replace(/\n/g, '<br>');
        return html;
    },

    esc(t) {
        const d = document.createElement('div');
        d.textContent = t;
        return d.innerHTML;
    },

    // ---- CODE ACTIONS ----
    copyCode(id) {
        const code = document.getElementById(id)?.querySelector('code')?.textContent;
        if (code) { navigator.clipboard.writeText(code); this.notify('Kod skopiowany!', 'success'); }
    },

    async runCode(id) {
        const code = document.getElementById(id)?.querySelector('code')?.textContent;
        if (code) await this.sendToPlugin({ code, lang: 'lua' });
    },

    extractCode(text) {
        const blocks = [];
        const re = /```(\w+)?\n([\s\S]*?)```/g;
        let m;
        while ((m = re.exec(text)) !== null) {
            blocks.push({ lang: m[1] || 'lua', code: m[2].trim() });
        }
        return blocks;
    },

    // ---- PLUGIN COMMUNICATION ----
    async sendToPlugin(block) {
        let scriptType = 'LocalScript';
        let parent = 'StarterGui';

        const tm = block.code.match(/--\s*SCRIPT_TYPE:\s*(\w+)/i);
        const pm = block.code.match(/--\s*PARENT:\s*(\w+)/i);
        if (tm) scriptType = tm[1];
        if (pm) parent = pm[1];

        try {
            const res = await fetch('/.netlify/functions/chat', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify({
                    action: 'addTask',
                    pluginKey: this.pluginKey,
                    task: {
                        id: crypto.randomUUID(),
                        code: block.code,
                        scriptType,
                        parent,
                        timestamp: Date.now()
                    }
                })
            });
            if (res.ok) this.notify(`📤 Wysłano do Studio (${scriptType})`, 'info');
        } catch {
            this.notify('Nie wysłano do plugin - skopiuj ręcznie', 'warn');
        }
    },

    // ---- HELPERS ----
    autoResize() {
        const ta = this.dom.msgInput;
        ta.style.height = 'auto';
        ta.style.height = Math.min(ta.scrollHeight, 140) + 'px';
    },

    scrollDown() {
        requestAnimationFrame(() => { this.dom.chat.scrollTop = this.dom.chat.scrollHeight; });
    },

    clearChat() {
        this.messages = [];
        this.msgCount = 0;
        this.codeCount = 0;
        this.dom.msgCount.textContent = '0';
        this.dom.codeCount.textContent = '0';
        this.dom.messages.innerHTML = '';
        this.dom.chatTitle.textContent = 'Nowa Rozmowa';
        this.dom.welcome.style.display = '';
        this.notify('Czat wyczyszczony', 'info');
    },

    exportChat() {
        if (!this.messages.length) return this.notify('Brak wiadomości', 'warn');
        let t = '=== RoboAI Export ===\n\n';
        this.messages.forEach(m => {
            t += `${m.role === 'user' ? '👤' : '🤖'}: ${m.text}\n\n---\n\n`;
        });
        const a = document.createElement('a');
        a.href = URL.createObjectURL(new Blob([t]));
        a.download = `roboai-${Date.now()}.txt`;
        a.click();
        this.notify('Wyeksportowano!', 'success');
    },

    notify(msg, type = 'info') {
        const icons = { success: 'fa-check-circle', error: 'fa-times-circle', warn: 'fa-exclamation-triangle', info: 'fa-info-circle' };
        const n = document.createElement('div');
        n.className = `notif ${type}`;
        n.innerHTML = `
            <i class="fas ${icons[type]} notif-icon"></i>
            <span class="notif-text">${msg}</span>
            <button class="notif-close" onclick="this.parentElement.remove()"><i class="fas fa-times"></i></button>`;
        this.dom.notifs.appendChild(n);
        setTimeout(() => { if (n.parentElement) n.remove(); }, 4500);
    }
};

// Start
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => App.init());
📄 netlify/functions/chat.js
JavaScript

const { Redis } = require('@upstash/redis');

let redis = null;
try {
    if (process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_URL) {
        redis = new Redis({
            url: process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_URL,
            token: process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_TOKEN,
        });
    }
} catch (e) {
    console.log('Redis not available, using fallback');
}

// Fallback in-memory store (limited but works for testing)
const memStore = {};

async function storeTask(pluginKey, task) {
    const key = `tasks:${pluginKey}`;
    if (redis) {
        let tasks = (await redis.get(key)) || [];
        tasks.push(task);
        await redis.set(key, tasks, { ex: 3600 });
    } else {
        if (!memStore[key]) memStore[key] = [];
        memStore[key].push(task);
    }
}

exports.handler = async (event) => {
    const headers = {
        'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*',
        'Access-Control-Allow-Headers': 'Content-Type',
        'Access-Control-Allow-Methods': 'GET, POST, OPTIONS',
        'Content-Type': 'application/json'
    };

    if (event.httpMethod === 'OPTIONS') {
        return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: '' };
    }

    if (event.httpMethod !== 'POST') {
        return { statusCode: 405, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: 'POST only' }) };
    }

    try {
        const body = JSON.parse(event.body);

        // ---- TASK STORAGE ----
        if (body.action === 'addTask') {
            await storeTask(body.pluginKey, body.task);
            return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ success: true }) };
        }

        // ---- AI CHAT ----
        const { apiKey, messages, model, testMode } = body;

        if (!apiKey) {
            return { statusCode: 400, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: 'Brak klucza API' }) };
        }

        // Test connection
        if (testMode) {
            const test = await fetch('https://api.openai.com/v1/models', {
                headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${apiKey}` }
            });
            return {
                statusCode: test.ok ? 200 : 401,
                headers,
                body: JSON.stringify(test.ok ? { success: true } : { error: 'Nieprawidłowy klucz API OpenAI' })
            };
        }

        // Call OpenAI
        const aiRes = await fetch('https://api.openai.com/v1/chat/completions', {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: {
                'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                Authorization: `Bearer ${apiKey}`
            },
            body: JSON.stringify({
                model: model || 'gpt-4o-mini',
                messages,
                max_tokens: 4096,
                temperature: 0.7
            })
        });

        if (!aiRes.ok) {
            const err = await aiRes.json();
            return {
                statusCode: aiRes.status,
                headers,
                body: JSON.stringify({ error: err.error?.message || 'Błąd OpenAI' })
            };
        }

        const data = await aiRes.json();
        return {
            statusCode: 200,
            headers,
            body: JSON.stringify({
                content: data.choices[0]?.message?.content || '',
                usage: data.usage
            })
        };

    } catch (err) {
        return {
            statusCode: 500,
            headers,
            body: JSON.stringify({ error: err.message })
        };
    }
};
📄 netlify/functions/get-task.js
JavaScript

const { Redis } = require('@upstash/redis');

let redis = null;
try {
    if (process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_URL) {
        redis = new Redis({
            url: process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_URL,
            token: process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_TOKEN,
        });
    }
} catch (e) {}

// Same fallback as chat.js
const memStore = {};

exports.handler = async (event) => {
    const headers = {
        'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*',
        'Access-Control-Allow-Headers': 'Content-Type',
        'Access-Control-Allow-Methods': 'GET, POST, OPTIONS',
        'Content-Type': 'application/json'
    };

    if (event.httpMethod === 'OPTIONS') {
        return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: '' };
    }

    // Plugin sends POST to mark task complete
    if (event.httpMethod === 'POST') {
        try {
            const body = JSON.parse(event.body);
            // Just acknowledge - task completed
            return { statusCode: 200, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ success: true }) };
        } catch {
            return { statusCode: 400, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: 'Bad request' }) };
        }
    }

    // Plugin sends GET to fetch tasks
    const pluginKey = event.queryStringParameters?.pluginKey;
    if (!pluginKey) {
        return { statusCode: 400, headers, body: JSON.stringify({ error: 'pluginKey required' }) };
    }

    try {
        const key = `tasks:${pluginKey}`;
        let tasks = [];

        if (redis) {
            tasks = (await redis.get(key)) || [];
            if (tasks.length > 0) await redis.del(key);
        } else {
            tasks = memStore[key] || [];
            if (tasks.length > 0) memStore[key] = [];
        }

        return {
            statusCode: 200,
            headers,
            body: JSON.stringify({ tasks })
        };

    } catch (err) {
        return {
            statusCode: 500,
            headers,
            body: JSON.stringify({ error: err.message })
        };
    }
};
KROK 3: Wrzuć na GitHub
3.1 Zainstaluj Git (jeśli nie masz)
Pobierz z https://git-scm.com/downloads i zainstaluj

3.2 Stwórz konto na GitHub
Idź na https://github.com i załóż konto (jeśli nie masz)

3.3 Stwórz nowe repozytorium
Na GitHub kliknij zielony przycisk "New" (albo + w rogu)
Nazwa repo: roblox-ai-assistant
Zostaw Public
NIE zaznaczaj "Add README"
Kliknij Create repository
3.4 Wypchnij pliki
Otwórz terminal/cmd w folderze projektu:

Bash

cd ścieżka/do/roblox-ai-assistant

git init
git add .
git commit -m "first commit"
git branch -M main
git remote add origin https://github.com/TWOJ-LOGIN/roblox-ai-assistant.git
git push -u origin main
KROK 4: Deploy na Netlify
Idź na https://app.netlify.com i załóż konto (przez GitHub)
Kliknij "Add new site" → "Import an existing project"
Wybierz GitHub
Znajdź repo roblox-ai-assistant
Ustaw:
Build command: zostaw puste
Publish directory: . (kropka)
Kliknij "Deploy site"
Poczekaj ~1 minutę
Netlify da ci link np. https://amazing-name-123456.netlify.app
KROK 5: Dodaj Upstash Redis (WAŻNE!)
Bez tego komunikacja strona↔plugin nie będzie działać stabilnie.

5.1 Stwórz bazę Redis
Idź na https://upstash.com → załóż konto (za darmo)
Kliknij "Create Database"
Nazwa: roboai
Region: EU West (albo najbliższy)
Kliknij Create
Skopiuj:
UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_URL (np. https://xyz.upstash.io)
UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_TOKEN (długi string)
5.2 Dodaj zmienne w Netlify
W Netlify → twoja strona → Site configuration → Environment variables
Kliknij "Add a variable"
Dodaj dwie zmienne:
text

UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_URL = https://twoje-xyz.upstash.io
UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_TOKEN = AXxxxxxxxxxxxxx...
Kliknij "Deploys" → "Trigger deploy" → "Deploy site"
KROK 6: Zdobądź klucz OpenAI
Idź na https://platform.openai.com
Załóż konto / zaloguj się
Idź do API Keys → "Create new secret key"
Skopiuj klucz (zaczyna się od sk-...)
Dodaj środki na koncie (minimum $5, GPT-4o-mini jest bardzo tani)
KROK 7: Stwórz Plugin w Roblox Studio
Jak nazwać plugin?
Nazwa: RoboAI (albo jak chcesz, np. AI-Assistant)

Jak go stworzyć?
Sposób 1 - Plik na dysku (ZALECANY):
Znajdź folder pluginów Roblox:

Windows: %LOCALAPPDATA%\Roblox\Plugins\
Wklej to w pasek adresu Eksploratora plików
Mac: ~/Documents/Roblox/Plugins/
W tym folderze stwórz nowy plik: RoboAI.lua

Wklej do niego ten kod:

Lua

--[[
    ==========================================
    ROBOAI STUDIO PLUGIN
    ==========================================
    
    INSTRUKCJA:
    1. Zmień SERVER_URL na adres twojej strony Netlify
    2. Zmień PLUGIN_KEY na klucz ze strony (kopiujesz z sidebara)
    3. Zapisz plik
    4. Zrestartuj Roblox Studio
    5. Kliknij "RoboAI" w toolbarze
    6. Kliknij "Uruchom" w panelu
    
    WAŻNE: Włącz HttpService!
    Game Settings → Security → Allow HTTP Requests → ON
--]]

----------------------------------------------------
-- ⚙️ KONFIGURACJA - ZMIEŃ TO!
----------------------------------------------------
local SERVER_URL  = "https://TWOJA-STRONA.netlify.app"   -- <- ZMIEŃ!
local PLUGIN_KEY  = "rk_TWOJ_KLUCZ"                      -- <- ZMIEŃ!
local POLL_DELAY  = 3  -- sekundy między sprawdzaniem
----------------------------------------------------

local HttpService = game:GetService("HttpService")
local Selection = game:GetService("Selection")
local ChangeHistoryService = game:GetService("ChangeHistoryService")

-- Toolbar
local toolbar = plugin:CreateToolbar("RoboAI Studio")
local mainButton = toolbar:CreateButton(
    "RoboAI",
    "Otwórz panel AI Assistant",
    "rbxassetid://4458901886"
)

-- Widget
local widgetInfo = DockWidgetPluginGuiInfo.new(
    Enum.InitialDockState.Right,
    false, false,
    300, 450, 250, 300
)
local widget = plugin:CreateDockWidgetPluginGui("RoboAIPanel", widgetInfo)
widget.Title = "🤖 RoboAI"

-- ==========================================
-- LOGIKA
-- ==========================================

local isRunning = false
local logCount = 0

local function log(msg, color)
    logCount += 1
    local lbl = Instance.new("TextLabel")
    lbl.Size = UDim2.new(1,0,0,0)
    lbl.AutomaticSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.Y
    lbl.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    lbl.Text = os.date("[%H:%M:%S] ") .. msg
    lbl.TextColor3 = color or Color3.fromRGB(138,155,192)
    lbl.Font = Enum.Font.RobotoMono
    lbl.TextSize = 10
    lbl.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
    lbl.TextWrapped = true
    lbl.LayoutOrder = logCount
    lbl.Parent = logScroll
    
    task.defer(function()
        logScroll.CanvasPosition = Vector2.new(0, logScroll.AbsoluteCanvasSize.Y)
    end)
end

local function getParent(name)
    local map = {
        StarterGui = game:GetService("StarterGui"),
        ServerScriptService = game:GetService("ServerScriptService"),
        ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"),
        StarterPlayerScripts = game:GetService("StarterPlayer"):FindFirstChild("StarterPlayerScripts"),
        Workspace = workspace,
    }
    return map[name] or game:GetService("StarterGui")
end

local function runTask(t)
    log("📥 Zadanie: " .. (t.scriptType or "Script"), Color3.fromRGB(96,165,250))
    
    local ok, err = pcall(function()
        local inst
        local sType = t.scriptType or "LocalScript"
        
        if sType == "LocalScript" then
            inst = Instance.new("LocalScript")
        elseif sType == "ModuleScript" then
            inst = Instance.new("ModuleScript")
        else
            inst = Instance.new("Script")
        end
        
        inst.Source = t.code
        inst.Name = "AI_" .. sType .. "_" .. os.time()
        inst.Parent = getParent(t.parent or "StarterGui")
        
        Selection:Set({inst})
        ChangeHistoryService:SetWaypoint("RoboAI: " .. sType)
        
        log("✅ Stworzono " .. sType .. " → " .. (t.parent or "StarterGui"), Color3.fromRGB(16,185,129))
    end)
    
    if not ok then
        log("❌ Błąd: " .. tostring(err), Color3.fromRGB(239,68,68))
    end
    
    -- Powiadom serwer
    pcall(function()
        HttpService:PostAsync(
            SERVER_URL .. "/.netlify/functions/get-task",
            HttpService:JSONEncode({ pluginKey = PLUGIN_KEY, taskId = t.id, completed = true }),
            Enum.HttpContentType.ApplicationJson
        )
    end)
end

local function poll()
    local ok, result = pcall(function()
        local url = SERVER_URL .. "/.netlify/functions/get-task?pluginKey=" .. PLUGIN_KEY
        local response = HttpService:GetAsync(url)
        local data = HttpService:JSONDecode(response)
        
        if data.tasks and #data.tasks > 0 then
            log("📨 Otrzymano " .. #data.tasks .. " zadań!", Color3.fromRGB(96,165,250))
            for _, t in ipairs(data.tasks) do
                runTask(t)
            end
        end
    end)
    
    if not ok then
        -- Cichy błąd - nie spamuj logów
    end
end

local function start()
    if isRunning then return end
    isRunning = true
    
    statusDot.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(16,185,129)
    statusLabel.Text = "Aktywny - nasłuchuję..."
    statusLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(16,185,129)
    toggleBtn.Text = "⏸  ZATRZYMAJ"
    toggleBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(239,68,68)
    
    log("🚀 Uruchomiono!", Color3.fromRGB(16,185,129))
    log("🔗 " .. SERVER_URL, Color3.fromRGB(96,165,250))
    log("⏳ Sprawdzam co " .. POLL_DELAY .. "s...", Color3.fromRGB(138,155,192))
    
    task.spawn(function()
        while isRunning do
            poll()
            task.wait(POLL_DELAY)
        end
    end)
end

local function stop()
    isRunning = false
    statusDot.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(245,158,11)
    statusLabel.Text = "Zatrzymany"
    statusLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(245,158,11)
    toggleBtn.Text = "▶  URUCHOM"
    toggleBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(59,130,246)
    log("⏸ Zatrzymano", Color3.fromRGB(245,158,11))
end

-- Events
toggleBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
    if isRunning then stop() else start() end
end)

mainButton.Click:Connect(function()
    widget.Enabled = not widget.Enabled
end)

-- Start message
log("🤖 RoboAI Plugin załadowany", Color3.fromRGB(96,165,250))
log("Kliknij URUCHOM aby połączyć", Color3.fromRGB(138,155,192))

Otwórz Roblox Studio

W Explorer kliknij prawym na ServerStorage (to nie ma znaczenia gdzie)

Lua

local f = Instance.new("Script")

ALE to NIE jest sposób na plugin. Plugin musi być jako plik .lua w folderze Plugins. Użyj Sposób 1.

KROK 8: Konfiguracja Pluginu
8.1 Włącz HttpService w Roblox Studio
Otwórz swoje Place
Home → Game Settings → Security
Allow HTTP Requests → ON ✅
Zamknij
8.2 Zmień konfigurację w pliku RoboAI.lua
Otwórz plik RoboAI.lua (w folderze Plugins) w Notatniku i zmień:

Lua

local SERVER_URL  = "https://amazing-name-123456.netlify.app"  -- Twój URL z Netlify
local PLUGIN_KEY  = "rk_a1b2c3d4e5f6..."                       -- Klucz ze strony
Klucz pluginu znajdziesz na stronie w sidebarze pod "Plugin Key" - skopiuj go.

8.3 Zrestartuj Roblox Studio
Zamknij i otwórz ponownie. Plugin powinien się załadować automatycznie.

KROK 9: Testuj Wszystko!
text

1. 🌐 Otwórz stronę → wpisz API key OpenAI → Połącz
2. 🎮 W Roblox Studio → kliknij "RoboAI" w toolbarze → "Uruchom"
3. 💬 Na stronie napisz: "Stwórz ładne GUI menu głównego"
4. 🤖 AI wygeneruje kod Luau
5. 📤 Kod automatycznie trafi do Roblox Studio!
6. ✅ W Studio pojawi się nowy LocalScript w StarterGui
❓ Najczęstsze Problemy
text

Problem: "Nie mogę połączyć z AI"
→ Sprawdź czy klucz OpenAI zaczyna się od "sk-"
→ Sprawdź czy masz środki na koncie OpenAI

Problem: "Plugin nie odbiera kodu"
→ Sprawdź czy HttpService jest włączony
→ Sprawdź czy URL i Plugin Key się zgadzają
→ Sprawdź czy kliknąłeś "Uruchom" w panelu pluginu

Problem: "Netlify deploy failed"
→ Sprawdź czy struktura folderów jest prawidłowa
→ Sprawdź czy netlify.toml jest w głównym folderze

Problem: "Functions error"
→ Dodaj zmienne UPSTASH w Netlify env variables
→ Zrób redeploy po dodaniu zmiennych
💰 Koszty
Usługa	Koszt
Netlify hosting	$0 (darmowy tier)
Netlify Functions	$0 (125k wywołań/mies.)
Upstash Redis	$0 (10k komend/dzień)
OpenAI GPT-4o-mini	~$0.15 / 1M tokenów
Razem	Praktycznie darmowe
Za normalny use (50-100 zapytań dziennie) zapłacisz OpenAI mniej niż $1/miesiąc.

toml

[build]
  functions = "netlify/functions"
  publish = "."

[functions]
  node_bundler = "esbuild"

[[headers]]
  for = "/*"
  [headers.values]
    Access-Control-Allow-Origin = "*"
    Access-Control-Allow-Headers = "Content-Type, X-API-Key"
    Access-Control-Allow-Methods = "GET, POST, OPTIONS"
