JavaScript

// ============================================
// AI ROBLOX STUDIO ASSISTANT - Main Script
// ============================================

class RoboAI {
    constructor() {
        // State
        this.messages = [];
        this.isGenerating = false;
        this.apiKey = localStorage.getItem('roboai_apikey') || '';
        this.pluginKey = localStorage.getItem('roboai_pluginkey') || this.generateKey();
        this.connected = false;
        this.messageCount = 0;
        this.codeCount = 0;
        this.pendingTasks = [];
        this.history = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('roboai_history') || '[]');
        
        // DOM Elements
        this.elements = {};
        this.cacheElements();
        
        // Initialize
        this.init();
    }

    cacheElements() {
        const ids = [
            'sidebar', 'sidebarToggle', 'mobileMenuBtn', 'connectionStatus',
            'statusDot', 'statusText', 'statusSub', 'apiKeyInput', 'toggleApiKey',
            'connectBtn', 'chatArea', 'welcomeScreen', 'messagesContainer',
            'typingIndicator', 'messageInput', 'sendBtn', 'charCounter',
            'autoExecute', 'messageCount', 'codeCount', 'currentChatTitle',
            'modelSelect', 'settingsModal', 'closeSettings', 'settingsBtn',
            'clearChat', 'exportChat', 'historyList', 'notificationContainer',
            'pluginKeyDisplay', 'serverUrl', 'generatePluginKey', 'particles'
        ];
        
        ids.forEach(id => {
            this.elements[id] = document.getElementById(id);
        });
    }

    init() {
        this.setupEventListeners();
        this.loadApiKey();
        this.loadHistory();
        this.setupParticles();
        this.setupAutoResize();
        this.updateServerUrl();
        this.displayPluginKey();
        this.startPolling();
    }

    // ============================================
    // EVENT LISTENERS
    // ============================================

    setupEventListeners() {
        // Sidebar toggle
        this.elements.sidebarToggle?.addEventListener('click', () => {
            this.elements.sidebar.classList.toggle('collapsed');
        });

        this.elements.mobileMenuBtn?.addEventListener('click', () => {
            this.elements.sidebar.classList.toggle('mobile-open');
        });

        // Close sidebar on outside click (mobile)
        document.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
            if (window.innerWidth <= 768 && 
                !this.elements.sidebar.contains(e.target) && 
                !this.elements.mobileMenuBtn.contains(e.target)) {
                this.elements.sidebar.classList.remove('mobile-open');
            }
        });

        // API Key
        this.elements.toggleApiKey?.addEventListener('click', () => {
            const input = this.elements.apiKeyInput;
            const icon = this.elements.toggleApiKey.querySelector('i');
            if (input.type === 'password') {
                input.type = 'text';
                icon.className = 'fas fa-eye-slash';
            } else {
                input.type = 'password';
                icon.className = 'fas fa-eye';
            }
        });

        this.elements.connectBtn?.addEventListener('click', () => this.connect());

        // Send message
        this.elements.sendBtn?.addEventListener('click', () => this.sendMessage());
        
        this.elements.messageInput?.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
            if (e.key === 'Enter' && !e.shiftKey) {
                e.preventDefault();
                this.sendMessage();
            }
        });

        this.elements.messageInput?.addEventListener('input', () => {
            this.updateCharCounter();
            this.updateSendButton();
        });

        // Quick actions
        document.querySelectorAll('.action-btn').forEach(btn => {
            btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
                const prompt = btn.getAttribute('data-prompt');
                if (prompt) {
                    this.elements.messageInput.value = prompt;
                    this.updateCharCounter();
                    this.updateSendButton();
                    this.sendMessage();
                }
            });
        });

        // Suggestion chips
        document.querySelectorAll('.suggestion-chip').forEach(chip => {
            chip.addEventListener('click', () => {
                const prompt = chip.getAttribute('data-prompt');
                if (prompt) {
                    this.elements.messageInput.value = prompt;
                    this.updateCharCounter();
                    this.updateSendButton();
                    this.sendMessage();
                }
            });
        });

        // Settings
        this.elements.settingsBtn?.addEventListener('click', () => {
            this.elements.settingsModal.classList.add('active');
        });

        this.elements.closeSettings?.addEventListener('click', () => {
            this.elements.settingsModal.classList.remove('active');
        });

        this.elements.settingsModal?.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
            if (e.target === this.elements.settingsModal) {
                this.elements.settingsModal.classList.remove('active');
            }
        });

        // Clear chat
        this.elements.clearChat?.addEventListener('click', () => {
            this.clearChat();
        });

        // Export
        this.elements.exportChat?.addEventListener('click', () => {
            this.exportChat();
        });

        // Plugin key
        this.elements.generatePluginKey?.addEventListener('click', () => {
            this.pluginKey = this.generateKey();
            localStorage.setItem('roboai_pluginkey', this.pluginKey);
            this.displayPluginKey();
            this.notify('Nowy klucz wygenerowany!', 'success');
        });
    }

    // ============================================
    // CONNECTION
    // ============================================

    loadApiKey() {
        if (this.apiKey) {
            this.elements.apiKeyInput.value = this.apiKey;
        }
    }

    async connect() {
        const key = this.elements.apiKeyInput.value.trim();
        if (!key) {
            this.notify('Podaj klucz API OpenAI!', 'error');
            return;
        }

        this.apiKey = key;
        localStorage.setItem('roboai_apikey', key);
        
        this.setConnectionStatus('connecting', 'Łączenie...', 'Weryfikacja klucza');

        try {
            const response = await fetch('/.netlify/functions/chat', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: {
                    'Content-Type': 'application/json'
                },
                body: JSON.stringify({
                    apiKey: this.apiKey,
                    messages: [{ role: 'user', content: 'test connection' }],
                    model: 'gpt-4o-mini',
                    testMode: true
                })
            });

            if (response.ok) {
                this.connected = true;
                this.setConnectionStatus('connected', 'Połączono', 'OpenAI API aktywne');
                this.notify('Połączono z AI!', 'success');
            } else {
                const data = await response.json();
                throw new Error(data.error || 'Błąd połączenia');
            }
        } catch (error) {
            this.connected = false;
            this.setConnectionStatus('disconnected', 'Błąd', error.message);
            this.notify(`Błąd: ${error.message}`, 'error');
        }
    }

    setConnectionStatus(status, text, sub) {
        const dot = this.elements.statusDot;
        dot.className = `status-indicator ${status}`;
        this.elements.statusText.textContent = text;
        this.elements.statusSub.textContent = sub;
    }

    // ============================================
    // MESSAGING
    // ============================================

    async sendMessage() {
        const input = this.elements.messageInput;
        const text = input.value.trim();
        
        if (!text || this.isGenerating) return;

        if (!this.apiKey) {
            this.notify('Najpierw podaj klucz API i połącz się!', 'warning');
            return;
        }

        // Hide welcome screen
        if (this.elements.welcomeScreen) {
            this.elements.welcomeScreen.style.display = 'none';
        }

        // Add user message
        this.addMessage('user', text);
        input.value = '';
        this.updateCharCounter();
        this.updateSendButton();
        this.autoResize();

        // Update title
        if (this.messages.length === 1) {
            const title = text.substring(0, 50) + (text.length > 50 ? '...' : '');
            this.elements.currentChatTitle.textContent = title;
        }

        // Show typing indicator
        this.isGenerating = true;
        this.showTyping(true);

        try {
            // Prepare messages for API
            const systemPrompt = this.getSystemPrompt();
            const apiMessages = [
                { role: 'system', content: systemPrompt },
                ...this.messages.map(m => ({ role: m.role, content: m.content }))
            ];

            const response = await fetch('/.netlify/functions/chat', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: {
                    'Content-Type': 'application/json'
                },
                body: JSON.stringify({
                    apiKey: this.apiKey,
                    messages: apiMessages,
                    model: this.elements.modelSelect.value
                })
            });

            if (!response.ok) {
                const errorData = await response.json();
                throw new Error(errorData.error || 'Błąd API');
            }

            const data = await response.json();
            const assistantMessage = data.content;

            // Add assistant message
            this.addMessage('assistant', assistantMessage);

            // Extract and handle code blocks
            const codeBlocks = this.extractCodeBlocks(assistantMessage);
            if (codeBlocks.length > 0 && this.elements.autoExecute.checked) {
                for (const block of codeBlocks) {
                    await this.sendToPlugin(block.code, block.language);
                }
            }

            // Save to history
            this.saveToHistory(text);

        } catch (error) {
            this.notify(`Błąd: ${error.message}`, 'error');
            this.addMessage('assistant', `❌ Wystąpił błąd: ${error.message}. Sprawdź klucz API i spróbuj ponownie.`);
        } finally {
            this.isGenerating = false;
            this.showTyping(false);
        }
    }

    getSystemPrompt() {
        const codeStyle = document.getElementById('codeStyle')?.value || 'detailed';
        const scriptType = document.getElementById('scriptType')?.value || 'auto';
        
        return `Jesteś ekspertem od Roblox Studio i Luau. Twoje zadanie to generowanie kodu i pomaganie w tworzeniu gier w Roblox.

ZASADY:
1. Zawsze pisz kod w Luau (Roblox Lua)
2. Kod musi być gotowy do wklejenia i działać natychmiast
3. Używaj najnowszych praktyk Roblox (nie przestarzałych API)
4. Dla GUI twórz kompletne drzewa z ScreenGui, Frame, TextButton, TextLabel, UICorner, UIStroke, UIGradient, UIListLayout itp.
5. Dodawaj animacje TweenService do GUI
6. Kod GUI wstawiaj do LocalScript w StarterPlayerScripts lub StarterGui
7. Serwer code wstawiaj w ServerScriptService
8. Każdy blok kodu oznaczaj jako \`\`\`lua
9. Styl kodu: ${codeStyle}
10. Preferowany typ skryptu: ${scriptType}

WAŻNE FORMAT:
- Dla GUI: twórz PEŁNY kod tworzący GUI programatycznie (Instance.new)
- NIE używaj XML/HTML, tylko Lua/Luau
- Dodawaj komentarze wyjaśniające co robi każda część
- Na końcu kodu dodaj komentarz -- SCRIPT_TYPE: LocalScript/Script/ModuleScript
- Na końcu dodaj komentarz -- PARENT: StarterGui/ServerScriptService/StarterPlayerScripts/ReplicatedStorage

Odpowiadaj po polsku. Bądź pomocny i szczegółowy.`;
    }

    addMessage(role, content) {
        const message = {
            role,
            content,
            timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
        };
        this.messages.push(message);

        // Update counters
        this.messageCount++;
        this.elements.messageCount.textContent = this.messageCount;

        // Render message
        this.renderMessage(message);

        // Scroll to bottom
        this.scrollToBottom();
    }

    renderMessage(message) {
        const container = this.elements.messagesContainer;
        const div = document.createElement('div');
        div.className = `message ${message.role}`;

        const time = new Date(message.timestamp).toLocaleTimeString('pl-PL', {
            hour: '2-digit',
            minute: '2-digit'
        });

        const avatarIcon = message.role === 'assistant' ? 'fa-robot' : 'fa-user';
        
        let processedContent = message.content;
        if (message.role === 'assistant') {
            processedContent = this.processContent(message.content);
        } else {
            processedContent = this.escapeHtml(message.content);
        }

        div.innerHTML = `
            <div class="message-avatar">
                <i class="fas ${avatarIcon}"></i>
            </div>
            <div class="message-content">
                <div class="message-bubble">${processedContent}</div>
                <div class="message-time">${time}</div>
                <div class="message-actions">
                    <button class="msg-action-btn" onclick="app.copyMessageText(this)" title="Kopiuj">
                        <i class="fas fa-copy"></i>
                    </button>
                </div>
            </div>
        `;

        container.appendChild(div);
    }

    processContent(content) {
        // Handle code blocks
        let processed = content.replace(/```(\w+)?\n([\s\S]*?)```/g, (match, lang, code) => {
            lang = lang || 'lua';
            this.codeCount++;
            this.elements.codeCount.textContent = this.codeCount;
            
            const codeId = `code-${Date.now()}-${Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 9)}`;
            
            return `<div class="code-block" id="${codeId}">
                <div class="code-header">
                    <span class="code-lang"><i class="fas fa-code"></i> ${lang}</span>
                    <div class="code-actions">
                        <button class="code-action-btn" onclick="app.copyCode('${codeId}')">
                            <i class="fas fa-copy"></i> Kopiuj
                        </button>
                        <button class="code-action-btn execute-btn" onclick="app.executeCode('${codeId}')">
                            <i class="fas fa-play"></i> Wstaw do Studio
                        </button>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <pre><code>${this.escapeHtml(code.trim())}</code></pre>
            </div>`;
        });

        // Handle inline code
        processed = processed.replace(/`([^`]+)`/g, '<code>$1</code>');

        // Handle bold
        processed = processed.replace(/\*\*(.*?)\*\*/g, '<strong>$1</strong>');

        // Handle italic
        processed = processed.replace(/\*(.*?)\*/g, '<em>$1</em>');

        // Handle line breaks
        processed = processed.replace(/\n/g, '<br>');

        return processed;
    }

    escapeHtml(text) {
        const div = document.createElement('div');
        div.textContent = text;
        return div.innerHTML;
    }

    extractCodeBlocks(content) {
        const blocks = [];
        const regex = /```(\w+)?\n([\s\S]*?)```/g;
        let match;
        while ((match = regex.exec(content)) !== null) {
            blocks.push({
                language: match[1] || 'lua',
                code: match[2].trim()
            });
        }
        return blocks;
    }

    // ============================================
    // CODE ACTIONS
    // ============================================

    copyCode(codeId) {
        const block = document.getElementById(codeId);
        if (!block) return;
        
        const code = block.querySelector('code').textContent;
        navigator.clipboard.writeText(code).then(() => {
            this.notify('Kod skopiowany!', 'success');
        });
    }

    async executeCode(codeId) {
        const block = document.getElementById(codeId);
        if (!block) return;
        
        const code = block.querySelector('code').textContent;
        await this.sendToPlugin(code, 'lua');
    }

    copyMessageText(btn) {
        const bubble = btn.closest('.message-content').querySelector('.message-bubble');
        const text = bubble.textContent || bubble.innerText;
        navigator.clipboard.writeText(text).then(() => {
            this.notify('Skopiowano!', 'success');
        });
    }

    // ============================================
    // PLUGIN COMMUNICATION
    // ============================================

    async sendToPlugin(code, language) {
        // Determine script type and parent from code comments
        let scriptType = 'LocalScript';
        let parent = 'StarterGui';

        const typeMatch = code.match(/--\s*SCRIPT_TYPE:\s*(\w+)/i);
        const parentMatch = code.match(/--\s*PARENT:\s*(\w+)/i);

        if (typeMatch) scriptType = typeMatch[1];
        if (parentMatch) parent = parentMatch[1];

        const task = {
            id: this.generateKey(),
            code: code,
            scriptType: scriptType,
            parent: parent,
            timestamp: Date.now(),
            status: 'pending'
        };

        this.pendingTasks.push(task);

        try {
            const response = await fetch('/.netlify/functions/chat', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: {
                    'Content-Type': 'application/json'
                },
                body: JSON.stringify({
                    action: 'addTask',
                    pluginKey: this.pluginKey,
                    task: task
                })
            });

            if (response.ok) {
                this.notify(`📤 Kod wysłany do Studio (${scriptType})`, 'info');
            }
        } catch (error) {
            this.notify('Nie udało się wysłać do plugin. Skopiuj kod ręcznie.', 'warning');
        }
    }

    startPolling() {
        // Check for task completions every 5 seconds
        setInterval(async () => {
            if (this.pendingTasks.length === 0) return;

            try {
                const response = await fetch(`/.netlify/functions/get-task?pluginKey=${this.pluginKey}&check=completions`);
                if (response.ok) {
                    const data = await response.json();
                    if (data.completions) {
                        data.completions.forEach(taskId => {
                            this.pendingTasks = this.pendingTasks.filter(t => t.id !== taskId);
                            this.notify('✅ Kod wstawiony do Studio!', 'success');
                        });
                    }
                }
            } catch (e) {
                // Silence errors
            }
        }, 5000);
    }

    // ============================================
    // HISTORY
    // ============================================

    saveToHistory(prompt) {
        const item = {
            id: Date.now(),
            title: prompt.substring(0, 60),
            timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
        };

        this.history.unshift(item);
        if (this.history.length > 20) this.history.pop();
        
        localStorage.setItem('roboai_history', JSON.stringify(this.history));
        this.loadHistory();
    }

    loadHistory() {
        const list = this.elements.historyList;
        if (!list) return;

        if (this.history.length === 0) {
            list.innerHTML = `
                <div class="history-empty">
                    <i class="fas fa-inbox"></i>
                    <p>Brak historii</p>
                </div>
            `;
            return;
        }

        list.innerHTML = this.history.map(item => `
            <button class="history-item" onclick="app.loadHistoryItem('${item.title}')">
                <i class="fas fa-message"></i>
                <span>${this.escapeHtml(item.title)}</span>
            </button>
        `).join('');
    }

    loadHistoryItem(title) {
        this.elements.messageInput.value = title;
        this.updateCharCounter();
        this.updateSendButton();
        if (window.innerWidth <= 768) {
            this.elements.sidebar.classList.remove('mobile-open');
        }
    }

    // ============================================
    // UI HELPERS
    // ============================================

    showTyping(show) {
        const indicator = this.elements.typingIndicator;
        if (show) {
            indicator.classList.add('active');
        } else {
            indicator.classList.remove('active');
        }
        this.scrollToBottom();
    }

    scrollToBottom() {
        requestAnimationFrame(() => {
            const chatArea = this.elements.chatArea;
            chatArea.scrollTop = chatArea.scrollHeight;
        });
    }

    updateCharCounter() {
        const count = this.elements.messageInput.value.length;
        this.elements.charCounter.textContent = `${count}/4000`;
    }

    updateSendButton() {
        const hasText = this.elements.messageInput.value.trim().length > 0;
        this.elements.sendBtn.disabled = !hasText || this.isGenerating;
    }

    setupAutoResize() {
        const textarea = this.elements.messageInput;
        if (!textarea) return;

        textarea.addEventListener('input', () => this.autoResize());
    }

    autoResize() {
        const textarea = this.elements.messageInput;
        textarea.style.height = 'auto';
        textarea.style.height = Math.min(textarea.scrollHeight, 150) + 'px';
    }

    clearChat() {
        this.messages = [];
        this.messageCount = 0;
        this.codeCount = 0;
        this.elements.messageCount.textContent = '0';
        this.elements.codeCount.textContent = '0';
        this.elements.messagesContainer.innerHTML = '';
        this.elements.currentChatTitle.textContent = 'Nowa Rozmowa';
        this.elements.welcomeScreen.style.display = 'flex';
        this.notify('Czat wyczyszczony', 'info');
    }

    exportChat() {
        if (this.messages.length === 0) {
            this.notify('Brak wiadomości do eksportu', 'warning');
            return;
        }

        let text = '=== RoboAI Studio - Export ===\n\n';
        this.messages.forEach(m => {
            const role = m.role === 'user' ? '👤 Ty' : '🤖 AI';
            const time = new Date(m.timestamp).toLocaleString('pl-PL');
            text += `${role} (${time}):\n${m.content}\n\n---\n\n`;
        });

        const blob = new Blob([text], { type: 'text/plain' });
        const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
        const a = document.createElement('a');
        a.href = url;
        a.download = `roboai-chat-${Date.now()}.txt`;
        a.click();
        URL.revokeObjectURL(url);

        this.notify('Czat wyeksportowany!', 'success');
    }

    // ============================================
    // NOTIFICATIONS
    // ============================================

    notify(message, type = 'info') {
        const container = this.elements.notificationContainer;
        const icons = {
            success: 'fa-check-circle',
            error: 'fa-exclamation-circle',
            warning: 'fa-exclamation-triangle',
            info: 'fa-info-circle'
        };

        const notif = document.createElement('div');
        notif.className = `notification ${type}`;
        notif.innerHTML = `
            <i class="fas ${icons[type]} notification-icon"></i>
            <span class="notification-text">${message}</span>
            <button class="notification-close" onclick="this.parentElement.remove()">
                <i class="fas fa-times"></i>
            </button>
        `;

        container.appendChild(notif);

        setTimeout(() => {
            notif.style.animation = 'notifOut 0.3s ease-in forwards';
            setTimeout(() => notif.remove(), 300);
        }, 4000);
    }

    // ============================================
    // UTILITIES
    // ============================================

    generateKey() {
        return 'rk_' + Array.from(crypto.getRandomValues(new Uint8Array(16)))
            .map(b => b.toString(16).padStart(2, '0')).join('');
    }

    displayPluginKey() {
        if (this.elements.pluginKeyDisplay) {
            this.elements.pluginKeyDisplay.textContent = this.pluginKey;
        }
    }

    updateServerUrl() {
        if (this.elements.serverUrl) {
            this.elements.serverUrl.textContent = window.location.origin;
        }
    }

    // ============================================
    // PARTICLES
    // ============================================

    setupParticles() {
        const canvas = this.elements.particles;
        if (!canvas) return;

        const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
        let particles = [];
        let animationId;

        const resize = () => {
            canvas.width = window.innerWidth;
            canvas.height = window.innerHeight;
        };

        resize();
        window.addEventListener('resize', resize);

        class Particle {
            constructor() {
                this.reset();
            }

            reset() {
                this.x = Math.random() * canvas.width;
                this.y = Math.random() * canvas.height;
                this.size = Math.random() * 2 + 0.5;
                this.speedX = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.5;
                this.speedY = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.5;
                this.opacity = Math.random() * 0.3 + 0.1;
            }

            update() {
                this.x += this.speedX;
                this.y += this.speedY;

                if (this.x < 0 || this.x > canvas.width ||
                    this.y < 0 || this.y > canvas.height) {
                    this.reset();
                }
            }

            draw() {
                ctx.beginPath();
                ctx.arc(this.x, this.y, this.size, 0, Math.PI * 2);
                ctx.fillStyle = `rgba(96, 165, 250, ${this.opacity})`;
                ctx.fill();
            }
        }

        // Create particles
        for (let i = 0; i < 50; i++) {
            particles.push(new Particle());
        }

        const animate = () => {
            ctx.clearRect(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);

            particles.forEach(p => {
                p.update();
                p.draw();
            });

            // Draw connections
            particles.forEach((a, i) => {
                particles.slice(i + 1).forEach(b => {
                    const dx = a.x - b.x;
                    const dy = a.y - b.y;
                    const dist = Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy);

                    if (dist < 150) {
                        ctx.beginPath();
                        ctx.moveTo(a.x, a.y);
                        ctx.lineTo(b.x, b.y);
                        ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(59, 130, 246, ${0.05 * (1 - dist / 150)})`;
                        ctx.lineWidth = 0.5;
                        ctx.stroke();
                    }
                });
            });

            animationId = requestAnimationFrame(animate);
        };

        animate();
    }
}

// Initialize app
const app = new RoboAI();
6️⃣ netlify/functions/chat.js
JavaScript

// Netlify Function - Chat & Task Management

// In-memory task store (use Redis/DB for production)
const taskStore = {};

exports.handler = async (event) => {
    // Handle CORS preflight
    if (event.httpMethod === 'OPTIONS') {
        return {
            statusCode: 200,
            headers: {
                'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*',
                'Access-Control-Allow-Headers': 'Content-Type, X-API-Key',
                'Access-Control-Allow-Methods': 'GET, POST, OPTIONS'
            },
            body: ''
        };
    }

    if (event.httpMethod !== 'POST') {
        return {
            statusCode: 405,
            headers: { 'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*' },
            body: JSON.stringify({ error: 'Method not allowed' })
        };
    }

    try {
        const body = JSON.parse(event.body);

        // Handle task storage for plugin communication
        if (body.action === 'addTask') {
            const { pluginKey, task } = body;
            
            if (!taskStore[pluginKey]) {
                taskStore[pluginKey] = { tasks: [], completions: [] };
            }
            
            taskStore[pluginKey].tasks.push(task);

            return {
                statusCode: 200,
                headers: { 'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*' },
                body: JSON.stringify({ success: true, taskId: task.id })
            };
        }

        // Handle AI chat
        const { apiKey, messages, model, testMode } = body;

        if (!apiKey) {
            return {
                statusCode: 400,
                headers: { 'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*' },
                body: JSON.stringify({ error: 'API key is required' })
            };
        }

        // Test mode - just verify the key
        if (testMode) {
            const testResponse = await fetch('https://api.openai.com/v1/models', {
                headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${apiKey}` }
            });

            if (testResponse.ok) {
                return {
                    statusCode: 200,
                    headers: { 'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*' },
                    body: JSON.stringify({ success: true, message: 'Connected' })
                };
            } else {
                return {
                    statusCode: 401,
                    headers: { 'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*' },
                    body: JSON.stringify({ error: 'Nieprawidłowy klucz API' })
                };
            }
        }

        // Call OpenAI API
        const openaiResponse = await fetch('https://api.openai.com/v1/chat/completions', {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: {
                'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                'Authorization': `Bearer ${apiKey}`
            },
            body: JSON.stringify({
                model: model || 'gpt-4o-mini',
                messages: messages,
                max_tokens: 4096,
                temperature: 0.7
            })
        });

        if (!openaiResponse.ok) {
            const errorData = await openaiResponse.json();
            const errorMessage = errorData.error?.message || 'Błąd OpenAI API';
            
            return {
                statusCode: openaiResponse.status,
                headers: { 'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*' },
                body: JSON.stringify({ error: errorMessage })
            };
        }

        const data = await openaiResponse.json();
        const content = data.choices[0]?.message?.content || 'Brak odpowiedzi';

        return {
            statusCode: 200,
            headers: {
                'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*'
            },
            body: JSON.stringify({
                content: content,
                model: data.model,
                usage: data.usage
            })
        };

    } catch (error) {
        return {
            statusCode: 500,
            headers: { 'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*' },
            body: JSON.stringify({ error: `Server error: ${error.message}` })
        };
    }
};
7️⃣ netlify/functions/get-task.js
JavaScript

// Netlify Function - Get pending tasks for Roblox plugin

// Shared task store (in production use Redis/Database)
// For demo purposes, using global variable
const globalTasks = {};

exports.handler = async (event) => {
    // CORS
    if (event.httpMethod === 'OPTIONS') {
        return {
            statusCode: 200,
            headers: {
                'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*',
                'Access-Control-Allow-Headers': 'Content-Type, X-API-Key',
                'Access-Control-Allow-Methods': 'GET, POST, OPTIONS'
            },
            body: ''
        };
    }

    const params = event.queryStringParameters || {};
    const pluginKey = params.pluginKey;

    if (!pluginKey) {
        return {
            statusCode: 400,
            headers: { 'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*' },
            body: JSON.stringify({ error: 'pluginKey is required' })
        };
    }

    // Check for completions
    if (params.check === 'completions') {
        const store = globalTasks[pluginKey];
        const completions = store?.completions || [];
        
        // Clear completions after reading
        if (store) {
            store.completions = [];
        }

        return {
            statusCode: 200,
            headers: {
                'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*'
            },
            body: JSON.stringify({ completions })
        };
    }

    // Get pending tasks
    const store = globalTasks[pluginKey];
    const tasks = store?.tasks || [];

    // Clear tasks after sending (plugin received them)
    if (store) {
        store.tasks = [];
    }

    return {
        statusCode: 200,
        headers: {
            'Content-Type': 'application/json',
            'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*'
        },
        body: JSON.stringify({ tasks })
    };
};
8️⃣ netlify/functions/complete-task.js
JavaScript

// Netlify Function - Mark task as completed by plugin

const globalTasks = {};

exports.handler = async (event) => {
    if (event.httpMethod === 'OPTIONS') {
        return {
            statusCode: 200,
            headers: {
                'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*',
                'Access-Control-Allow-Headers': 'Content-Type',
                'Access-Control-Allow-Methods': 'POST, OPTIONS'
            },
            body: ''
        };
    }

    if (event.httpMethod !== 'POST') {
        return {
            statusCode: 405,
            headers: { 'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*' },
            body: JSON.stringify({ error: 'Method not allowed' })
        };
    }

    try {
        const body = JSON.parse(event.body);
        const { pluginKey, taskId } = body;

        if (!pluginKey || !taskId) {
            return {
                statusCode: 400,
                headers: { 'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*' },
                body: JSON.stringify({ error: 'pluginKey and taskId required' })
            };
        }

        if (!globalTasks[pluginKey]) {
            globalTasks[pluginKey] = { tasks: [], completions: [] };
        }

        globalTasks[pluginKey].completions.push(taskId);

        return {
            statusCode: 200,
            headers: {
                'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*'
            },
            body: JSON.stringify({ success: true })
        };

    } catch (error) {
        return {
            statusCode: 500,
            headers: { 'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*' },
            body: JSON.stringify({ error: error.message })
        };
    }
};

Lua

-- ============================================
-- RoboAI Studio Plugin
-- Wklej to w Roblox Studio jako Plugin
-- ============================================

-- KONFIGURACJA - ZMIEŃ TE WARTOŚCI!
local CONFIG = {
    SERVER_URL = "https://TWOJA-STRONA.netlify.app", -- Zmień na swój URL Netlify!
    PLUGIN_KEY = "rk_TWOJ_KLUCZ_Z_USTAWIEN",        -- Zmień na klucz z ustawień strony!
    POLL_INTERVAL = 3,                                  -- Co ile sekund sprawdzać zadania
}

-- Services
local HttpService = game:GetService("HttpService")
local ServerScriptService = game:GetService("ServerScriptService")
local StarterGui = game:GetService("StarterGui")
local StarterPlayer = game:GetService("StarterPlayer")
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
local Selection = game:GetService("Selection")
local ChangeHistoryService = game:GetService("ChangeHistoryService")

-- Plugin Setup
local toolbar = plugin:CreateToolbar("RoboAI Studio")

    "RoboAI",

local isRunning = false
local pollConnection = nil

-- ============================================

local widgetInfo = DockWidgetPluginGuiInfo.new(
    Enum.InitialDockState.Right,
    false,   -- Początkowo widoczny?

-- Create UI
local mainFrame = Instance.new("Frame")

-- ============================================
-- FUNCTIONS
-- ============================================

local logOrder = 0

local function addLog(message, color)
    logOrder += 1
    
    local label = Instance.new("TextLabel")
    label.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 0)
    label.AutomaticSize = Enum.AutomaticSize.Y
    label.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    label.Text = os.date("[%H:%M:%S] ") .. message
    label.TextColor3 = color or Color3.fromRGB(148, 163, 184)
    label.Font = Enum.Font.RobotoMono
    label.TextSize = 11
    label.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
    label.TextWrapped = true
    label.LayoutOrder = logOrder
    label.Parent = logFrame
    
    -- Auto scroll
    task.defer(function()
        logFrame.CanvasPosition = Vector2.new(0, logFrame.AbsoluteCanvasSize.Y)
    end)
end

local function getParentService(parentName)
    local parents = {
        StarterGui = StarterGui,
        ServerScriptService = ServerScriptService,
        StarterPlayerScripts = StarterPlayer:WaitForChild("StarterPlayerScripts"),
        ReplicatedStorage = ReplicatedStorage,
        Workspace = workspace,
    }
    return parents[parentName] or StarterGui
end

local function executeTask(taskData)
    addLog("📥 Otrzymano zadanie: " .. (taskData.scriptType or "Script"), Color3.fromRGB(96, 165, 250))
    
    local success, err = pcall(function()
        -- Determine instance type
        local scriptType = taskData.scriptType or "LocalScript"
        local parentName = taskData.parent or "StarterGui"
        
        -- Create the script instance
        local scriptInstance
        if scriptType == "LocalScript" then
            scriptInstance = Instance.new("LocalScript")
        elseif scriptType == "ModuleScript" then
            scriptInstance = Instance.new("ModuleScript")
        else
            scriptInstance = Instance.new("Script")
        end
        
        -- Set the source code
        scriptInstance.Source = taskData.code
        scriptInstance.Name = "AI_Generated_" .. os.time()
        
        -- Parent it
        local parent = getParentService(parentName)
        scriptInstance.Parent = parent
        
        -- Select it
        Selection:Set({scriptInstance})
        
        -- Record in change history
        ChangeHistoryService:SetWaypoint("RoboAI: Created " .. scriptType)
        
        addLog("✅ " .. scriptType .. " stworzony w " .. parentName, Color3.fromRGB(16, 185, 129))
        
        -- Notify server that task is complete
        pcall(function()
            HttpService:PostAsync(
                CONFIG.SERVER_URL .. "/.netlify/functions/complete-task",
                HttpService:JSONEncode({
                    pluginKey = CONFIG.PLUGIN_KEY,
                    taskId = taskData.id
                }),
                Enum.HttpContentType.ApplicationJson
            )
        end)
    end)
    
    if not success then
        addLog("❌ Błąd: " .. tostring(err), Color3.fromRGB(239, 68, 68))
    end
end

local function pollForTasks()
    local success, result = pcall(function()
        local url = CONFIG.SERVER_URL .. "/.netlify/functions/get-task?pluginKey=" .. CONFIG.PLUGIN_KEY
        local response = HttpService:GetAsync(url)
        local data = HttpService:JSONDecode(response)
        
        if data.tasks and #data.tasks > 0 then
            for _, taskData in ipairs(data.tasks) do
                executeTask(taskData)
            end
        end
    end)
    
    if not success then
        -- Silently handle errors (connection issues, etc.)
        -- Uncomment below for debugging:
        -- addLog("⚠ Poll error: " .. tostring(result), Color3.fromRGB(245, 158, 11))
    end
end

local function startPolling()
    if isRunning then return end
    isRunning = true
    
    statusLabel.Text = "🟢 Aktywny - nasłuchuję..."
    statusLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(16, 185, 129)
    toggleBtnUI.Text = "⏸ Zatrzymaj"
    toggleBtnUI.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(239, 68, 68)
    
    addLog("🚀 Plugin uruchomiony!", Color3.fromRGB(16, 185, 129))
    addLog("🔗 Serwer: " .. CONFIG.SERVER_URL, Color3.fromRGB(96, 165, 250))
    addLog("🔑 Klucz: " .. string.sub(CONFIG.PLUGIN_KEY, 1, 10) .. "...", Color3.fromRGB(96, 165, 250))
    
    -- Start polling loop
    task.spawn(function()
        while isRunning do
            pollForTasks()
            task.wait(CONFIG.POLL_INTERVAL)
        end
    end)
end

local function stopPolling()
    isRunning = false
    
    statusLabel.Text = "⏸ Zatrzymany"
    statusLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(245, 158, 11)
    toggleBtnUI.Text = "▶ Uruchom"
    toggleBtnUI.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(59, 130, 246)
    
    addLog("⏸ Plugin zatrzymany", Color3.fromRGB(245, 158, 11))
end

-- ============================================
-- EVENT HANDLERS
-- ============================================

toggleBtnUI.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
    if isRunning then
        stopPolling()
    else
        startPolling()
    end
end)

toggleButton.Click:Connect(function()
    widget.Enabled = not widget.Enabled
end)

-- Initial log
addLog("🤖 RoboAI Studio Plugin załadowany", Color3.fromRGB(96, 165, 250))
addLog("Kliknij 'Uruchom' aby połączyć ze stroną", Color3.fromRGB(148, 163, 184))
📋 INSTRUKCJA KROK PO KROKU
Krok 1: Przygotowanie projektu
Bash

# Stwórz folder projektu
mkdir roblox-ai-assistant
cd roblox-ai-assistant

# Skopiuj wszystkie pliki z powyższego przewodnika
# index.html, style.css, script.js do głównego folderu
# netlify.toml, package.json do głównego folderu
# chat.js, get-task.js, complete-task.js do netlify/functions/
Krok 2: Deploy na Netlify
Opcja A - Przez GitHub (ZALECANE):

Bash

# Zainicjuj git
git init
git add .
git commit -m "Initial commit"

# Stwórz repo na GitHub i wypchnij
git remote add origin https://github.com/TWOJ-USER/roblox-ai-assistant.git
git push -u origin main
Idź na https://app.netlify.com
Kliknij "Add new site" → "Import an existing project"
Wybierz GitHub i swoje repo
Ustawienia buildu:
Build command: (zostaw puste)
Publish directory: .
Functions directory: netlify/functions
Kliknij "Deploy site"
Opcja B - Przez Netlify CLI:

Bash

# Zainstaluj Netlify CLI
npm install -g netlify-cli

# Zaloguj się
netlify login

# Deploy
netlify deploy --prod
Krok 3: Zdobądź klucz OpenAI API
Idź na https://platform.openai.com/api-keys
Kliknij "Create new secret key"
Skopiuj klucz (zaczyna się od sk-...)
Krok 4: Skonfiguruj stronę
Otwórz swoją stronę na Netlify (np. https://twoja-strona.netlify.app)
Wpisz klucz OpenAI API w pole po lewej
Kliknij "Połącz"
Idź do Ustawienia (ikona zębatki) → Generuj klucz pluginu
Skopiuj klucz pluginu i URL serwera
Krok 5: Zainstaluj Plugin w Roblox Studio
Otwórz Roblox Studio
Upewnij się że masz włączone HttpService:
Game Settings → Security → Allow HTTP Requests → ✅ ON
W ServerScriptService stwórz nowy Script
WAŻNE: Nie Script - musisz stworzyć Plugin:
Idź do Plugins tab → Manage Plugins
Albo: stwórz folder Plugins w swoim komputerze:
Windows: %LOCALAPPDATA%\Roblox\Plugins\
Mac: ~/Documents/Roblox/Plugins/
Zapisz kod pluginu jako plik .lua w tym folderze
W pliku pluginu zmień CONFIG:
Lua

local CONFIG = {
    SERVER_URL = "https://twoja-strona.netlify.app",  -- Twój URL!
    PLUGIN_KEY = "rk_twoj_klucz_skopiowany",           -- Twój klucz!
    POLL_INTERVAL = 3,
}
Zrestartuj Roblox Studio
W toolbarze pojawi się przycisk "RoboAI" - kliknij go
Kliknij "Uruchom" w panelu pluginu
Krok 6: Testuj!
Na stronie wpisz np.: "Stwórz ładne GUI menu głównego z przyciskami Play i Settings"
AI wygeneruje kod
Kod automatycznie pojawi się w Roblox Studio!
⚠️ WAŻNE UWAGI
text

┌────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                    OGRANICZENIA                         │
├────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│                                                        │
│  1. Netlify Functions mają STATELESS - każde           │
│     wywołanie to osobna instancja. In-memory           │
│     task store NIE persystuje między wywołaniami!      │
│                                                        │
│  2. Dla produkcji użyj bazy danych:                   │
│     - Netlify Blobs                                    │
│     - Redis (Upstash - darmowy tier)                   │
│     - Supabase                                         │
│     - Firebase Realtime DB                             │
│                                                        │
│  3. OpenAI API jest PŁATNE - GPT-4o-mini jest          │
│     najtańszy (~$0.15/1M tokenów input)                │
│                                                        │
│  4. HttpService w Roblox Studio musi być WŁĄCZONY     │
│     (Game Settings → Security → Allow HTTP Requests)   │
│                                                        │
│  5. Plugin wymaga zapisu jako plik .lua w folderze     │
│     Plugins na twoim komputerze                        │
│                                                        │
└────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
🔧 Upgrade: Użyj Upstash Redis (darmowa baza)
Aby task store działał prawidłowo między wywołaniami, dodaj Upstash Redis:

1. Stwórz konto na upstash.com
Idź na https://upstash.com
Stwórz darmową bazę Redis
Skopiuj UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_URL i UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_TOKEN
2. Dodaj zmienne w Netlify
Site settings → Environment variables → Add:
UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_URL = twój URL
UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_TOKEN = twój token
3. Zaktualizuj package.json
JSON

{
  "dependencies": {
    "openai": "^4.52.0",
    "uuid": "^9.0.0",
    "@upstash/redis": "^1.28.0"
  }
}
4. Zaktualizuj chat.js z Redis
JavaScript

const { Redis } = require('@upstash/redis');

const redis = new Redis({
    url: process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_URL,
    token: process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_TOKEN,
});

exports.handler = async (event) => {
    if (event.httpMethod === 'OPTIONS') {
        return {
            statusCode: 200,
            headers: {
                'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*',
                'Access-Control-Allow-Headers': 'Content-Type',
                'Access-Control-Allow-Methods': 'GET, POST, OPTIONS'
            },
            body: ''
        };
    }

    if (event.httpMethod !== 'POST') {
        return { statusCode: 405, body: 'Method not allowed' };
    }

    try {
        const body = JSON.parse(event.body);

        // Task management with Redis
        if (body.action === 'addTask') {
            const { pluginKey, task } = body;
            const key = `tasks:${pluginKey}`;
            
            // Get existing tasks
            let tasks = await redis.get(key) || [];
            tasks.push(task);
            
            // Store with 1 hour TTL
            await redis.set(key, tasks, { ex: 3600 });

            return {
                statusCode: 200,
                headers: { 'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*' },
                body: JSON.stringify({ success: true, taskId: task.id })
            };
        }

        // AI Chat
        const { apiKey, messages, model, testMode } = body;

        if (!apiKey) {
            return {
                statusCode: 400,
                headers: { 'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*' },
                body: JSON.stringify({ error: 'API key required' })
            };
        }

        if (testMode) {
            const testResp = await fetch('https://api.openai.com/v1/models', {
                headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${apiKey}` }
            });
            
            return {
                statusCode: testResp.ok ? 200 : 401,
                headers: { 'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*' },
                body: JSON.stringify(testResp.ok 
                    ? { success: true } 
                    : { error: 'Invalid API key' })
            };
        }

        const openaiResp = await fetch('https://api.openai.com/v1/chat/completions', {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: {
                'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                'Authorization': `Bearer ${apiKey}`
            },
            body: JSON.stringify({
                model: model || 'gpt-4o-mini',
                messages,
                max_tokens: 4096,
                temperature: 0.7
            })
        });

        if (!openaiResp.ok) {
            const err = await openaiResp.json();
            return {
                statusCode: openaiResp.status,
                headers: { 'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*' },
                body: JSON.stringify({ error: err.error?.message || 'OpenAI error' })
            };
        }

        const data = await openaiResp.json();

        return {
            statusCode: 200,
            headers: {
                'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*'
            },
            body: JSON.stringify({
                content: data.choices[0]?.message?.content || '',
                model: data.model,
                usage: data.usage
            })
        };

    } catch (error) {
        return {
            statusCode: 500,
            headers: { 'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*' },
            body: JSON.stringify({ error: error.message })
        };
    }
};
5. Zaktualizuj get-task.js z Redis
JavaScript

const { Redis } = require('@upstash/redis');

const redis = new Redis({
    url: process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_URL,
    token: process.env.UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_TOKEN,
});

exports.handler = async (event) => {
    if (event.httpMethod === 'OPTIONS') {
        return {
            statusCode: 200,
            headers: {
                'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*',
                'Access-Control-Allow-Headers': 'Content-Type',
                'Access-Control-Allow-Methods': 'GET, OPTIONS'
            },
            body: ''
        };
    }

    const params = event.queryStringParameters || {};
    const pluginKey = params.pluginKey;

    if (!pluginKey) {
        return {
            statusCode: 400,
            headers: { 'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*' },
            body: JSON.stringify({ error: 'pluginKey required' })
        };
    }

    try {
        if (params.check === 'completions') {
            const completions = await redis.get(`completions:${pluginKey}`) || [];
            await redis.del(`completions:${pluginKey}`);
            
            return {
                statusCode: 200,
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*' },
                body: JSON.stringify({ completions })
            };
        }

        // Get and clear tasks
        const key = `tasks:${pluginKey}`;
        const tasks = await redis.get(key) || [];
        
        if (tasks.length > 0) {
            await redis.del(key);
        }

        return {
            statusCode: 200,
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*' },
            body: JSON.stringify({ tasks })
        };

    } catch (error) {
        return {
            statusCode: 500,
            headers: { 'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*' },
            body: JSON.stringify({ error: error.message })
        };
    }
};
🎯 Podsumowanie Przepływu
text

1. 👤 Piszesz na stronie: "Stwórz GUI menu"
          ↓
2. 🌐 Strona wysyła request do Netlify Function
          ↓  
3. 🤖 Netlify Function wysyła do OpenAI API
          ↓
4. 📝 AI generuje kod Luau
          ↓
5. 🌐 Kod wraca na stronę + zapisuje się w Redis
          ↓
6. 🔌 Plugin co 3 sekundy pyta: "Są nowe zadania?"
          ↓
7. 📥 Plugin pobiera kod z Redis
          ↓
8. 🎮 Plugin tworzy Script w Roblox Studio!
          ↓
9. ✅ Plugin informuje stronę: "Zrobione!"
Całość jest darmowa (Netlify free tier + Upstash free tier). Jedyny koszt to OpenAI API (GPT-4o-mini jest bardzo tani).
